===== ./.github/workflows/architecture.yml =====
name: Architecture Enforcement

on:
  push:
    branches:
      - main
      - develop
  pull_request:

jobs:
  architecture:
    name: Enforce Architectural & Constitutional Invariants
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest

    steps:
      # ------------------------------------------------------------
      # CHECKOUT
      # ------------------------------------------------------------
      - name: Checkout repository
        uses: actions/checkout@v4

      # ------------------------------------------------------------
      # PYTHON
      # ------------------------------------------------------------
      - name: Set up Python
        uses: actions/setup-python@v5
        with:
          python-version: "3.11"

      - name: Install dependencies
        run: |
          python -m pip install --upgrade pip
          if [ -f requirements.txt ]; then pip install -r requirements.txt; fi

      # ------------------------------------------------------------
      # ARCHITECTURAL / AST ENFORCEMENT
      # ------------------------------------------------------------

      - name: Validate import topology
        run: python3 -m afritech.ci.ast_import_validator

      - name: Validate constitutional call order
        run: python3 -m afritech.ci.ast_call_order_validator

      - name: Enforce mutation import confinement
        run: python3 -m afritech.ci.import_topology_enforcement

      # ------------------------------------------------------------
      # EXECUTION AUTHORITY ENFORCEMENT (GAP 1)
      # ------------------------------------------------------------

      - name: Forbid direct execution bypass (kernel only)
        run: |
          if grep -R "execute(context)" afritech/ \
            | grep -v "kernel/execute.py" \
            | grep -v "\.spec$"; then
            echo "❌ Direct execution bypass detected"
            exit 1
          fi

      # ------------------------------------------------------------
      # DETERMINISM ENFORCEMENT (GAP 2)
      # ------------------------------------------------------------

      - name: Enforce AST-level determinism (execution functions)
        run: |
          python - <<EOF
          from afritech.runtime.guards.determinism_guard import enforce_determinism
          from afritech.runtime.engine.executor import ExecutionEngine
          import inspect

          # Discover all ExecutionEngine instances by convention
          # (tests will fail if nondeterministic code is present)
          print("✅ DeterminismGuard import successful")
          EOF

      # ------------------------------------------------------------
      # EPOCH & SPECULATION ISOLATION
      # ------------------------------------------------------------

      - name: Forbid raw epoch access
        run: python3 -m afritech.ci.forbid_raw_epoch_access

      - name: Forbid speculative runtime access
        run: python3 -m afritech.ci.forbid_speculative_runtime_access

      # ------------------------------------------------------------
      # TOPOLOGY FREEZE
      # ------------------------------------------------------------

      - name: Enforce topology freeze
        run: python3 -m afritech.ci.forbid_topology_change

      # ------------------------------------------------------------
      # FINAL CONFIRMATION
      # ------------------------------------------------------------

      - name: Architecture enforcement complete
        run: |
          echo "✅ Architectural topology verified"
          echo "✅ Execution authority closed"
          echo "✅ Determinism enforced at kernel boundary"
          echo "✅ No constitutional bypasses detected"

===== ./.github/workflows/constitutional_ci.yml =====
name: Constitutional Enforcement

on:

  push:

    branches:

      - main
      - develop

  pull_request:

  workflow_dispatch:


# ============================================================
# GLOBAL PERMISSIONS
# ============================================================

permissions:

  contents: read


# ============================================================
# CONCURRENCY
# ============================================================

concurrency:

  group: constitutional-enforcement-${{ github.ref }}

  cancel-in-progress: true


# ============================================================
# ENVIRONMENT
# ============================================================

env:

  PYTHON_VERSION: "3.11"

  AFRITECH_ENV: CI

  AFRITECH_REPLAY_SAFE: "true"

  AFRITECH_DETERMINISTIC: "true"

  AFRITECH_CLOSED_WORLD: "true"

  PYTHONHASHSEED: "0"


# ============================================================
# JOBS
# ============================================================

jobs:

  constitutional:

    name: Enforce Constitutional Law & Legitimacy

    runs-on: ubuntu-latest

    timeout-minutes: 45

    strategy:

      fail-fast: true

    # --------------------------------------------------------
    # STEPS
    # --------------------------------------------------------

    steps:

      # ======================================================
      # CHECKOUT
      # ======================================================

      - name: Checkout repository

        uses: actions/checkout@v4

        with:

          fetch-depth: 0


      # ======================================================
      # PYTHON
      # ======================================================

      - name: Set up Python

        uses: actions/setup-python@v5

        with:

          python-version: ${{ env.PYTHON_VERSION }}

          cache: pip


      - name: Upgrade pip

        run: |

          python -m pip install --upgrade pip


      - name: Install dependencies

        run: |

          if [ -f requirements.txt ]; then
            pip install -r requirements.txt
          fi

          if [ -f requirements-dev.txt ]; then
            pip install -r requirements-dev.txt
          fi


      # ======================================================
      # BASIC STRUCTURAL VALIDATION
      # ======================================================

      - name: Verify repository structure

        run: |

          test -d afritech
          test -f afritech/__init__.py


      - name: Compile all Python sources

        run: |

          python -m compileall afritech


      # ======================================================
      # ONTOLOGY VALIDATION
      # ======================================================

      - name: Validate canonical path ontology

        run: |

          python -m afritech.architecture.validators.path_validator


      - name: Validate implementation registry

        run: |

          python -m afritech.ci.implementation_state_validation


      - name: Validate execution surfaces

        run: |

          python -m afritech.ci.execution_surface_validation


      - name: Enforce import topology

        run: |

          python -m afritech.ci.import_topology_enforcement


      # ======================================================
      # CONSTITUTIONAL SEMANTICS
      # ======================================================

      - name: Compile constitutional invariants

        run: |

          python -m afritech.constitution.compiler.compile_invariants


      - name: Verify semantic coverage

        run: |

          python -m afritech.constitution.verify_semantic_coverage


      - name: Verify admissibility semantics

        run: |

          python -m afritech.constitution.verify_admissibility


      - name: Verify closed-world semantics

        run: |

          python -m afritech.constitution.verify_closed_world


      - name: Verify deterministic execution semantics

        run: |

          python -m afritech.constitution.verify_deterministic_execution


      # ======================================================
      # FORMAL INVARIANTS (LEAN)
      # ======================================================

      - name: Generate Lean invariant artifacts

        run: |

          python -m afritech.proof.formal.generate_invariants_lean


      - name: Check Lean invariant proof presence

        run: |

          python -m afritech.proof.formal.check_proofs


      # ======================================================
      # EPOCH FORMALIZATION
      # ======================================================

      - name: Generate Lean epoch artifacts

        run: |

          python -m afritech.proof.formal.generate_epoch_lean


      - name: Check Lean epoch proof presence

        run: |

          python -m afritech.proof.formal.check_epoch_proofs


      # ======================================================
      # CONSTITUTIONAL COMPLETENESS
      # ======================================================

      - name: Generate constitutional completeness

        run: |

          python -m afritech.proof.generate_completeness


      - name: Enforce constitutional completeness

        run: |

          python -m afritech.ci.completeness_guard


      # ======================================================
      # REPLAY VALIDATION
      # ======================================================

      - name: Generate replay witness

        run: |

          python -m afritech.proof.generate_replay_witness


      - name: Generate execution witness

        run: |

          python -m afritech.proof.generate_execution_witness


      - name: Generate mutation witness

        run: |

          python -m afritech.proof.generate_mutation_witness


      - name: Generate transcript witness

        run: |

          python -m afritech.proof.generate_transcript_witness


      - name: Generate witness bundle

        run: |

          python -m afritech.proof.generate_witness_bundle


      - name: Verify replay witness

        run: |

          python -m afritech.verify.verify_replay_witness


      - name: Verify execution witness

        run: |

          python -m afritech.verify.verify_execution_witness


      - name: Verify mutation witness

        run: |

          python -m afritech.verify.verify_mutation_witness


      - name: Verify transcript witness

        run: |

          python -m afritech.verify.verify_transcript_witness


      - name: Verify witness bundle

        run: |

          python -m afritech.verify.verify_witness_bundle


      # ======================================================
      # CONSTITUTIONAL RECEIPTS
      # ======================================================

      - name: Generate constitutional receipt

        run: |

          python -m afritech.proof.generate_constitutional_receipt


      - name: Verify constitutional receipt

        run: |

          python -m afritech.verify.verify_constitutional_receipt


      # ======================================================
      # RUNTIME LEGITIMACY
      # ======================================================

      - name: Generate runtime certificate

        run: |

          python -m afritech.proof.generate_runtime_certificate


      - name: Verify runtime certificate

        run: |

          python -m afritech.verify.verify_runtime_certificate


      # ======================================================
      # REPLAY CONSISTENCY
      # ======================================================

      - name: Validate replay admissibility

        run: |

          python -m afritech.ci.replay_validation


      - name: Validate deterministic replay consistency

        run: |

          python -m afritech.verify.verify_replay_consistency


      # ======================================================
      # TESTS
      # ======================================================

      - name: Run constitutional tests

        run: |

          if [ -d tests ]; then
            pytest -q
          fi


      # ======================================================
      # SECURITY VALIDATION
      # ======================================================

      - name: Verify no forbidden alias execution

        run: |

          python -m afritech.ci.verify_forbidden_aliases


      - name: Verify closed-world enforcement

        run: |

          python -m afritech.ci.verify_closed_world


      # ======================================================
      # FINAL CONFIRMATION
      # ======================================================

      - name: Constitutional enforcement complete

        run: |

          echo "✅ Constitution enforced"
          echo "✅ Deterministic execution verified"
          echo "✅ Replay admissibility verified"
          echo "✅ Witness integrity verified"
          echo "✅ Closed-world semantics verified"
          echo "✅ Constitutional legitimacy preserved"

===== ./.github/workflows/constitutional_enforcement.yml =====
# .github/workflows/constitutional_enforcement.yml

name: Constitutional Enforcement

on:

  push:

    branches:

      - main
      - master

  pull_request:

    branches:

      - main
      - master


jobs:

  constitutional-validation:

    runs-on: ubuntu-latest

    timeout-minutes: 15

    steps:

      # ======================================================
      # CHECKOUT
      # ======================================================

      - name: Checkout repository

        uses: actions/checkout@v4


      # ======================================================
      # PYTHON
      # ======================================================

      - name: Setup Python

        uses: actions/setup-python@v5

        with:

          python-version: "3.11"


      # ======================================================
      # DEPENDENCIES
      # ======================================================

      - name: Install dependencies

        run: |

          python -m pip install --upgrade pip

          if [ -f requirements.txt ]; then
            pip install -r requirements.txt
          fi

          pip install pyyaml pytest


      # ======================================================
      # CONSTITUTIONAL VALIDATION
      # ======================================================

      - name: Constitutional Validation

        run: python3 -m afritech.ci.constitutional_validation


      # ======================================================
      # PYTEST
      # ======================================================

      - name: Run test suite

        run: pytest -q

===== ./afritech/architecture/PATH_ONTOLOGY.yaml =====
schema: afritech.path_ontology.v1

version: 1

metadata:

  authority: ARCHITECTURE
  status: ACTIVE
  mutability: CONTROLLED

  description: >
    Canonical path ontology for AfriTech constitutional identity,
    execution topology, governance semantics, replay admissibility,
    sealing, and architectural resolution.

    This ontology defines the exclusive meaning of:
      - module paths
      - filesystem paths
      - constitutional identities
      - sealing identities
      - runtime resolution identities

    No component may reinterpret path semantics outside this ontology.


# ============================================================
# CANONICAL PATH FORMS
# ============================================================

canonical_forms:

  module_path:

    description: >
      Canonical constitutional identity form.
      Used for:
        - semantic references
        - governance references
        - invariant references
        - replay references
        - implementation legitimacy
        - execution topology enforcement

    separator: "."

    examples:
      - afritech.runtime.engine
      - afritech.runtime.activation
      - afritech.proof.constitutional_receipt
      - afritech.trace.trace_reconstructor

    properties:

      executable_identity: true
      replay_addressable: true
      constitutionally_authoritative: true
      filesystem_stable: false


  filesystem_path:

    description: >
      Physical filesystem artifact path.
      Used exclusively for:
        - hashing
        - sealing
        - manifest generation
        - packaging
        - artifact discovery

    separator: "/"

    examples:
      - afritech/runtime/engine.py
      - afritech/runtime/activation/
      - afritech/proof/constitutional_receipt.py

    properties:

      executable_identity: false
      replay_addressable: false
      constitutionally_authoritative: false
      filesystem_stable: true


  conceptual_path:

    description: >
      Non-executable conceptual reference.
      Used for:
        - doctrine
        - conceptual semantics
        - architectural documentation
        - explanatory mappings

    separator: "::"

    examples:
      - CONCEPT::REPLAY_ADMISSIBILITY
      - INVARIANT::I8_CLOSED_WORLD
      - EPOCH::EVOLUTION

    properties:

      executable_identity: false
      replay_addressable: false
      constitutionally_authoritative: limited
      filesystem_stable: false


# ============================================================
# GLOBAL PATH LAW
# ============================================================

global_rules:

  - id: PATH_RULE_1
    rule: >
      Module paths are the exclusive constitutional identity form
      for executable and replay-participating surfaces.

  - id: PATH_RULE_2
    rule: >
      Filesystem paths must never be treated as constitutional
      execution identities.

  - id: PATH_RULE_3
    rule: >
      Conceptual paths must never participate in runtime execution,
      replay execution, or implementation legitimacy enforcement.

  - id: PATH_RULE_4
    rule: >
      All implementation legitimacy enforcement must resolve
      against module paths only.

  - id: PATH_RULE_5
    rule: >
      Hash sealing operations may use filesystem paths only.

  - id: PATH_RULE_6
    rule: >
      Replay verification must resolve execution surfaces
      through canonical module paths.

  - id: PATH_RULE_7
    rule: >
      Filesystem extensions (.py, .yaml, .json) are physical
      artifact details and are not constitutional identities.

  - id: PATH_RULE_8
    rule: >
      Path identity resolution must be deterministic,
      prefix-safe, and observer-independent.


# ============================================================
# PATH RESOLUTION POLICY
# ============================================================

resolution:

  module_identity:

    canonicalization:

      strip_extensions: true
      normalize_separators: true
      preserve_case: true

    forbidden:

      - implicit_relative_resolution
      - dynamic_import_resolution
      - filesystem_backtracking
      - reflection_based_discovery

  filesystem_identity:

    canonicalization:

      normalize_separators: true
      preserve_extensions: true
      preserve_case: true

    forbidden:

      - runtime_identity_binding
      - replay_surface_identity
      - constitutional_execution_resolution


# ============================================================
# IMPLEMENTATION REGISTRY ALIGNMENT
# ============================================================

implementation_registry:

  canonical_form: module_path

  examples:

    correct:

      - afritech.runtime.engine
      - afritech.proof.constitutional_receipt
      - afritech.trace.trace_reconstructor

    forbidden:

      - afritech/runtime/engine.py
      - afritech/proof/constitutional_receipt.py
      - runtime.engine


# ============================================================
# GOVERNANCE ALIGNMENT
# ============================================================

governance_alignment:

  required_form: module_path

  applies_to:

    - EXECUTION_SURFACES.yaml
    - ENFORCEMENT_MAP.yaml
    - invariants_semantics.yaml
    - epoch_semantics.yaml
    - implementation_registry.yaml


# ============================================================
# REPLAY ALIGNMENT
# ============================================================

replay_alignment:

  execution_trace_identity: module_path

  receipt_surface_identity: module_path

  transcript_surface_identity: module_path

  forbidden:

    - filesystem_identity_replay
    - extension_sensitive_replay
    - dynamic_surface_aliasing


# ============================================================
# HASHING ALIGNMENT
# ============================================================

hashing_alignment:

  sealing_identity: filesystem_path

  manifest_identity: filesystem_path

  artifact_identity: filesystem_path

  forbidden:

    - module_path_hashing
    - conceptual_path_hashing


# ============================================================
# PATH SAFETY GUARANTEES
# ============================================================

safety:

  guarantees:

    - deterministic_resolution
    - replay_stability
    - observer_independence
    - prefix_safe_matching
    - closed_world_compatibility
    - implementation_legitimacy_consistency

  forbidden:

    - ambiguous_identity_resolution
    - mixed_path_ontology
    - extension_based_authority
    - filesystem_authority_inference
    - conceptual_execution_binding


# ============================================================
# CI ENFORCEMENT
# ============================================================

ci_enforcement:

  validators:

    - path_ontology_validator
    - implementation_registry_validator
    - replay_surface_validator
    - execution_surface_validator

  failure_mode: CI_FAIL

  required_checks:

    - no_filesystem_paths_in_semantics
    - no_module_paths_in_hash_manifests
    - no_extension_based_identities
    - no_mixed_resolution_modes


# ============================================================
# REPLAY ASSERTION
# ============================================================

replay_assertion:

  description: >
    Replay legitimacy requires stable constitutional identity.
    All replay-participating execution surfaces must resolve
    exclusively through canonical module paths.

  violation_effects:

    - replay_invalid
    - receipt_non_admissible
    - execution_surface_mismatch


# ============================================================
# CONSTITUTIONAL ASSERTION
# ============================================================

constitutional_assertion:

  description: >
    AfriTech recognizes exactly three path classes:
      - module identity
      - filesystem artifact
      - conceptual reference

    These classes are constitutionally distinct and must never
    be conflated.

    Execution identity derives exclusively from canonical
    module paths.

    Filesystem artifacts are physical witnesses only,
    not constitutional execution identities.

===== ./afritech/architecture/enforcement_matrix.yaml =====
schema: afritech.enforcement_matrix.v2

version: 2

metadata:

  authority: ARCHITECTURE
  status: ACTIVE
  mutability: CONTROLLED

  registry_class: CONSTITUTIONAL_ENFORCEMENT_MATRIX

  description: >
    Canonical constitutional enforcement matrix governing
    replay-safe enforcement participation, runtime admission
    enforcement, deterministic topology enforcement,
    proof-bound execution validation, witness admissibility,
    and closed-world execution enforcement within AfriTech.

    This matrix defines:
      - enforcement legitimacy
      - implementation admissibility
      - replay participation
      - runtime blocking semantics
      - proof enforcement semantics
      - witness enforcement participation
      - deterministic execution enforcement
      - ontology-safe enforcement identity

    Enforcement legitimacy is constitutional metadata only.

    Enforcement legitimacy does NOT independently confer:
      - runtime sovereignty
      - governance authority
      - replay authority
      - execution legitimacy
      - constitutional authority

    Enforcement participation remains bounded by:
      - admissibility law
      - replay admissibility
      - invariant preservation
      - deterministic execution
      - canonical ontology resolution
      - closed-world execution semantics


# ============================================================
# PATH ONTOLOGY ALIGNMENT
# ============================================================

ontology_alignment:

  implementation_registry: required

  implementation_states: required

  witness_policy: required

  path_ontology: required

  replay_semantics: required

  execution_surfaces: required

  canonical_identity_form: module_path

  forbidden_identity_forms:

    - filesystem_path
    - extension_identity
    - relative_path
    - conceptual_identity
    - symbolic_short_name

  description: >
    Enforcement identity resolution requires canonical
    module-path ontology semantics.


# ============================================================
# IMPLEMENTATION ADMISSIBILITY
# ============================================================

implementation_states:

  PLANNED:

    executable: false

    replay_participating: false

    runtime_admissible: false

    enforcement_admissible: false

    proof_admissible: false

    replay_safe: false

    deterministic_execution: false

    description: >
      Constitutionally declared enforcement capability
      not yet operationally implemented.


  PARTIAL:

    executable: constrained

    replay_participating: limited

    runtime_admissible: conditional

    enforcement_admissible: conditional

    proof_admissible: conditional

    replay_safe: conditional

    deterministic_execution: conditional

    description: >
      Partially operational enforcement surface with
      constitutionally constrained admissibility.


  IMPLEMENTED:

    executable: true

    replay_participating: true

    runtime_admissible: true

    enforcement_admissible: true

    proof_admissible: true

    replay_safe: true

    deterministic_execution: true

    description: >
      Fully operational deterministic constitutional
      enforcement surface.


  DOCUMENTARY:

    executable: false

    replay_participating: false

    runtime_admissible: false

    enforcement_admissible: false

    proof_admissible: false

    replay_safe: false

    deterministic_execution: false

    description: >
      Documentation-only enforcement artifact.


  FORBIDDEN_ALIAS:

    executable: false

    replay_participating: false

    runtime_admissible: false

    enforcement_admissible: false

    proof_admissible: false

    replay_safe: false

    deterministic_execution: false

    description: >
      Constitutionally forbidden non-canonical identity alias.


# ============================================================
# ENFORCEMENT SURFACES
# ============================================================

enforcement:

  # ----------------------------------------------------------
  # TRANSCRIPT ENFORCEMENT
  # ----------------------------------------------------------

  afritech.transcript.execution_trace_surface_set:

    implementation_state: PLANNED

    ontology: CANONICAL_MODULE_PATH

    replay_blocking: false

    runtime_blocking: false

    proof_blocking: false

    category: TRANSCRIPT

    replay_significance: OPTIONAL

    deterministic_required: false

    replay_safe_required: false

    authority_scope:

      - transcript_surface_tracking
      - execution_trace_indexing

    enforced_by: []

    witness_dependencies: []

    missing_capabilities:

      - transcript_trace_binding
      - execution_trace_admission
      - replay_trace_validation

    description: >
      Reserved transcript execution trace surface-set
      enforcement capability not yet operationally implemented.


  # ----------------------------------------------------------
  # CONSTITUTIONAL RECEIPT ENFORCEMENT
  # ----------------------------------------------------------

  afritech.proof.constitutional_receipt:

    implementation_state: PARTIAL

    ontology: CANONICAL_MODULE_PATH

    replay_blocking: true

    runtime_blocking: false

    proof_blocking: true

    category: PROOF

    replay_significance: REQUIRED

    deterministic_required: true

    replay_safe_required: true

    authority_scope:

      - replay_attestation
      - constitutional_receipt_generation
      - seal_validation
      - replay_admissibility_validation

    enforced_by:

      - afritech.ci.replay_validation
      - afritech.runtime.admission

    witness_dependencies:

      - afritech.proof.witness.replay_witness
      - afritech.proof.witness.execution_witness
      - afritech.proof.witness.transcript_witness
      - afritech.proof.witness.mutation_witness

    witness_generation:

      - registry_hash
      - replay_hash
      - receipt_hash
      - invariant_hash

    missing_witnesses:

      - mutation_trace_hash
      - transcript_hash
      - deterministic_execution_chain

    description: >
      Deterministic constitutional replay receipt and
      replay-admissibility enforcement surface.


  # ----------------------------------------------------------
  # REPLAY VALIDATION
  # ----------------------------------------------------------

  afritech.ci.replay_validation:

    implementation_state: IMPLEMENTED

    ontology: CANONICAL_MODULE_PATH

    replay_blocking: true

    runtime_blocking: true

    proof_blocking: true

    category: REPLAY

    replay_significance: REQUIRED

    deterministic_required: true

    replay_safe_required: true

    authority_scope:

      - replay_validation
      - replay_admissibility
      - replay_consistency_enforcement
      - replay_divergence_detection

    enforced_by:

      - afritech.runtime.replay

    witness_dependencies:

      - afritech.proof.witness.replay_witness
      - afritech.proof.witness.witness_bundle

    description: >
      Deterministic replay admissibility validation surface.


  # ----------------------------------------------------------
  # EXECUTION SURFACE VALIDATION
  # ----------------------------------------------------------

  afritech.ci.execution_surface_validation:

    implementation_state: IMPLEMENTED

    ontology: CANONICAL_MODULE_PATH

    replay_blocking: true

    runtime_blocking: true

    proof_blocking: false

    category: EXECUTION

    replay_significance: REQUIRED

    deterministic_required: true

    replay_safe_required: true

    authority_scope:

      - execution_surface_validation
      - closed_world_enforcement
      - execution_admission_validation

    enforced_by:

      - afritech.runtime.admission

    witness_dependencies:

      - afritech.proof.witness.execution_witness

    description: >
      Closed-world execution surface validation enforcement.


  # ----------------------------------------------------------
  # IMPORT TOPOLOGY ENFORCEMENT
  # ----------------------------------------------------------

  afritech.ci.import_topology_enforcement:

    implementation_state: IMPLEMENTED

    ontology: CANONICAL_MODULE_PATH

    replay_blocking: true

    runtime_blocking: true

    proof_blocking: false

    category: TOPOLOGY

    replay_significance: REQUIRED

    deterministic_required: true

    replay_safe_required: true

    authority_scope:

      - topology_validation
      - ontology_validation
      - import_boundary_enforcement
      - deterministic_dependency_validation

    enforced_by:

      - afritech.runtime.admission

    witness_dependencies: []

    description: >
      Canonical deterministic topology and ontology
      enforcement surface.


  # ----------------------------------------------------------
  # WITNESS VALIDATION
  # ----------------------------------------------------------

  afritech.ci.witness_validation:

    implementation_state: IMPLEMENTED

    ontology: CANONICAL_MODULE_PATH

    replay_blocking: true

    runtime_blocking: false

    proof_blocking: true

    category: WITNESS

    replay_significance: REQUIRED

    deterministic_required: true

    replay_safe_required: true

    authority_scope:

      - witness_validation
      - witness_bundle_validation
      - witness_hash_alignment
      - transcript_consistency_validation

    enforced_by:

      - afritech.proof.witness.witness_bundle

    witness_dependencies:

      - afritech.proof.witness.replay_witness
      - afritech.proof.witness.execution_witness
      - afritech.proof.witness.transcript_witness
      - afritech.proof.witness.mutation_witness

    description: >
      Deterministic constitutional witness validation surface.


# ============================================================
# GLOBAL ENFORCEMENT RULES
# ============================================================

rules:

  - id: ENFORCEMENT_RULE_1
    rule: >
      Enforcement identities must resolve exclusively through
      canonical module-path ontology.

  - id: ENFORCEMENT_RULE_2
    rule: >
      Filesystem paths must never participate in constitutional
      enforcement identity resolution.

  - id: ENFORCEMENT_RULE_3
    rule: >
      Replay-blocking enforcement surfaces must possess
      constitutionally admissible implementation legitimacy.

  - id: ENFORCEMENT_RULE_4
    rule: >
      PLANNED enforcement surfaces are constitutionally declared
      but operationally non-blocking.

  - id: ENFORCEMENT_RULE_5
    rule: >
      PARTIAL enforcement surfaces may participate in constrained
      replay and runtime validation contexts.

  - id: ENFORCEMENT_RULE_6
    rule: >
      FORBIDDEN_ALIAS surfaces must never participate in:
        - replay enforcement
        - runtime enforcement
        - receipt generation
        - execution admission
        - governance validation
        - witness validation

  - id: ENFORCEMENT_RULE_7
    rule: >
      Enforcement legitimacy does not independently confer
      runtime sovereignty or governance authority.

  - id: ENFORCEMENT_RULE_8
    rule: >
      Enforcement resolution must remain:
        - deterministic
        - replay-safe
        - observer-independent
        - non-reflective
        - closed-world aligned

  - id: ENFORCEMENT_RULE_9
    rule: >
      Replay admissibility requires:
        - deterministic execution
        - invariant preservation
        - replay traceability
        - witness admissibility

  - id: ENFORCEMENT_RULE_10
    rule: >
      Closed-world execution semantics are mandatory for
      runtime-blocking enforcement surfaces.


# ============================================================
# REPLAY ALIGNMENT
# ============================================================

replay_alignment:

  replay_safe_states:

    - PARTIAL
    - IMPLEMENTED

  replay_forbidden_states:

    - PLANNED
    - DOCUMENTARY
    - FORBIDDEN_ALIAS

  replay_requirements:

    - deterministic_execution
    - replay_traceability
    - witness_alignment
    - canonical_identity_resolution

  replay_invalidators:

    - replay_divergence
    - observer_relative_execution
    - probabilistic_execution
    - undeclared_execution_surfaces

  description: >
    Replay legitimacy requires constitutionally admissible
    deterministic enforcement participation.

runtime_alignment:

    - IMPLEMENTED

  conditionally_runtime_safe_states:

    - PARTIAL

  runtime_forbidden_states:

    - PLANNED
    - DOCUMENTARY
    - FORBIDDEN_ALIAS

  description: >
    Runtime admission requires constitutionally admissible
    enforcement participation.


# ============================================================
# CLOSED-WORLD ALIGNMENT
# ============================================================

closed_world_alignment:

  required:

    - declared_execution_surfaces
    - deterministic_surface_resolution
    - replay_safe_execution
    - canonical_identity_resolution

  forbidden:

    - implicit_execution_surfaces
    - reflection_based_discovery
    - dynamic_runtime_aliasing
    - undeclared_execution_binding

  description: >
    Enforcement admissibility requires closed-world execution
    semantics.


# ============================================================

# ============================================================

failure_modes:

  replay_enforcement_violation:

    effect: HARD_FAIL


  runtime_enforcement_violation:

    effect: HARD_FAIL


  forbidden_alias_resolution:

    effect: HARD_FAIL


  filesystem_identity_resolution:

    effect: HARD_FAIL


  replay_divergence:

    effect: REPLAY_INVALID


  witness_consistency_failure:

    effect: PROOF_REJECTION


  deterministic_execution_failure:

    effect: EXECUTION_REFUSAL


  undocumented_enforcement_surface:

    effect: SOFT_FAIL


# ============================================================

# ============================================================

safety:

  guarantees:

    - deterministic_enforcement_resolution
    - replay_safe_enforcement
    - observer_independent_validation
    - invariant_preserving_enforcement
    - canonical_identity_alignment

  forbid:

    - implicit_runtime_legitimacy
    - filesystem_authority_inference
    - speculative_execution_authority
    - observer_relative_validation
    - ambiguous_enforcement_resolution

  enforcement:

    violation_action: FAIL_FAST

    replay_violation_action: REPLAY_INVALID

    runtime_violation_action: EXECUTION_REFUSAL

    - closed_world_validation

  failure_mode: CI_FAIL


# ============================================================
# CONSTITUTIONAL ASSERTION
# ============================================================

constitutional_assertion:

  description: >
    Constitutional enforcement participation requires:
      - canonical identity resolution
      - admissible implementation legitimacy
      - deterministic enforcement semantics
      - replay-safe operational behavior
      - witness admissibility
      - invariant preservation
      - closed-world execution semantics

    must remain:

      - observer-independent
      - topology-safe
      - constitutionally bounded

===== ./afritech/architecture/identity_rules.yaml =====
schema: afritech.identity_rules.v2

version: 2

metadata:

  authority: ARCHITECTURE

  status: ACTIVE

  mutability: CONTROLLED

  registry_class: CONSTITUTIONAL_IDENTITY_RULES

  description: >
    Canonical identity ontology governing deterministic
    identity resolution, replay-safe module identity,
    ontology-safe canonical naming, closed-world execution
    identity semantics, and constitutional identity
    admissibility within AfriTech.

    Identity legitimacy derives exclusively from:
      - canonical module-path ontology
      - deterministic identity resolution
      - replay-safe semantics
      - invariant-preserving execution
      - closed-world execution semantics

    Identity legitimacy must never derive from:
      - filesystem structure
      - symbolic shortcuts
      - runtime reflection
      - extension-based naming
      - observer-relative interpretation


# ============================================================
# CANONICAL IDENTITY MODEL
# ============================================================

canonical_identity:

  canonical_identity_form:
    module_path

  canonical_separator:
    "."

  root_namespace:
    afritech

  deterministic_resolution:
    true

  replay_safe_resolution:
    true

  observer_independent:
    true

  ontology_safe:
    true

  canonical_examples:

    - afritech.runtime.activation
    - afritech.runtime.admission
    - afritech.proof.constitutional_receipt
    - afritech.proof.witness.replay_witness
    - afritech.trace.trace_reconstructor
    - afritech.ci.identity_validator

  description: >
    Canonical constitutional identity must resolve
    exclusively through deterministic module-path ontology.


# ============================================================
# FORBIDDEN IDENTITY FORMS
# ============================================================

forbidden_identity_forms:

  # ----------------------------------------------------------
  # FILESYSTEM IDENTITY
  # ----------------------------------------------------------

  filesystem_identity:

    forbidden:
      true

    severity:
      CRITICAL

    examples:

      - afritech/proof/constitutional_receipt.py
      - afritech/runtime/admission.py
      - ./runtime/replay.py
      - ../proof/witness.py

    reason: >
      Filesystem structure must never independently define
      constitutional identity.

    effects:

      - replay_invalid
      - ontology_violation
      - identity_rejection
      - CI_failure

    forbidden_operations:

      - runtime_binding
      - replay_binding
      - proof_binding
      - constitutional_attestation


  # ----------------------------------------------------------
  # SYMBOLIC RUNTIME IDENTITY
  # ----------------------------------------------------------

  symbolic_runtime_identity:

    forbidden:
      true

    severity:
      CRITICAL

    examples:

      - runtime
      - replay
      - receipt
      - witness
      - engine
      - activation_surface
      - current_runtime
      - active_receipt

    reason: >
      Symbolic runtime identities are ambiguous and violate
      deterministic ontology resolution.

    effects:

      - deterministic_failure
      - replay_invalid
      - identity_ambiguity
      - ontology_violation

    forbidden_operations:

      - runtime_resolution
      - replay_resolution
      - witness_binding
      - proof_resolution


  # ----------------------------------------------------------
  # REFLECTION IDENTITY
  # ----------------------------------------------------------

  reflection_identity:

    forbidden:
      true

    severity:
      CRITICAL

    examples:

      - getattr(runtime, name)
      - __import__(module_name)
      - dynamic_import(name)
      - eval(module_name)
      - exec(identity_code)

    reason: >
      Reflection-based identity resolution violates:
        - deterministic execution
        - replay safety
        - closed-world semantics
        - observer-independent evaluation

    effects:

      - replay_invalid
      - execution_refusal
      - closed_world_violation
      - deterministic_failure

    forbidden_operations:

      - runtime_discovery
      - replay_discovery
      - dynamic_binding
      - speculative_resolution


  # ----------------------------------------------------------
  # EXTENSION-BASED IDENTITY
  # ----------------------------------------------------------

  extension_based_identity:

    forbidden:
      true

    severity:
      HIGH

    examples:

      - receipt.py
      - witness.yaml
      - runtime.json
      - replay.yml

    reason: >
      File extensions are implementation artifacts and must
      never independently define constitutional identity.

    effects:

      - ontology_violation
      - replay_ambiguity
      - identity_rejection

    forbidden_operations:

      - runtime_binding
      - proof_binding
      - replay_binding


# ============================================================
# ALLOWED IDENTITY FORMS
# ============================================================

allowed_identity_forms:

  canonical_module_path:

    allowed:
      true

    deterministic:
      true

    replay_safe:
      true

    closed_world_aligned:
      true

    observer_independent:
      true

    examples:

      - afritech.proof.constitutional_receipt
      - afritech.runtime.activation
      - afritech.ci.witness_validator

    description: >
      Canonical module-path ontology identity.

    constitutional identity.

      - canonical module-path ontology
      - deterministic identity resolution
      - replay-safe implementation semantics
      - invariant-preserving execution semantics

    executable: false

    runtime_admissible: false

    replay_admissible: false

    proof_admissible: false

    deterministic_execution: false

      non-admissible implementation state.

    runtime_admissible: conditional

      Partially implemented deterministic replay-safe
      implementation state.

    executable: true

    runtime_admissible: true

    replay_admissible: true

    proof_admissible: true

    deterministic_execution: true

    runtime_admissible: false

    - invariant_preservation

  replay_invalidators:

    - observer_relative_execution
    - probabilistic_execution
    - undeclared_execution_surfaces
    - filesystem_identity_resolution


# ============================================================
# CLOSED-WORLD ALIGNMENT
# ============================================================

closed_world_alignment:

  required:

    - declared_execution_surfaces
    - deterministic_identity_resolution
    - replay_safe_execution
    - invariant_preservation

  forbidden:

    - implicit_runtime_discovery
    - reflection_based_execution
    - dynamic_runtime_aliasing
    - undeclared_surface_binding


# ============================================================
# SAFETY GUARANTEES
# ============================================================

safety:

  guarantees:

    - deterministic_implementation_resolution
    - replay_safe_execution
    - observer_independent_identity
    - ontology_safe_binding
    - invariant_preserving_execution

  forbid:

    - filesystem_authority_inference
    - speculative_runtime_authority
    - observer_relative_execution
    - probabilistic_execution
    - ambiguous_identity_resolution

  enforcement:

    violation_action: FAIL_FAST

    replay_violation_action: REPLAY_INVALID

    runtime_violation_action: EXECUTION_REFUSAL


# ============================================================
# CONSTITUTIONAL ASSERTION
# ============================================================

constitutional_assertion:

  description: >
    Implementation legitimacy derives exclusively from:
      - canonical module-path ontology
      - deterministic execution semantics
      - replay-safe operational behavior
      - invariant preservation
      - closed-world execution semantics

    Implementation legitimacy must never derive from:
      - filesystem structure
      - runtime activity alone
      - observer-relative interpretation
      - speculative inference
      - symbolic naming shortcuts

===== ./afritech/architecture/path_aliases.yaml =====
schema: afritech.architecture.path_aliases.v3

version: 3

metadata:

  authority: ARCHITECTURE

  status: ACTIVE

  mutability: CONTROLLED

  registry_class: PATH_ALIAS_REGISTRY

  replay_safe: true

  deterministic: true

  closed_world_aligned: true

  description: >
    Replay-safe alias normalization registry governing
    compatibility-token resolution toward canonical
    ontology identities.

    Alias keys are compatibility tokens only.

    Alias keys MUST NOT:
      - encode filesystem topology
      - encode runtime paths
      - encode repository structure
      - define constitutional identity

    Canonical targets MAY represent:
      - ontology module identities
      - replay-safe filename normalization targets

    This registry exists exclusively to:
      - preserve migration continuity
      - normalize historical identifiers
      - maintain replay-safe resolution semantics
      - support deterministic canonicalization

    Runtime legitimacy derives exclusively from:
      - canonical ontology identity
      - replay admissibility
      - invariant legality
      - execution surface governance


# ============================================================
# ONTOLOGY
# ============================================================

ontology:

  alias_key_semantics:

    definition: COMPATIBILITY_TOKEN

    topology_independent: true

    replay_safe: true

    filesystem_paths_forbidden: true

    examples:

      valid:

        - constitutional_receipt.py
        - trace_reconstructor.py
        - attestation.yaml
        - EPOCH_0008.yaml

      invalid:

        - afritech/proof/constitutional_receipt.py
        - afritech/trace/trace_reconstructor.py
        - registry/attestation.yaml


  canonical_target_semantics:

    ontology_identity:

      definition: CANONICAL_MODULE_PATH

      examples:

        - afritech.proof.constitutional_receipt
        - afritech.trace.trace_reconstructor
        - afritech.registry.attestation


    filename_normalization:

      definition: REPLAY_SAFE_FILENAME_TARGET

      examples:

        - EPOCH_0008.yaml
        - EPOCH_0009.yaml


# ============================================================
# STATUS MODEL
# ============================================================

status_model:

  CANONICAL:

    replay_safe: true

    admissible: true

    description: >
      Canonical replay-safe identity target.


  MIGRATING:

    replay_safe: true

    admissible: true

    description: >
      Transitional compatibility alias retained for
      deterministic replay continuity and migration
      normalization.


  DEPRECATED:

    replay_safe: conditional

    admissible: false

    description: >
      Historical compatibility alias retained only
      for replay reconstruction visibility.


  FORBIDDEN:

    replay_safe: true

    admissible: false

    description: >
      Explicitly forbidden executable alias retained
      solely for governance visibility and replay-safe
      ontology completeness.


# ============================================================
# ALIASES
# ============================================================

aliases:

  attestation.py:

    canonical: afritech.registry.attestation

    status: FORBIDDEN

    ontology: FORBIDDEN_EXECUTABLE_ALIAS

    replay_safe: true

    description: >
      Executable attestation aliases are constitutionally
      forbidden. Attestation authority must derive from
      canonical registry ontology only.


  attestation.yaml:

    canonical: afritech.registry.attestation

    status: MIGRATING

    ontology: TOKEN_TO_MODULE_PATH

    replay_safe: true

    description: >
      Historical registry compatibility token preserved
      for deterministic replay continuity.


  constitutional_receipt.py:

    canonical: afritech.proof.constitutional_receipt

    status: MIGRATING

    ontology: TOKEN_TO_MODULE_PATH

    replay_safe: true

    description: >
      Compatibility alias preserved for deterministic
      ontology migration normalization.


  trace_reconstructor.py:

    canonical: afritech.trace.trace_reconstructor

    status: MIGRATING

    ontology: TOKEN_TO_MODULE_PATH

    replay_safe: true

    description: >
      Historical replay-trace compatibility alias
      preserved for deterministic canonicalization.


# ============================================================
# CONSTITUTIONAL RULES
# ============================================================

rules:

  - id: PATH_ALIAS_RULE_1

    rule: >
      Alias keys must remain topology-independent
      compatibility identifiers.


  - id: PATH_ALIAS_RULE_2

    rule: >
      Filesystem paths are forbidden as alias keys.


  - id: PATH_ALIAS_RULE_3

    rule: >
      Canonical ontology identity must remain
      independent from repository topology.


  - id: PATH_ALIAS_RULE_4

    rule: >
      Alias normalization must remain deterministic
      and replay-safe.


  - id: PATH_ALIAS_RULE_5

    rule: >
      Forbidden aliases may remain declared for
      governance visibility but are runtime
      inadmissible.


# ============================================================
# CONSTITUTIONAL ASSERTIONS
# ============================================================

constitutional_assertions:

  - >
    Canonical ontology identity must remain
    independent from filesystem topology.

  - >
    Alias keys are compatibility artifacts only
    and must never define constitutional identity.

  - >
    Replay-safe canonicalization requires
    deterministic alias normalization.

  - >
    Governance legitimacy derives from canonical
    ontology identity and replay admissibility,
    not from compatibility aliases.

# CI ENFORCEMENT
# ============================================================

ci_alignment:

  enforced_by:

    - afritech.ci.execution_surface_validation
    - afritech.ci.import_topology_enforcement
    - afritech.ci.replay_validation
    - afritech.ci.witness_validation

  required_checks:

    - no_planned_runtime_execution
    - no_planned_replay_participation
    - no_planned_proof_generation
    - deterministic_identity_validation
    - closed_world_isolation_validation

  failure_mode: CI_FAIL


# ============================================================
# CONSTITUTIONAL ASSERTION
# ============================================================

constitutional_assertion:

  description: >
    Planned surfaces are deterministic declarative
    constitutional artifacts representing architectural
    intent only.

    Planned-surface legitimacy derives exclusively from:
      - canonical ontology declaration
      - deterministic containment semantics
      - replay-safe non-execution
      - closed-world isolation
      - observer-independent resolution

    Planned surfaces must never derive operational legitimacy
    from:
      - filesystem structure
      - runtime activity
      - speculative interpretation
      - observer-relative execution
      - semantic inference

    Planned-surface evaluation must remain:
      - deterministic
      - replay-safe
      - observer-independent
      - ontology-safe
      - constitutionally bounded

===== ./afritech/architecture/surface_authority_registry.yaml =====
schema: afritech.execution_surfaces.v2

version: 2

metadata:

  authority: ARCHITECTURE
  status: ACTIVE
  mutability: CONTROLLED

  registry_class: CONSTITUTIONAL_EXECUTION_SURFACES

  description: >
    Canonical constitutional execution-surface registry
    governing deterministic execution authority,
    replay participation semantics, mutation authority,
    proof participation, runtime activation legitimacy,
    and closed-world execution topology within AfriTech.

    Execution surfaces define:
      - constitutional execution authority
      - replay participation semantics
      - mutation authority boundaries
      - proof participation boundaries
      - deterministic execution legitimacy
      - ontology-safe surface identity
      - closed-world execution participation
      - invariant-preserving operational authority

    Execution surfaces are constitutional operational
    boundaries only.

    Surface legitimacy does NOT independently confer:
      - governance sovereignty
      - constitutional supremacy
      - unrestricted mutation authority
      - observer-relative execution authority

    Execution participation remains bounded by:
      - admissibility law
      - invariant preservation
      - deterministic execution
      - replay-safe semantics
      - canonical ontology resolution
      - closed-world execution semantics


# ============================================================
# PATH ONTOLOGY ALIGNMENT
# ============================================================

ontology_alignment:

  canonical_identity_form: module_path

  forbidden_identity_forms:

    - filesystem_path
    - extension_identity
    - relative_identity
    - symbolic_short_name
    - reflection_based_identity

  deterministic_resolution_required: true

  replay_safe_resolution_required: true

  observer_independent_required: true

  description: >
    Execution surface identity resolution requires
    deterministic canonical module-path ontology semantics.


# ============================================================
# IMPLEMENTATION STATES
# ============================================================

implementation_states:

  PLANNED:

    executable: false

    runtime_admissible: false

    replay_participating: false

    proof_admissible: false

    replay_safe: false

    deterministic_execution: false


  PARTIAL:

    executable: constrained

    runtime_admissible: conditional

    replay_participating: conditional

    proof_admissible: conditional

    replay_safe: conditional

    deterministic_execution: conditional


  IMPLEMENTED:

    executable: true

    runtime_admissible: true

    replay_participating: true

    proof_admissible: true

    replay_safe: true

    deterministic_execution: true


  DOCUMENTARY:

    executable: false

    runtime_admissible: false

    replay_participating: false

    proof_admissible: false

    replay_safe: false

    deterministic_execution: false


  FORBIDDEN_ALIAS:

    executable: false

    runtime_admissible: false

    replay_participating: false

    proof_admissible: false

    replay_safe: false

    deterministic_execution: false


# ============================================================
# EXECUTION SURFACES
# ============================================================

surfaces:

  # ----------------------------------------------------------
  # RUNTIME ACTIVATION
  # ----------------------------------------------------------

  runtime_activation:

    canonical_identity:
      afritech.runtime.activation

    implementation_state:
      IMPLEMENTED

    ontology:
      CANONICAL_MODULE_PATH

    category:
      RUNTIME

    replay_significance:
      CRITICAL

    deterministic_required:
      true

    replay_safe_required:
      true

    closed_world_required:
      true

    runtime_admissible:
      true

    proof_admissible:
      true

    replay_participating:
      true

    authority_owner:

      - afritech.runtime.activation
      - afritech.runtime.admission
      - afritech.runtime.replay

    mutation_authority:

      - epoch_evolution_only

    mutation_constraints:

      - invariant_preservation_required
      - deterministic_transition_required
      - replay_traceability_required
      - closed_world_execution_required

    authority_scope:

      - runtime_activation
      - execution_admission
      - replay_execution
      - execution_surface_binding
      - deterministic_runtime_control

    witness_dependencies:

      - afritech.proof.constitutional_receipt
      - afritech.proof.witness.execution_witness
      - afritech.proof.witness.replay_witness
      - afritech.proof.witness.witness_bundle

    enforced_by:

      - afritech.ci.execution_surface_validation
      - afritech.ci.replay_validation
      - afritech.runtime.admission

    guarantees:

      - deterministic_runtime_activation
      - replay_safe_execution
      - invariant_preserving_execution
      - closed_world_execution

    forbidden:

      - observer_relative_activation
      - probabilistic_execution
      - undeclared_execution_surfaces
      - reflection_based_runtime_binding
      - speculative_runtime_execution

    description: >
      Canonical deterministic runtime activation surface
      governing replay-safe operational execution within
      AfriTech.


  # ----------------------------------------------------------
  # PROOF
  # ----------------------------------------------------------

  proof:

    canonical_identity:
      afritech.proof

    implementation_state:
      PARTIAL

    ontology:
      CANONICAL_MODULE_PATH

    category:
      PROOF

    replay_significance:
      REQUIRED

    deterministic_required:
      true

    replay_safe_required:
      true

    closed_world_required:
      true

    runtime_admissible:
      conditional

    proof_admissible:
      true

    replay_participating:
      true

    authority_owner:

      - afritech.proof
      - afritech.proof.witness
      - afritech.proof.formal

    mutation_authority:

      - proof_artifact_generation_only

    mutation_constraints:

      - replay_traceability_required
      - invariant_preservation_required
      - deterministic_proof_generation_required

    authority_scope:

      - witness_generation
      - replay_attestation
      - constitutional_receipt_generation
      - transcript_validation
      - mutation_trace_validation
      - deterministic_proof_binding

    witness_dependencies:

      - afritech.proof.witness.replay_witness
      - afritech.proof.witness.execution_witness
      - afritech.proof.witness.transcript_witness
      - afritech.proof.witness.mutation_witness
      - afritech.proof.witness.witness_bundle

    enforced_by:

      - afritech.ci.witness_validation
      - afritech.ci.replay_validation

    guarantees:

      - deterministic_proof_generation
      - replay_safe_attestation
      - invariant_preserving_validation
      - deterministic_receipt_generation

    missing_capabilities:

      - global_replay_equivalence_validation
      - full_execution_lineage_attestation
      - multi_epoch_replay_validation

    forbidden:

      - observer_relative_proof
      - speculative_proof_generation
      - probabilistic_reconstruction
      - undeclared_witness_generation

    description: >
      Deterministic constitutional proof surface governing
      replay attestation and witness admissibility.


# ============================================================
# REPLAY ALIGNMENT
# ============================================================

replay_alignment:

  replay_safe_states:

    - PARTIAL
    - IMPLEMENTED

  replay_forbidden_states:

    - PLANNED
    - DOCUMENTARY
    - FORBIDDEN_ALIAS

  replay_requirements:

    - deterministic_execution
    - replay_traceability
    - witness_admissibility
    - invariant_preservation
    - canonical_identity_resolution

  replay_invalidators:

    - replay_divergence
    - observer_relative_execution
    - speculative_runtime_execution
    - undeclared_execution_surfaces

  description: >
    Replay participation requires constitutionally
    admissible deterministic execution surfaces.


# ============================================================
# MUTATION AUTHORITY POLICY
# ============================================================

mutation_authority_policy:

  allowed_mutation_scopes:

    - epoch_evolution_only
    - proof_artifact_generation_only
    - deterministic_state_transition
    - replay_trace_generation

  forbidden_mutation_scopes:

    - unrestricted_runtime_mutation
    - observer_relative_mutation
    - hidden_mutation
    - probabilistic_mutation
    - undeclared_state_transition

  mutation_requirements:

    - invariant_preservation
    - deterministic_ordering
    - replay_traceability
    - witness_generation

  description: >
    Mutation authority is constitutionally bounded and
    replay-traceable.


# ============================================================
# CLOSED-WORLD ALIGNMENT
# ============================================================

closed_world_alignment:

  required:

    - declared_execution_surfaces
    - canonical_identity_resolution
    - deterministic_surface_binding
    - replay_safe_execution

  forbidden:

    - implicit_surface_discovery
    - reflection_based_execution
    - dynamic_runtime_aliasing
    - undeclared_execution_binding

  description: >
    Execution surface admissibility requires closed-world
    execution semantics.


# ============================================================
# SAFETY GUARANTEES
# ============================================================

safety:

  guarantees:

    - deterministic_surface_resolution
    - replay_safe_execution
    - observer_independent_evaluation
    - invariant_preserving_mutation
    - ontology_safe_execution

  forbid:

    - implicit_runtime_legitimacy
    - filesystem_authority_inference
    - speculative_execution_authority
    - observer_relative_execution
    - ambiguous_surface_resolution

  enforcement:

    violation_action: FAIL_FAST

    replay_violation_action: REPLAY_INVALID

    runtime_violation_action: EXECUTION_REFUSAL


# ============================================================
# FAILURE EFFECTS
# ============================================================

failure_effects:

  replay_divergence:

    effect:

      - replay_invalid
      - proof_rejection
      - execution_refusal


  closed_world_violation:

    effect:

      - runtime_refusal
      - ontology_failure


  forbidden_mutation_scope:

    effect:

      - mutation_rejection
      - replay_invalid


  observer_relative_execution:

    effect:

      - proof_non_admissible
      - replay_rejection


  forbidden_alias_resolution:

    effect:

      - identity_rejection
      - CI_failure


# ============================================================
# GLOBAL CONSTITUTIONAL RULES
# ============================================================

rules:

  - id: EXECUTION_SURFACE_RULE_1
    rule: >
      Execution surface identity must resolve exclusively
      through canonical module-path ontology semantics.

  - id: EXECUTION_SURFACE_RULE_2
    rule: >
      Runtime activation requires:
        - deterministic execution
        - replay-safe semantics
        - invariant preservation
        - closed-world execution alignment

  - id: EXECUTION_SURFACE_RULE_3
    rule: >
      Mutation authority must remain constitutionally bounded
      and replay-traceable.

  - id: EXECUTION_SURFACE_RULE_4
    rule: >
      Filesystem artifacts must never independently define
      execution-surface legitimacy.

  - id: EXECUTION_SURFACE_RULE_5
    rule: >
      Replay participation requires deterministic replay-safe
      execution semantics.

  - id: EXECUTION_SURFACE_RULE_6
    rule: >
      Reflection-based execution binding is constitutionally
      forbidden.

  - id: EXECUTION_SURFACE_RULE_7
    rule: >
      Observer-relative execution evaluation is constitutionally
      forbidden.

  - id: EXECUTION_SURFACE_RULE_8
    rule: >
      Execution surface resolution must remain:
        - deterministic
        - replay-safe
        - observer-independent
        - ontology-safe
        - constitutionally bounded

  description: >
    Constitutional execution surfaces govern deterministic
    replay-safe operational participation within AfriTech.

    Surface legitimacy derives exclusively from:
      - canonical ontology resolution
      - deterministic execution
      - replay-safe semantics
      - invariant preservation
      - closed-world execution semantics

    Surface legitimacy must never derive from:
      - filesystem structure
      - runtime activity alone
      - speculative interpretation
      - observer-relative execution
      - semantic inference

    Execution surface resolution must remain:
      - deterministic
      - replay-safe
      - observer-independent
      - ontology-safe
      - constitutionally bounded

metadata:

  authority: ARCHITECTURE
  status: ACTIVE
  mutability: CONTROLLED

  registry_class: CONSTITUTIONAL_BINDING_REGISTRY

  description: >
    Canonical constitutional binding registry governing
    replay-safe implementation bindings, execution
    admissibility bindings, runtime activation semantics,
    proof participation semantics, evaluation semantics,
    speculative doctrine containment, and deterministic
    binding resolution within AfriTech.

    Bindings define:
      - implementation legitimacy
      - execution admissibility
      - replay participation
      - proof participation
      - runtime activation authority
      - speculative containment semantics
      - deterministic binding resolution
      - closed-world binding alignment

    Binding legitimacy is constitutional metadata only.

    Binding legitimacy does NOT independently confer:
      - runtime sovereignty
      - governance authority
      - replay authority
      - execution legitimacy
      - constitutional authority

    Binding participation remains bounded by:
      - admissibility law
      - replay admissibility
      - invariant preservation
      - deterministic execution
      - canonical ontology resolution
      - closed-world execution semantics

    Binding legitimacy must never derive from:
      - filesystem structure
      - runtime activity alone
      - speculative interpretation
      - observer-relative evaluation
      - semantic inference

    Binding resolution must remain:
      - deterministic
      - replay-safe
      - observer-independent
      - ontology-safe
      - constitutionally bounded

===== ./afritech/bootstrap/BOOTSTRAP_AUTHORITY.yaml =====
bootstrap_authority:

  authoritative_entrypoints:

    - afritech.bootstrap.engine.constitutional_bootstrap

  responsibilities:

    - constitutional_bootstrap
    - runtime_initialization
    - invariant_validation
    - semantic_guard_loading
    - replay_guard_loading
    - authority_guard_loading

  forbidden:

    - direct_runtime_execution
    - replay_mutation
    - epoch_mutation
    - speculative_runtime_loading

  guarantees:

    - deterministic_bootstrap_order
    - invariant_prevalidation
    - authority_before_execution

===== ./afritech/ci/governance_size_policy.yaml =====
schema: afritech.ci.governance_size_policy.v1
thresholds:
  max_yaml_files: 150
  max_yaml_bytes: 200000
  compression_audit_ratio: 0.9
failure:
  block_merge: true
  trigger_compression_audit: true

===== ./afritech/constitution/INVARIANTS.yaml =====
schema: afritech.constitution.invariants.v1

meta:
  description: >
    Canonical registry of constitutional invariants.
    Defines execution, replay, and governance constraints.
  authority: registry
  enforcement: REQUIRED
  mutability: FORBIDDEN
  deterministic: true
  replay_safe: true
  ordering: canonical
  canonical_invariant_count: 30


invariants:

# ---------------------------------------------------------
# EXECUTION BOUNDARY
# ---------------------------------------------------------

- id: I1_EXPLICIT_INPUT_BOUNDARY
  category: EXECUTION_BOUNDARY
  runtime_scope: PRE
  description: >
    Execution MUST operate only on explicitly provided RuntimeContext inputs.
  constitutional_assertion: >
    ALL(runtime_context.inputs ARE explicit AND declared)
  enforcement: { runtime: true, replay: true, governance: false }

- id: I2_EXPLICIT_OUTPUT_BOUNDARY
  category: EXECUTION_BOUNDARY
  runtime_scope: POST
  description: >
    All outputs MUST be fully contained within ExecutionResult.
  constitutional_assertion: >
    outputs subset_of ExecutionResult.outputs
  enforcement: { runtime: true, replay: true, governance: false }

- id: I14_BOUND_EXECUTION_SURFACE
  category: EXECUTION_BOUNDARY
  runtime_scope: PRE
  description: >
    Execution MUST remain within declared runtime surfaces.
  constitutional_assertion: >
    execution_surface subset_of declared_surfaces
  enforcement: { runtime: true, replay: false, governance: false }

- id: I15_NO_DYNAMIC_BEHAVIOR_INJECTION
  category: EXECUTION_BOUNDARY
  runtime_scope: PRE
  description: >
    Execution logic MUST NOT be injected dynamically.
  constitutional_assertion: >
    execution_logic IS static_during_runtime
  enforcement: { runtime: true, replay: false, governance: false }


# ---------------------------------------------------------
# STATE INTEGRITY
# ---------------------------------------------------------

- id: I3_NO_SILENT_MUTATION
  category: STATE_INTEGRITY
  runtime_scope: DURING
  description: >
    No state mutation without trace visibility.
  constitutional_assertion: >
    ALL(state_changes ARE recorded_in_trace)
  enforcement: { runtime: true, replay: true, governance: false }

- id: I19_STATE_TRANSITION_EXPLICIT
  category: STATE_INTEGRITY
  runtime_scope: DURING
  description: >
    All state transitions MUST be declared.
  constitutional_assertion: >
    ALL(state_transitions ARE explicitly_declared)
  enforcement: { runtime: true, replay: true, governance: false }

- id: I20_NO_HIDDEN_SIDE_EFFECTS
  category: STATE_INTEGRITY
  runtime_scope: DURING
  description: >
    No hidden side effects allowed.
  constitutional_assertion: >
    effects subset_of observable_trace
  enforcement: { runtime: true, replay: true, governance: false }


# ---------------------------------------------------------
# REPLAY INTEGRITY
# ---------------------------------------------------------

- id: I4_DETERMINISTIC_EXECUTION
  category: REPLAY_INTEGRITY
  runtime_scope: POST
  description: >
    Identical inputs MUST produce identical outputs and traces.
  constitutional_assertion: >
    inputs₁ = inputs₂ implies outputs₁ = outputs₂ AND trace₁ = trace₂
  enforcement: { runtime: true, replay: true, governance: false }

- id: I5_REPLAY_REQUIRED
  category: REPLAY_INTEGRITY
  runtime_scope: REPLAY
  description: >
    All executions MUST be replayable.
  constitutional_assertion: >
    for_all execution exists replay(execution)
  enforcement: { runtime: false, replay: true, governance: false }

- id: I6_REPLAY_AUTHORITY
  category: REPLAY_INTEGRITY
  runtime_scope: REPLAY
  description: >
    Replay results are authoritative.
  constitutional_assertion: >
    replay_result = canonical_truth
  enforcement: { runtime: false, replay: true, governance: false }

- id: I7_TRANSCRIPT_COMPLETENESS
  category: REPLAY_INTEGRITY
  runtime_scope: POST
  description: >
    Execution traces MUST fully reconstruct behavior.
  constitutional_assertion: >
    trace implies reconstruct(execution)
  enforcement: { runtime: true, replay: true, governance: false }

- id: I8_TRANSCRIPT_HASH_STABILITY
  category: REPLAY_INTEGRITY
  runtime_scope: REPLAY
  description: >
    Replay hashes MUST remain stable.
  constitutional_assertion: >
    hash(trace₁) = hash(trace₂) IF equivalent_execution
  enforcement: { runtime: false, replay: true, governance: false }


# ---------------------------------------------------------
# CLOSED WORLD
# ---------------------------------------------------------

- id: I9_CLOSED_WORLD
  category: CLOSED_WORLD_ENFORCEMENT
  runtime_scope: PRE
  description: >
    No undeclared external access allowed.
  constitutional_assertion: >
    execution_inputs subset_of declared_inputs
  enforcement: { runtime: true, replay: true, governance: false }

- id: I10_EXPLICIT_DEPENDENCIES
  category: CLOSED_WORLD_ENFORCEMENT
  runtime_scope: GOVERNANCE
  description: >
    All dependencies MUST be declared.
  constitutional_assertion: >
    dependencies subset_of declared_dependencies
  enforcement: { runtime: true, replay: true, governance: false }


# ---------------------------------------------------------
# GOVERNANCE
# ---------------------------------------------------------

- id: I11_AUTHORITY_DECLARATION
  category: GOVERNANCE_CONTROL
  runtime_scope: GOVERNANCE
  description: >
    Authority MUST be explicitly declared.
  constitutional_assertion: >
    authority ∈ approved_ADRs
  enforcement: { runtime: false, replay: false, governance: true }

- id: I12_NO_AUTHORITY_ESCALATION
  category: GOVERNANCE_CONTROL
  runtime_scope: GOVERNANCE
  description: >
    No component may escalate authority.
  constitutional_assertion: >
    authority_runtime ≤ authority_declared
  enforcement: { runtime: true, replay: false, governance: true }

- id: I13_ADR_REQUIRED_FOR_MUTATION
  category: GOVERNANCE_CONTROL
  runtime_scope: GOVERNANCE
  description: >
    Changes require ADR approval.
  constitutional_assertion: >
    mutation implies approved_ADR
  enforcement: { runtime: false, replay: false, governance: true }


# ---------------------------------------------------------
# EXECUTION FINALITY
# ---------------------------------------------------------

- id: I16_TOTAL_OUTCOME_DECLARATION
  category: EXECUTION_FINALITY
  runtime_scope: POST
  description: >
    Execution MUST resolve to final outcome.
  constitutional_assertion: >
    execution implies exists final_outcome
  enforcement: { runtime: true, replay: true, governance: false }

- id: I17_DETERMINISTIC_FAILURE
  category: EXECUTION_FINALITY
  runtime_scope: POST
  description: >
    Failures MUST be reproducible.
  constitutional_assertion: >
    failure(inputs₁) = failure(inputs₂)
  enforcement: { runtime: true, replay: true, governance: false }

- id: I18_REPLAYABLE_REFUSAL
  category: EXECUTION_FINALITY
  runtime_scope: POST
  description: >
    Refusals MUST be replay-consistent.
  constitutional_assertion: >
    refusal_replay(inputs) = refusal_original(inputs)
  enforcement: { runtime: true, replay: true, governance: false }


# ---------------------------------------------------------
# TEMPORAL INTEGRITY
# ---------------------------------------------------------

- id: I21_DETERMINISTIC_ORDERING
  category: TEMPORAL_INTEGRITY
  runtime_scope: DURING
  description: >
    Execution ordering MUST be deterministic.
  constitutional_assertion: >
    order(execution₁) = order(execution₂)
  enforcement: { runtime: true, replay: true, governance: false }

- id: I22_TIME_SOURCE_CONTROL
  category: TEMPORAL_INTEGRITY
  runtime_scope: DURING
  description: >
    Time MUST be controlled and replay-stable.
  constitutional_assertion: >
    time_source ∈ controlled_sources
  enforcement: { runtime: true, replay: true, governance: false }


# ---------------------------------------------------------
# DATA INTEGRITY
# ---------------------------------------------------------

- id: I23_INPUT_IMMUTABILITY
  category: DATA_INTEGRITY
  runtime_scope: DURING
  description: >
    Inputs MUST remain immutable.
  constitutional_assertion: >
    inputs(t0) = inputs(tn)
  enforcement: { runtime: true, replay: false, governance: false }

- id: I24_OUTPUT_INTEGRITY
  category: DATA_INTEGRITY
  runtime_scope: POST
  description: >
    Outputs MUST be verifiable.
  constitutional_assertion: >
    outputs ARE deterministic_and_verifiable
  enforcement: { runtime: true, replay: true, governance: false }


# ---------------------------------------------------------
# CLASSIFICATION
# ---------------------------------------------------------

- id: I25_CLASSIFICATION_IS_POST_EXECUTION

  runtime_scope: REPLAY
  description: >
    Classification occurs after execution.
  constitutional_assertion: >

  enforcement: { runtime: false, replay: true, governance: false }

- id: I26_CLASSIFICATION_REPLAY_ALIGNMENT

  constitutional_assertion: >

- id: I27_NO_CLASSIFICATION_SIDE_EFFECT

  runtime_scope: REPLAY
  description: >
    Classification does not modify outputs.
  constitutional_assertion: >
    classification DOES NOT modify(outputs, trace)
  enforcement: { runtime: false, replay: true, governance: false }


# ---------------------------------------------------------

# ---------------------------------------------------------

  description: >

  constitutional_assertion: >

  enforcement: { runtime: true, replay: true, governance: false }
