schema: afritech.concept.admissibility.v1

version: 1

metadata:
  authority: CONSTITUTION
  status: ACTIVE
  mutability: CONTROLLED
  concept_class: CANONICAL_CONCEPT
  description: >
    Canonical constitutional definition of admissibility within AfriTech.

    Admissibility governs whether a surface, execution artifact,
    replay artifact, transcript, receipt, mutation, or runtime
    action may constitutionally participate in:
      - runtime execution
      - replay verification
      - governance evaluation
      - constitutional enforcement
      - proof generation

    Admissibility is a constitutional validation property.


# ============================================================
# ✅ CANONICAL CONCEPT IDENTITY
# ============================================================

concept:
  id: CONCEPT_ADMISSIBILITY
  canonical_name: admissibility

  # ✅ REQUIRED NORMALIZED FIELD
  name: admissibility

  # ✅ REQUIRED NORMALIZED FIELD
  domain:
    - runtime
    - replay
    - governance
    - enforcement

  constitutional_domain:
    - runtime
    - replay
    - governance
    - proof
    - enforcement

  authoritative_sources:
    - afritech.constitution.invariants_semantics
    - afritech.architecture.execution_surfaces
    - afritech.architecture.enforcement_matrix
    - afritech.architecture.implementation_registry
    - afritech.epoch.epoch_semantics


# ============================================================
# ✅ CORE DEFINITION
# ============================================================

definition:

  # ✅ REQUIRED NORMALIZED FIELD
  summary: >
    Admissibility defines whether an entity may constitutionally
    participate in execution, replay, governance, or enforcement.

  # ✅ REQUIRED NORMALIZED FIELD
  requires:
    - canonical_identity_resolution
    - deterministic_execution
    - execution_surface_declaration
    - invariant_alignment
    - replay_legitimacy
    - authority_alignment

  # ✅ REQUIRED NORMALIZED FIELD
  forbidden_when:
    - identity_is_ambiguous
    - execution_surface_is_undeclared
    - replay_legitimacy_fails
    - invariant_violation_exists
    - forbidden_alias_detected
    - authority_boundary_violated
    - speculative_surface_used_operationally

  canonical_statement: >
    Admissibility is the constitutional determination that an
    artifact, execution surface, runtime action, replay trace,
    governance declaration, or enforcement surface may lawfully
    participate within the AfriTech constitutional system.


# ============================================================
# ✅ NORMALIZED CI PROJECTION (CRITICAL)

enforcement_points:
  - afritech.ci.witness_validator
  - afritech.ci.import_topology_enforcement
  - afritech.ci.semantic_concept_validator

  - replay_witness
  - execution_witness
  - transcript_witness
  - mutation_witness

  - invariant_preservation
  - canonical_identity_resolution
  - replay_traceability

# ============================================================

domains:

  runtime:
    requires:
      - implementation_state_admissible
      - execution_surface_declared
      - invariant_alignment
      - replay_safe_operation
    forbidden:
      - speculative_execution
      - forbidden_alias_resolution

    forbidden:

    forbidden:

      - runtime_policy_mutation

    replay:
      - PARTIAL
      - IMPLEMENTED

  forbidden_states:
    - PLANNED
    - DOCUMENTARY
    - FORBIDDEN_ALIAS

  description: >

    but does not independently confer constitutional authority.

  forbidden_identity_forms:

    - conceptual_identity

  # ✅ FULL DOCTRINAL DESCRIPTION PRESERVED

    Constitutional admissibility is the deterministic and
    observer-independent validation boundary governing lawful
    participation within the AfriTech constitutional system.

    Admissibility derives from:
      - canonical identity
      - deterministic execution semantics
      - replay legitimacy
      - invariant alignment
      - constitutional authority boundaries

      - replay_invalid

    effect:
      - invariant_violation
      - replay_divergence

# ============================================================

  - id: DETERMINISM_RULE_1
    rule: >
      Equivalent inputs must produce identical outputs.

  - id: DETERMINISM_RULE_2
    rule: >
      Observer-relative execution is forbidden.

  - id: DETERMINISM_RULE_3
    rule: >
      Reflection-based execution is forbidden.

# ============================================================

constitutional_assertion:

  # ✅ REQUIRED
  statement: >
    Execution must be deterministic, replay-safe, and invariant-preserving.

  # ✅ FULL DOCTRINE
  description: >
    Deterministic execution defines the constitutional requirement
    that all admissible execution produces replay-equivalent,
    observer-independent results under equivalent conditions.

    Determinism derives from canonical identity, invariant
    preservation, replay-safe execution, and controlled mutation.

    Execution must never depend on observer identity, filesystem
    structure, speculative behavior, or undeclared surfaces.

===== ./afritech/constitution/invariants_semantics.yaml =====
# =========================================================
# AFRITECH INVARIANT SEMANTICS REGISTRY
# =========================================================

schema: afritech.constitution.invariants.semantics.v1

meta:
  description: >
    Semantic interpretation layer for constitutional invariants.

    This file provides controlled semantic annotations used for:
      - audit understanding
      - classification alignment
      - documentation
      - tooling interpretation

    This layer DOES NOT introduce behavior.
    Execution authority remains in IR and runtime layers.

  authority: derived
  mutability: GOVERNED
  deterministic: true
  replay_safe: true


# =========================================================
# SEMANTIC DEFINITIONS
# =========================================================

semantics:

  # =====================================================
  # EXECUTION BOUNDARY
  # =====================================================

  I1_EXPLICIT_INPUT_BOUNDARY:
    meaning: input_is_closed_set
    interpretation: >
      Execution depends strictly on declared RuntimeContext inputs.
    semantic_tags: [boundary, input, determinism]

  I2_EXPLICIT_OUTPUT_BOUNDARY:
    meaning: output_is_fully_declared
    interpretation: >
      Execution produces only explicitly declared outputs.
    semantic_tags: [boundary, output, containment]

  I14_BOUND_EXECUTION_SURFACE:
    meaning: execution_surface_is_closed
    interpretation: >
      Execution cannot escape defined runtime boundaries.
    semantic_tags: [surface, isolation]

  I15_NO_DYNAMIC_BEHAVIOR_INJECTION:
    meaning: execution_is_static
    interpretation: >
      Behavior cannot be modified during execution.
    semantic_tags: [immutability, safety]


  # =====================================================
  # STATE INTEGRITY
  # =====================================================

  I3_NO_SILENT_MUTATION:
    meaning: mutation_requires_visibility
    interpretation: >
      All state changes must be observable in trace.
    semantic_tags: [mutation, traceability]

  I19_STATE_TRANSITION_EXPLICIT:
    meaning: transitions_are_declared
    interpretation: >
      Every state transition must be formally declared.
    semantic_tags: [state, transitions]

  I20_NO_HIDDEN_SIDE_EFFECTS:
    meaning: no_untracked_effects
    interpretation: >
      No hidden or implicit side effects exist.
    semantic_tags: [effects, trace]


  # =====================================================
  # REPLAY INTEGRITY
  # =====================================================

  I4_DETERMINISTIC_EXECUTION:
    meaning: same_input_same_output
    interpretation: >
      Execution must always produce identical outcomes for identical inputs.
    semantic_tags: [determinism, replay]

  I5_REPLAY_REQUIRED:
    meaning: execution_must_be_replayable
    interpretation: >
      System must support full replay of all executions.
    semantic_tags: [replay, validation]

  I6_REPLAY_AUTHORITY:
    meaning: replay_is_source_of_truth
    interpretation: >
      Replay defines behavioral correctness.
    semantic_tags: [authority, replay]

  I7_TRANSCRIPT_COMPLETENESS:
    meaning: trace_is_complete
    interpretation: >
      Execution trace must fully describe behavior.
    semantic_tags: [trace, completeness]

  I8_TRANSCRIPT_HASH_STABILITY:
    meaning: hash_is_stable
    interpretation: >
      Replay hashes must remain identical across runs.
    semantic_tags: [hash, determinism]


  # =====================================================
  # CLOSED WORLD
  # =====================================================

  I9_CLOSED_WORLD:
    meaning: no_external_dependency
    interpretation: >
      Execution cannot depend on undeclared external systems.
    semantic_tags: [closed_world, dependency]

  I10_EXPLICIT_DEPENDENCIES:
    meaning: dependencies_are_declared
    interpretation: >
      All dependencies must be explicitly defined.
    semantic_tags: [dependency, declaration]


  # =====================================================
  # GOVERNANCE
  # =====================================================

  I11_AUTHORITY_DECLARATION:
    meaning: authority_is_declared
    interpretation: >
      Authority must be formally defined via governance.
    semantic_tags: [authority, governance]

  I12_NO_AUTHORITY_ESCALATION:
    meaning: no_privilege_escalation
    interpretation: >
      Components cannot exceed authorized roles.
    semantic_tags: [security, governance]

  I13_ADR_REQUIRED_FOR_MUTATION:
    meaning: change_requires_adr
    interpretation: >
      System evolution requires governance approval.
    semantic_tags: [change_management]


  # =====================================================

  # =====================================================

  I16_TOTAL_OUTCOME_DECLARATION:
    meaning: outcome_is_complete
    interpretation: >
      Every execution must resolve fully.
    semantic_tags: [finality]

  I17_DETERMINISTIC_FAILURE:

    interpretation: >

    semantic_tags: [failure, replay]

  I18_REPLAYABLE_REFUSAL:
    meaning: refusal_is_stable
    interpretation: >

    semantic_tags: [refusal]


  # =====================================================

  # =====================================================

    semantic_tags: [data, immutability]

  I24_OUTPUT_INTEGRITY:

    semantic_tags: [data, verification]


  # =====================================================

===== ./afritech/constitution/meta.yaml =====
#====================================================
# The system governs not only execution,
# but the structure of meaning itself.
#====================================================

schema: afritech.constitution.meta.v3

meta:
  authority: constitutional
  enforcement: REQUIRED
  mutability: FORBIDDEN

  guarantees:
    - SEM-DET-001
    - SEM-RPL-001
    - SEM-CW-001
    - SEM-ID-001
    - SEM-ADM-001


#====================================================
# META PRINCIPLES (CANONICAL + ATOMIC)
#====================================================

meta_principles:

  #--------------------------------------------------
  # SEMANTIC MINIMALITY
  #--------------------------------------------------

  - id: META-001
    guarantees: [SEM-ADM-001]

    rule: SEMANTIC_MINIMALITY

    assertion: |
      semantics = canonical_minimal_set

    enforcement:
      semantic_registry_required: true
      duplicate_semantics_forbidden: true


  #--------------------------------------------------
  # TRACEABLE ENFORCEMENT
  #--------------------------------------------------

  - id: META-002
    guarantees: [SEM-RPL-001, SEM-ID-001]

    rule: ENFORCEMENT_TRACEABILITY

    assertion: |
      enforcement → semantic_atom_reference

    enforcement:
      semantic_reference_required: true
      orphan_enforcement_forbidden: true


  #--------------------------------------------------
  # CLOSED-WORLD SEMANTICS
  #--------------------------------------------------

  - id: META-003
    guarantees: [SEM-CW-001]

    rule: CLOSED_WORLD_SEMANTICS

    assertion: |
      semantics ⊆ declared_semantic_atoms

    enforcement:
      undeclared_semantics_forbidden: true
      dynamic_semantics_forbidden: true


  #--------------------------------------------------
  # DETERMINISTIC INTERPRETATION
  #--------------------------------------------------

  - id: META-004
    guarantees: [SEM-DET-001]

    rule: DETERMINISTIC_MEANING

    assertion: |
      identical_input → identical_interpretation

    enforcement:
      interpretation_deterministic: true
      replay_consistent: true


  #--------------------------------------------------
  # SEMANTIC / EXECUTION SEPARATION
  #--------------------------------------------------

  - id: META-005
    guarantees: [SEM-ID-001]

    rule: SEMANTIC_EXECUTION_SEPARATION

    assertion: |
      semantics ≠ execution_mechanics
      AND semantics → admissibility_constraints

    enforcement:
      execution_independence_required: true
      admissibility_semantic_control: true


  #--------------------------------------------------
  # REPLAY-BASED CONSISTENCY
  #--------------------------------------------------

  - id: META-006
    guarantees: [SEM-RPL-001, SEM-ADM-001]

    rule: REPLAY_SEMANTIC_CONSISTENCY

    assertion: |
      replay ⇒ semantic_consistency

    enforcement:
      replay_verification_required: true
      semantic_alignment_required: true


#====================================================
# META DEPENDENCY GRAPH (STRICT DAG)
#====================================================

meta_dependencies:

  META-002:
    depends_on: [META-001]

  META-003:
    depends_on: [META-001]

  META-004:
    depends_on: [META-003]

  META-005:
    depends_on: [META-002]

  META-006:
    depends_on: [META-002, META-004]


#====================================================
# GLOBAL ENFORCEMENT (CI + RUNTIME)
#====================================================

enforcement:

  semantic_directionality:
    core_only_definition: true
    downward_flow_required: true
    upward_definition_forbidden: true

  semantic_usage:
    atom_reference_only: true
    freeform_semantics_forbidden: true

  system_integrity:
    closed_world_enforced: true
    deterministic_interpretation_enforced: true


#====================================================
# CI POLICY (BLOCKING)
#====================================================

ci:

  required_checks:
    - semantic_atom_reference_required
    - no_duplicate_semantic_expression
    - meta_dependency_acyclic
    - no_undeclared_semantics
    - deterministic_interpretation_verified
    - semantic_traceability_complete

  failure_policy:
    block_merge: true
    block_release: true


#====================================================
# DRIFT PREVENTION
#====================================================

drift_control:

  semantic_equivalence_detection: REQUIRED
  duplicate_meaning_detection: REQUIRED
  semantic_hash_alignment: REQUIRED


#====================================================
# VALIDATION LAYERS (STRUCTURAL)
#====================================================

validation:

  semantic_layer:
    canonical_atoms_only: true
    registry_required: true

  enforcement_layer:
    semantic_trace_required: true
    invariant_mapping_required: true

  interpretation_layer:
    deterministic_only: true
    replay_consistency_required: true

  boundary_layer:
    closed_world_required: true
    undefined_semantics_forbidden: true

===== ./afritech/constitution/path_ontology.yaml =====
schema: afritech.path.ontology.v2

rules:

  # =========================================================
  # GLOBAL IGNORE
  # =========================================================
  ignore_patterns:
    - "__pycache__"
    - "*.pyc"
    - ".DS_Store"
    - "*.tmp"
    - "*.bak"

  # =========================================================
  # EXPLICIT ALLOWED FILES
  # =========================================================
  allowed_exceptions:
    - "__init__.py"

  # =========================================================
  # STRICT EXECUTION TOPOLOGY
  #
  # Runtime/core paths are constitutionally enforced.
  # These must remain deterministic and machine-safe.
  # =========================================================
  strict_paths:
    - "ecosystems/**/runtime/**"
    - "ecosystems/**/core/**"
    - "afritech/runtime/**"

  strict_rules:

    # ---------------------------------------------------------
    # lowercase enforcement
    # ---------------------------------------------------------
    lowercase_only: true

    # ---------------------------------------------------------
    # snake_case enforcement
    # ---------------------------------------------------------
    snake_case_only: true

    # ---------------------------------------------------------
    # whitespace forbidden
    # ---------------------------------------------------------
    no_spaces: true

    # ---------------------------------------------------------
    # allowed file extensions
    # ---------------------------------------------------------
    allowed_extensions:
      - ".py"
      - ".yaml"
      - ".yml"
      - ".json"
      - ".toml"
      - ".md"

    # ---------------------------------------------------------
    # malformed / forbidden naming patterns
    # ---------------------------------------------------------
    forbidden_patterns:

      # duplicated pluralization
      - ".*usecasess.*"
      - ".*casess$"
      - ".*ssess$"

      # double underscore forbidden
      - ".*__.*"

      # temporary artifacts
      - ".*~$"
      - ".*\\.tmp$"

  # =========================================================
  # GOVERNANCE / CONSTITUTION
  #
  # Governance artifacts are typed constitutional objects.
  # =========================================================
  governance_paths:
    - "**/governance/**"
    - "**/constitution/**"
    - "**/registry/**"

  governance_rules:

    # ---------------------------------------------------------
    # structured constitutional artifacts
    # ---------------------------------------------------------
    structured_patterns:

      # RULE artifacts
      - "^RULE-[0-9]{4}-[a-z0-9\\-]+\\.yaml$"

      # ADR artifacts
      - "^ADR-[0-9]{4}-[a-z0-9\\-]+\\.(md|yaml)$"

      # epoch declarations
      - "^EPOCH-[0-9]{4}-[a-z0-9\\-]+\\.yaml$"

      # invariant declarations
      - "^I[0-9]{1,4}_[a-z0-9_]+\\.yaml$"

    # ---------------------------------------------------------
    # registry-style governance artifacts
    # ---------------------------------------------------------
    registry_patterns:

      - "^[a-z0-9_]+\\.yaml$"
      - "^[a-z0-9_]+\\.yml$"

    # ---------------------------------------------------------
    # python tooling allowed
    # ---------------------------------------------------------
    allow_python: true

    # ---------------------------------------------------------
    # governance docs allowed
    # ---------------------------------------------------------
    allow_docs: true

    # ---------------------------------------------------------
    # directories always allowed
    # ---------------------------------------------------------
    allow_directories: true

  # =========================================================
  # DOCUMENTATION
  #
  # Documentation is intentionally relaxed.
  # =========================================================
  docs_paths:
    - "**/docs/**"
    - "*.md"

  docs_rules:

    allow_uppercase: true
    allow_spaces: true
    allow_hyphens: true

  # =========================================================
  # OPTIONAL FUTURE EXTENSIONS
  # =========================================================
  future_rules:

    # enforce deterministic registry ordering
    deterministic_registry_sorting: false

    # enforce ontology checksum manifests
    require_manifest_checksums: false

    # enforce semantic naming lineage
    semantic_lineage_validation: false

===== ./afritech/epoch/epoch_path_aliases.yaml =====
schema: afritech.epoch.path_aliases.v2

version: 2

metadata:

  authority: ARCHITECTURE
  status: ACTIVE
  mutability: CONTROLLED

  registry_class: EPOCH_ALIAS_REGISTRY

  description: >
    Canonical epoch path alias registry governing deterministic
    epoch filename normalization, canonical identity mapping,
    replay-safe alias resolution, and filesystem-to-canonical
    transition semantics within AfriTech.

    This registry exists exclusively to:
      - normalize historical epoch filenames
      - preserve replay-safe epoch lineage continuity
      - support deterministic migration semantics
      - prevent ambiguous epoch identity resolution
      - enforce canonical epoch naming doctrine

    Alias mappings are filesystem compatibility artifacts only.

    Constitutional epoch identity derives exclusively from:
      - epoch semantic identity
      - canonical epoch registry lineage
      - deterministic replay admissibility
      - canonical module-path ontology

    Filesystem aliases must never independently define:
      - epoch legitimacy
      - replay authority
      - runtime authority
      - constitutional identity


# ============================================================
# PATH ONTOLOGY ALIGNMENT
# ============================================================

path_alignment:

  canonical_identity_form: module_path

  alias_resolution_form: filesystem_path

  forbidden_identity_forms:

    - extension_identity
    - conceptual_identity
    - relative_identity

  description: >
    Alias mappings are compatibility-layer filesystem
    artifacts only and must never override canonical
    constitutional identity semantics.


# ============================================================
# ALIAS STATUS MODEL
# ============================================================

alias_status_model:

  CANONICAL:

    replay_safe: true

    mutable: false

    redirect_required: false

    description: >
      Canonical epoch filename recognized as the authoritative
      filesystem representation.


  MIGRATING:

    replay_safe: conditional

    mutable: true

    redirect_required: true

    description: >
      Transitional compatibility alias pending deterministic
      normalization toward canonical naming semantics.


  DEPRECATED:

    replay_safe: false

    mutable: false

    redirect_required: true

    description: >
      Historical compatibility alias retained temporarily for
      deterministic replay continuity only.


  FORBIDDEN:

    replay_safe: false

    mutable: false

    redirect_required: false

    description: >
      Constitutionally forbidden alias identity.


# ============================================================
# ALIAS REGISTRY
# ============================================================

aliases:

  # ----------------------------------------------------------
  # LEGACY HYphenated COMPATIBILITY ALIAS
  # ----------------------------------------------------------

  EPOCH-0008.yaml:

    canonical: EPOCH_0008.yaml

    status: MIGRATING

    replay_admissible: true

    redirect_required: true

    migration_target:

      canonical_filename: EPOCH_0008.yaml

      migration_required: true

      deterministic_resolution_required: true

    description: >
      Transitional hyphenated epoch filename retained
      temporarily for replay-safe lineage continuity.


  # ----------------------------------------------------------
  # CANONICAL FILENAMES
  # ----------------------------------------------------------

  EPOCH_0006.yaml:

    status: CANONICAL

    replay_admissible: true

    redirect_required: false

    description: >
      Canonical replay-safe epoch filename.


  EPOCH_0007.yaml:

    status: CANONICAL

    replay_admissible: true

    redirect_required: false

    description: >
      Canonical replay-safe epoch filename.


  EPOCH_0008.yaml:

    status: CANONICAL

    replay_admissible: true

    redirect_required: false

    description: >
      Canonical replay-safe epoch filename.


# ============================================================
# GLOBAL ALIAS RULES
# ============================================================

rules:

  - id: EPOCH_ALIAS_RULE_1

    rule: >
      Canonical epoch filenames must use deterministic
      underscore-separated normalization semantics.


  - id: EPOCH_ALIAS_RULE_2

    rule: >
      Hyphenated epoch filenames are transitional
      compatibility aliases only and must resolve
      deterministically toward canonical identities.


  - id: EPOCH_ALIAS_RULE_3

    rule: >
      Canonical epoch identities must never alias
      themselves directly or indirectly.


  - id: EPOCH_ALIAS_RULE_4

    rule: >
      Alias graphs must remain acyclic and replay-safe.


# ============================================================
# CONSTITUTIONAL ASSERTIONS
# ============================================================

constitutional_assertions:

  - >
    Canonical epoch identities are terminal replay-safe
    identity anchors.

  - >
    Alias mappings may preserve compatibility continuity
    but may never redefine constitutional identity.

  - >
    Replay-safe epoch resolution requires deterministic,
    acyclic alias normalization semantics.

schema: afritech.epoch.registry.v2

version: 2

metadata:

  authority: CONSTITUTION
  status: ACTIVE
  mutability: CONTROLLED

  registry_class: CANONICAL_EPOCH_REGISTRY

  description: >
    Canonical constitutional epoch registry governing
    deterministic temporal evolution, replay-safe epoch
    transitions, lineage continuity, runtime activation,
    reseal semantics, and temporal finality within AfriTech.

    This registry is the authoritative constitutional source
    for:
      - epoch transition legality
      - temporal monotonicity
      - replay-safe epoch evolution
      - active epoch exclusivity
      - seal semantics
      - epoch lifecycle admissibility
      - registry continuity
      - deterministic temporal ordering

    No runtime, replay, governance, proof, CI, or
    enforcement component may reinterpret epoch semantics
    outside deterministic artifacts derived from this registry.


# ============================================================
# PATH ONTOLOGY ALIGNMENT
# ============================================================

path_alignment:

  canonical_identity_form: module_path

  forbidden_identity_forms:

    - filesystem_path
    - extension_identity
    - conceptual_identity
    - relative_identity

  description: >
    Epoch registry identity resolution requires canonical
    module-path ontology alignment.


# ============================================================
# EPOCH REGISTRY
# ============================================================

epoch_registry:

  metadata:

    registry_version: v2

    registry_authority: CONSTITUTION

    replay_admissibility_required: true

    deterministic_ordering: enforced

    description: >
      Canonical registry defining temporal evolution rules,
      replay admissibility, lifecycle constraints, reseal
      semantics, lineage continuity, and deterministic epoch
      progression within AfriTech.


  # ==========================================================
  # CORE RULES
  # ==========================================================

  rules:

    - id: EPOCH_MONOTONIC_VERSION

      rule: >
        epoch.version MUST strictly increase across all
        constitutionally admissible transitions.

      violation_class: B_TEMPORAL


    - id: EPOCH_SEAL_REQUIRED

      rule: >
        Previous epoch MUST be constitutionally sealed before
        any subsequent epoch transition.

      violation_class: B_FINALITY


    - id: EPOCH_INSTANCE_UNIQUE

      rule: >
        epoch.instance_id MUST remain globally unique across
        all epoch transitions.

      violation_class: B_IDENTITY


    - id: EPOCH_ACTIVE_SINGLETON

      rule: >
        Exactly one runtime-active epoch MAY exist at any
        constitutionally admissible moment.

      violation_class: B_RUNTIME


    - id: EPOCH_SEALED_IMMUTABLE

      rule: >
        Constitutionally sealed epochs MUST remain immutable.

      violation_class: B_IMMUTABILITY


    - id: EPOCH_NO_BACKWARD_TIME

      rule: >
        Temporal progression MUST remain monotonic under all
        runtime, replay, governance, and proof conditions.

      violation_class: B_TEMPORAL


    - id: EPOCH_REPLAY_REQUIRED

      rule: >
        All constitutionally admissible epochs MUST remain
        replay-reconstructible.

      violation_class: B_REPLAY


    - id: EPOCH_CANONICAL_IDENTITY

      rule: >
        Epoch identity resolution MUST derive exclusively from
        canonical module-path ontology.

      violation_class: B_IDENTITY


    - id: EPOCH_RESEAL_REQUIRED

      rule: >
        Epoch evolution legitimacy requires deterministic
        reseal validation and replay-safe attestation.

      violation_class: B_ATTESTATION


    - id: EPOCH_CLOSED_WORLD_REQUIRED

      rule: >
        Epoch evolution MUST preserve declared execution
        surfaces and closed-world execution semantics.

      violation_class: B_CLOSED_WORLD


  # ==========================================================
  # CONSTITUTIONAL INVARIANTS
  # ==========================================================

  invariants:

    - I30_EPOCH_MONOTONICITY
    - I30_1_NO_BACKWARD_TIME
    - I30_2_SEAL_BEFORE_TRANSITION
    - I30_3_DETERMINISTIC_EVOLUTION
    - I30_4_GLOBAL_EPOCH_CONSISTENCY
    - I31_REPLAY_ADMISSIBILITY_REQUIRED
    - I32_RESEAL_REQUIRED
    - I33_CLOSED_WORLD_EVOLUTION
    - I34_CANONICAL_IDENTITY_REQUIRED
    - I35_DETERMINISTIC_LINEAGE


  # ==========================================================
  # TRANSITION POLICY
  # ==========================================================

  transition:

    mode: STRICT

    replay_admissibility_required: true

    deterministic_transition_required: true

    constraints:

      require_sealed_previous: true

      require_version_increment: true

      require_instance_change: true

      forbid_parallel_epochs: true

      require_replay_alignment: true

      require_receipt_alignment: true

      require_registry_hash_alignment: true

      require_invariant_validation: true

      require_deterministic_trace_validation: true

      forbid_speculative_transition: true

      forbid_observer_relative_transition: true

    forbidden:

      - probabilistic_transition
      - replay_divergence
      - lineage_rewrite
      - speculative_epoch_activation
      - undeclared_execution_surface_transition


  # ==========================================================
  # EPOCH STATE MODEL
  # ==========================================================

  state:

    constitutional_status:

      ACTIVE:

        immutable: false

        replay_admissible: conditional

        description: >
          Constitutionally active epoch not yet sealed.


      SEALED:

        immutable: true

        replay_admissible: true

        description: >
          Constitutionally finalized immutable epoch.


    runtime_status:

      ACTIVE:

        execution_enabled: true

        description: >
          Runtime-active epoch participating in sovereign
          execution.


      ARCHIVED:

        execution_enabled: false

        description: >
          Historical epoch retained exclusively for replay,
          proof, and lineage continuity.


    active_rules:

      only_one_active_epoch: true

      active_epoch_must_not_be_sealed: true

      active_epoch_must_be_admissible: true

      active_epoch_must_be_replay_safe: true


    sealed_rules:

      sealed_epoch_is_immutable: true

      sealed_epoch_is_not_runtime_mutable: true

      sealed_epoch_is_replay_admissible: true

      sealed_epoch_is_not_active: true


  # ==========================================================
  # DETERMINISM
  # ==========================================================

  determinism:

    ordering: STRICT

    evaluation: DETERMINISTIC

    replay_consistency: ENFORCED

    observer_independence: REQUIRED

    deterministic_requirements:

      - canonical_identity_resolution
      - replay_safe_execution
      - deterministic_mutation_ordering
      - deterministic_transition_ordering
      - invariant_preservation

    forbidden:

      - probabilistic_execution
      - observer_relative_replay
      - dynamic_surface_aliasing
      - uncontrolled_mutation
      - reflection_based_resolution


  # ==========================================================
  # REPLAY ADMISSIBILITY
  # ==========================================================

  replay_admissibility:

    required: true

    replay_requirements:

      - deterministic_execution
      - deterministic_transition
      - canonical_identity_resolution
      - replay_traceability
      - invariant_preservation
      - admissible_execution_surfaces

    replay_invalidators:

      - replay_divergence
      - probabilistic_reconstruction
      - observer_relative_replay
      - speculative_execution
      - undeclared_execution_surfaces

    witness_requirements:

      - receipt_hash
      - replay_hash
      - execution_trace_hash
      - transcript_hash
      - mutation_trace_hash


  # ==========================================================
  # REGISTRY ALIGNMENT
  # ==========================================================

  registry_alignment:

    registry_is_source_of_truth: true

    runtime_must_match_registry: true

    replay_must_match_registry: true

    proof_must_match_registry: true

    required_fields:

      - epoch_id
      - instance_id
      - version
      - constitutional_status
      - runtime_status
      - replay_hash
      - receipt_hash
      - registry_hash

    constraints:

      canonical_identity_required: true

      deterministic_resolution_required: true

      replay_alignment_required: true

      invariant_alignment_required: true

      no_registry_gaps: true

      no_duplicate_epoch_identity: true

      no_filesystem_identity_resolution: true


  # ==========================================================
  # RESEAL LAW
  # ==========================================================

  reseal:

    reseal_required: true

    reseal_requirements:

      - registry_hash_alignment
      - replay_hash_alignment
      - receipt_generation
      - deterministic_trace_validation
      - invariant_validation

    forbidden:

      - reseal_without_attestation
      - reseal_without_replay_alignment
      - reseal_after_terminal_epoch
      - observer_relative_reseal

    guarantees:

      - immutable_lineage
      - deterministic_history
      - replay_safe_epoch_finality


  # ==========================================================
  # SAFETY GUARANTEES
  # ==========================================================

  safety:

    guarantees:

      - deterministic_epoch_ordering
      - replay_safe_lineage
      - immutable_resealed_history
      - canonical_identity_resolution
      - deterministic_transition_validation
      - observer_independent_replay
      - closed_world_epoch_evolution

    forbid:

      - epoch_regression
      - epoch_reuse
      - unsealed_transition
      - multiple_active_epochs
      - hidden_epoch_mutation
      - speculative_epoch_activation
      - filesystem_identity_resolution
      - probabilistic_transition
      - replay_divergence

    enforcement:

      violation_action: FAIL_FAST

      replay_violation_action: REPLAY_INVALID

      lineage_violation_action: REGISTRY_REJECTION

      attestation_violation_action: RESEAL_REJECTION


# ============================================================
# FAILURE EFFECTS
# ============================================================

failure_effects:

  replay_divergence:

    effect:

      - replay_invalid
      - transcript_rejection
      - receipt_non_admissible


  lineage_violation:

    effect:

      - registry_invalid
      - epoch_rejection


  temporal_regression:

    effect:

      - replay_invalid

constitutional_assertion:

  description: >
    AfriTech epoch evolution is constitutionally deterministic,
    replay-safe, monotonic, and lineage-preserving.

    Epoch legitimacy derives exclusively from:
      - deterministic temporal ordering
      - replay admissibility
      - invariant preservation
      - canonical identity resolution
      - admissible execution topology
      - constitutionally valid reseal semantics

    No epoch legitimacy may emerge from:
      - filesystem structure
      - speculative interpretation
      - observer-relative replay
      - runtime activity alone
      - undeclared execution surfaces
      - probabilistic reconstruction

    Epoch evolution must remain:
      - deterministic
      - replay-safe
      - observer-independent
      - constitutionally bounded
      - closed-world aligned

global_law:

  monotonicity:

    required: true

    rule: STRICTLY_INCREASING

    description: >
      Epoch numbers must increase monotonically without
      rollback or reuse.

    violation_class: B_TEMPORAL


  parent_lineage:

    required: true

    root_epoch_parent: null

    description: >
      Every epoch except genesis must reference exactly
      one canonical parent epoch.

    violation_class: B_LINEAGE


  replay_determinism:

    required: true

    rule: CANONICAL_REPLAY_REQUIRED

    description: >
      Epoch state must be deterministically reconstructible
      under replay-safe constitutional conditions.

    violation_class: B_REPLAY


  registry_continuity:

    required: true

    rule: NO_EPOCH_GAPS

    description: >
      Epoch registry lineage must remain continuous,
      deterministic, and gap-free.

    violation_class: B_REGISTRY


  attestation_binding:

    required: true

    rule: RECEIPT_AND_REGISTRY_HASH_MATCH

    description: >
      Epoch legitimacy requires receipt, replay,
      transcript, and registry alignment.

    violation_class: B_ATTESTATION


  temporal_finality:

    resealed_epochs_mutable: false

    description: >
      Resealed epochs become constitutionally immutable.

    violation_class: B_FINALITY


  closed_world_execution:

    required: true

    description: >
      Epoch evolution must preserve declared execution
      surfaces and deterministic execution topology.

    violation_class: B_CLOSED_WORLD


  deterministic_transition:

    required: true

    description: >
      Equivalent constitutional epoch transitions must
      produce replay-equivalent outcomes.

    violation_class: B_DETERMINISM

# ============================================================
# EPOCH TYPES
# ============================================================

epoch_types:

  GENESIS:

    description: >
      Foundational epoch establishing constitutional root,
      trust anchor, replay root, and initial authority.

    permits:

      - constitutional_initialization
      - root_attestation
      - baseline_receipt_generation
      - initial_execution_surface_declaration

    prohibits:

      - parent_reference
      - replay_fork
      - authority_derivation
      - prior_lineage_reference

    reseal_required: true


  EVOLUTION:

    description: >
      Epoch introducing constitutional capability expansion
      while preserving deterministic lineage continuity.

    permits:

      - invariant_extension
      - runtime_surface_expansion
      - proof_extension
      - replay_extension
      - registry_evolution

    prohibits:

      - lineage_rewrite
      - replay_reset
      - authority_escalation
      - historical_mutation

    reseal_required: true


  NORMALIZATION:

    description: >
      Structural normalization epoch without constitutional
      capability expansion.

    permits:

      - internal_refactor
      - artifact_relayout
      - replay_alignment
      - receipt_schema_stabilization
      - ontology_normalization

    prohibits:

      - invariant_addition
      - authority_change
      - execution_surface_change
      - replay_semantic_change

    reseal_required: true


  CORRECTION:

    description: >
      Epoch repairing semantic inconsistency while preserving
      constitutional authority boundaries.

    permits:

      - semantic_repair
      - attestation_fix
      - replay_consistency_repair
      - registry_consistency_repair

    prohibits:

      - capability_addition
      - authority_broadening
      - execution_surface_extension
      - replay_semantic_expansion

    reseal_required: true


  TERMINAL:

    description: >
      Final immutable constitutional epoch.
      No further constitutional evolution permitted.

    permits:

      - proof_discharge
      - terminal_attestation
      - replay_finalization

    prohibits:

      - further_transition
      - mutation
      - reseal_after_final
      - runtime_expansion

    reseal_required: true

===== ./afritech/genesis/genesis_schema.yaml =====
schema: afritech.genesis.v1

genesis:

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # IDENTITY
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  id: "GENESIS-0001"                  # immutable system root identifier
  issued_at: "ISO-8601 timestamp"    # creation time (deterministic or fixed)

  constitutional_version: 1          # version of constitutional model
  initial_epoch: 0                   # MUST be 0 (absolute start)

  authority_seed: "REGISTRY"         # MUST be REGISTRY (anchor rule)

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # ROOT BINDINGS (CORE SYSTEM STATE)
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  registry_origin_hash: sha256         # hash of registry.yaml
  invariant_root_hash: sha256          # hash of INVARIANTS.yaml
  constitutional_surface_hash: sha256  # hash of constitutional surfaces
  execution_surface_hash: sha256       # hash of execution surfaces

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # TRUST ROOT (CRITICAL)
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  trust_anchor: sha256
  # MUST equal:
  # sha256(
  #   registry_origin_hash
  # + invariant_root_hash
  # + constitutional_surface_hash
  # + execution_surface_hash
  # )

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # PROOF OF ORIGIN
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  issuance_proof: "genesis_proof.json"
  # optional but recommended:
  # proof of initial construction / governance approval

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # SIGNATURE (EPOCH ZERO AUTHORITY)
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  epoch_zero_signature:

    algorithm: ED25519

    payload_hash: sha256
    # hash of canonical genesis payload (excluding signature block)

    signature: hex
    public_key: hex

    version: v1

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # OPTIONAL METADATA (STRICTLY NON-AUTHORITATIVE)
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  metadata:

    description: "AfriTech Genesis Root Artifact"
    environment: "production | staging | test"

    created_by: "system | authority"
    notes: "optional human-readable context"

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # INVARIANTS (ENFORCED CONTRACT)
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  invariants:

    - I17_GENESIS_ROOT_AUTHORITY
      # All authority MUST derive from genesis

    - I17_1_IMMUTABILITY
      # Genesis MUST NOT change after issuance

    - I17_2_AUTHORITY_SEED_FIXED
      # authority_seed MUST equal REGISTRY

    - I17_3_INITIAL_EPOCH_ZERO
      # initial_epoch MUST be 0

    - I17_4_HASH_BINDING_COMPLETE
      # All root hashes MUST be present and valid

    - I17_5_TRUST_ANCHOR_CORRECT
      # trust_anchor MUST equal computed root hash

    - I17_6_SIGNATURE_VALID
      # signature MUST verify payload_hash

    - I17_7_PAYLOAD_HASH_CORRECT
      # payload_hash MUST match canonical genesis payload

    - I17_8_REPLAY_STABLE
      # canonical serialization MUST be deterministic

    - I17_9_NO_EXTERNAL_STATE
      # genesis must fully define authority without external inputs

    - I17_10_SINGLE_ORIGIN
      # only one genesis allowed per system identity

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # VALIDATION CONTRACT
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  validation:

    required_at_boot: true
    required_for_runtime_admission: true
    required_for_epoch_validation: true

    enforce_signature: true
    enforce_trust_anchor: true
    enforce_hash_consistency: true

    failure_response:

      type: HARD_FAILURE
      effect: SYSTEM_NON_EXISTENCE
      description: "Genesis validation failure results in system non-existence"

    - REPLAY_VERIFIER_SPEC
    - RUNTIME_ADMISSION_LAYER
    - RUNTIME_CERTIFICATE
