===== ./afritech/governance/adr/ADR-0001.yaml =====
schema: afritech.governance.adr.v1

adr:
  id: ADR-0001
  title: Genesis Trust Root Establishment
  status: APPROVED
  type: ARCHITECTURAL

  epoch: 0

  date: "2026-01-01"

  context: >
    AfriTech requires a deterministic and verifiable trust root to anchor all
    subsequent constitutional execution, registry sealing, epoch transitions,
    and replay validation. Without a canonical genesis decision, all downstream
    governance artifacts lack a stable origin reference.

  decision: >
    Establish a single immutable Genesis Trust Root that defines:
    1. The initial authority baseline for all system execution
    2. The cryptographic and structural origin of registry sealing
    3. The canonical starting epoch (epoch-0)
    4. The deterministic replay anchor for all future state transitions

    This trust root is considered non-revisable once sealed and must be
    referenced by all epochs, guards, and governance bindings.

  consequences:
    positive:
      - Provides a deterministic origin for all system state
      - Enables reproducible replay validation
      - Establishes trust anchor for registry sealing
      - Unifies epoch and governance lineage under a single root

    negative:
      - Introduces hard dependency on genesis correctness
      - Any error in genesis requires full system reseal
      - Reduces flexibility for retroactive structural changes

  invariants:
    - genesis_trust_root_is_immutable
    - all_epochs_must_reference_ADR_0001
    - registry_seal_derives_from_genesis
    - replay_fails_if_genesis_missing_or_modified

  links:
    epochs:
      - EPOCH_0000
    dependencies: []
    required_by:
      - ADR-0002
      - ADR-0003
      - ADR-0004
      - ADR-0005
      - ADR-0006
      - ADR-0007
      - ADR-0008
      - ADR-0009

===== ./afritech/governance/adr/ADR-0002.yaml =====
schema: afritech.governance.adr.v1

adr:
  id: ADR-0002
  title: Epoch Governance and Temporal Authority Model
  status: APPROVED
  type: ARCHITECTURAL

  epoch: 1

  approved_at: "2026-01-02T00:00:00Z"

  context: >
    AfriTech requires a deterministic model for time-aware execution. Without
    a formal epoch system, governance decisions, state transitions, and replay
    validation cannot be consistently ordered or validated against a canonical
    temporal structure.

    Existing system components (state machine, guards, registry sealing)
    depend on a consistent definition of "valid time window for execution".

  decision: >
    Introduce a formal Epoch Governance Model that defines:

    1. Epochs as immutable temporal execution segments
    2. Each epoch as a bounded container for state transitions and governance rules
    3. Epoch transitions as deterministic, validator-approved operations
    4. A strict requirement that all system actions must occur within a valid epoch
    5. A single active epoch pointer enforced by epoch_manager

    Epochs are sequential, non-overlapping, and strictly ordered. Once closed,
    an epoch becomes read-only and replay-anchored.

  structure:
    epoch:
      id: string
      start_timestamp: int
      end_timestamp: int_or_null
      status: [ACTIVE, CLOSED, INVALIDATED]
      parent_epoch: string_or_null
      allowed_transitions: list[string]
      governance_snapshot_hash: string

  invariants:
    - single_active_epoch_enforced
    - closed_epochs_are_immutable
    - all_transitions_require_valid_epoch
    - epoch_lineage_must_be_acyclic
    - epoch_closure_produces_hash_snapshot
    - replay_reconstructs_epoch_order_exactly

  dependencies:
    - ADR-0001

  required_by:
    - ADR-0003
    - ADR-0004
    - ADR-0005
    - ADR-0006
    - ADR-0007
    - ADR-0008
    - ADR-0009

  consequences:
    positive:
      - Enables deterministic temporal replay of system state
      - Prevents cross-time state corruption
      - Provides clear boundaries for governance decisions
      - Strengthens auditability of all system actions

    negative:
      - Adds strict coupling between execution and time model
      - Requires careful epoch lifecycle management
      - Failures in epoch transitions can halt system execution

  implementation_notes: >
    Epoch enforcement is delegated to:
      - afritech.epoch.epoch_manager
      - afritech.epoch.epoch_validator
      - afritech.epoch.epoch_transition

    Guards MUST reject any operation outside ACTIVE epoch scope.

    Replay engine MUST reconstruct system state by:
      1. Loading epoch chain
      2. Validating epoch hashes
      3. Replaying transitions in strict epoch order

  links:
    epochs:
      - EPOCH_0001


===== ./afritech/governance/adr/ADR-0003.yaml =====
schema: afritech.governance.adr.v1

adr:
  id: ADR-0003
  title: Deterministic State Transition and Execution Contract
  status: APPROVED
  type: ARCHITECTURAL

  epoch: 1

  approved_at: "2026-01-03T00:00:00Z"

  context: >
    AfriTech operates a stateful execution system where all mutations must be
    reproducible, verifiable, and replayable. While ADR-0002 defines epoch
    boundaries for time governance, there is no formal contract defining how
    state transitions occur within those epochs.

    Without a deterministic transition model, replay validation and registry
    sealing cannot guarantee identical reconstruction of system state.

  decision: >
    Define a Deterministic State Transition Contract that governs all system
    state changes within an active epoch.

    This contract enforces:

    1. All state transitions are pure functions of (state, event, epoch)
    2. No hidden side effects are permitted during transitions
    3. Every transition must produce a verifiable state hash
    4. Transitions must be validated before execution by state_validator
    5. Transition outputs must be identical across replay executions
    6. Invalid transitions MUST be rejected before state mutation

    The state machine is the only permitted mechanism for mutating system state.

  model:
    inputs:
      - current_state
      - event
      - epoch_context
    output:
      - new_state
      - state_hash
      - transition_proof

  invariants:
    - state_transitions_are_deterministic
    - state_mutation_restricted_to_state_engine
    - transitions_must_be_epoch_bound
    - transition_outputs_are_cryptographically_verifiable
    - replay_produces_identical_state_hashes

  validation_pipeline:
    - state_validator
    - epoch_validator
    - guard_engine
    - registry_seal_check

  dependencies:
    - ADR-0001
    - ADR-0002

  required_by:
    - ADR-0004
    - ADR-0005
    - ADR-0006
    - ADR-0007
    - ADR-0008
    - ADR-0009

  implementation_notes: >
    The deterministic execution model is implemented in:
      - afritech.state_machine.state_engine
      - afritech.state_machine.state_validator
      - afritech.state_machine.state_transition_proof

    All transitions MUST be replayable using the same input sequence and epoch
    context. Any divergence in state hash MUST result in replay failure.

    Guards MAY block transitions before execution but MUST NOT alter outputs.

  consequences:
    positive:
      - Guarantees full replay determinism of system state
      - Strengthens audit and verification capabilities
      - Prevents hidden side-effect execution paths
      - Enables cryptographic traceability of all mutations

    negative:
      - Strict limitation on runtime flexibility
      - Requires full validation overhead per transition
      - Failure in validator pipeline halts state progression

  links:
    epochs:
      - EPOCH_0001
    genesis:
      - ADR-0001

===== ./afritech/governance/adr/ADR-0004.yaml =====
schema: afritech.governance.adr.v1

adr:
  id: ADR-0004
  title: Guard Enforcement and Runtime Protection Model
  status: APPROVED
  type: ARCHITECTURAL

  epoch: 4

  approved_at: "2026-01-04T00:00:00Z"

  context: >
    AfriTech now has deterministic identity (ADR-0001), temporal governance
    (ADR-0002), and state transition determinism (ADR-0003). However, there is
    no formal enforcement layer that controls whether a transition or operation
    is allowed to execute at runtime.

    Without enforcement, deterministic systems can still execute invalid actions
    if not properly constrained at runtime.

  decision: >
    Introduce a Guard Enforcement Model as the mandatory runtime protection layer.

    Guards act as pre- and post-execution validators that enforce constitutional
    correctness before any state mutation or epoch transition is committed.

    The system MUST enforce:

    1. All operations pass through guard_engine before execution
    2. Guards may block, quarantine, or escalate violations
    3. Guards MUST NOT mutate state directly
    4. Guards operate under epoch constraints (ADR-0002)
    5. Guards enforce state rules (ADR-0003)
    6. Guards are deterministic and replayable

  guard_types:
    invariant_guard:
      purpose: Enforces system invariants must never be violated

    authority_guard:
      purpose: Ensures only authorized execution surfaces are permitted

    epoch_guard:
      purpose: Ensures execution occurs within valid epoch boundaries

    rollback_engine:
      purpose: Restores last valid state on violation detection

    quarantine_manager:
      purpose: Isolates invalid or suspicious execution flows

    escalation_handler:
      purpose: Routes critical violations to higher governance layers

    halt_controller:
      purpose: Performs deterministic system halt on fatal violations

  invariants:
    - all_execution_passes_guard_engine
    - guards_are_deterministic_and_replay_consistent
    - guards_do_not_modify_state_directly
    - invariant_violation_triggers_halt_or_quarantine
    - guard_decisions_must_be_traceable

  execution_flow:
    - input_event
    - epoch_validation
    - guard_engine_check
    - state_transition
    - state_commit
    - trace_recording

  dependencies:
    - ADR-0001
    - ADR-0002
    - ADR-0003

  required_by:
    - ADR-0005
    - ADR-0006
    - ADR-0007
    - ADR-0008
    - ADR-0009

  implementation_notes: >
    Guard enforcement is implemented in:
      - afritech.guards.guard_engine
      - afritech.guards.guard_validator
      - afritech.guards.guard_runtime
      - afritech.guards.invariant_guard
      - afritech.guards.authority_guard
      - afritech.guards.epoch_guard

    All runtime execution MUST pass through guard_engine before state_engine
    is invoked.

    Fail-fast behavior is mandatory: any guard rejection aborts execution.

  consequences:
    positive:
      - Prevents invalid or unauthorized state mutations
      - Adds formal runtime safety layer
      - Enables deterministic violation detection and replay analysis
      - Strengthens system trust boundaries

    negative:
      - Adds runtime overhead for every execution
      - Improves safety at the cost of latency
      - Requires strict determinism in guard logic

  links:
    dependencies:
      - ADR-0001
      - ADR-0002
      - ADR-0003

    epochs:
      - EPOCH_0004

===== ./afritech/governance/adr/ADR-0005.yaml =====
schema: afritech.governance.adr.v1

adr:
  id: ADR-0005
  title: Registry Seal Lifecycle and Authority Finalization Model
  status: APPROVED
  type: ARCHITECTURAL

  epoch: 5

  approved_at: "2026-01-05T00:00:00Z"

  context: >
    AfriTech now has:
    - A trust root (ADR-0001)
    - Temporal governance via epochs (ADR-0002)
    - Deterministic state transitions (ADR-0003)
    - Runtime enforcement via guards (ADR-0004)

    However, there is no formal model defining how system-wide truth is
    finalized, sealed, and made immutable for replay verification.

    Without a registry sealing mechanism, system state remains mutable from a
    governance perspective, breaking auditability guarantees.

  decision: >
    Introduce a Registry Seal Lifecycle Model that defines how system state,
    governance decisions, and execution history are finalized into an immutable
    canonical registry.

    The registry seal acts as the authoritative snapshot of system truth at a
    given epoch boundary.

    The system MUST enforce:

    1. Registry state is sealed per epoch boundary
    2. A sealed registry is immutable and replay-verifiable
    3. Any mutation requires a new seal cycle
    4. Seal operations must be cryptographically hash-chained
    5. Registry seals MUST reference:
       - genesis trust root (ADR-0001)
       - epoch state (ADR-0002)
       - state hashes (ADR-0003)
       - guard outcomes (ADR-0004)
    6. Seal validation MUST occur before replay acceptance

  registry_model:
    components:
      registry_state:
        description: Current mutable system snapshot before sealing

      registry_seal:
        description: Immutable cryptographic snapshot of system state

      seal_hash:
        description: Deterministic hash of full system state at epoch closure

      attestation:
        description: Proof of validity of sealed state

  lifecycle:
    - collect_state
    - validate_guards
    - validate_epoch
    - compute_state_hashes
    - generate_seal_hash
    - persist_registry_seal
    - lock_registry_state

  invariants:
    - sealed_registry_is_immutable
    - single_registry_seal_per_epoch
    - replay_rejects_unsealed_states
    - registry_hash_chain_is_continuous
    - seal_validation_requires_all_dependencies

  dependencies:
    - ADR-0001
    - ADR-0002
    - ADR-0003
    - ADR-0004

  required_by:
    - ADR-0006
    - ADR-0007
    - ADR-0008
    - ADR-0009

  implementation_notes: >
    Registry sealing is implemented in:
      - afritech.registry.seal
      - afritech.registry.history
      - afritech.verify.replay

    The seal process MUST:
      1. Freeze epoch state
      2. Validate guard outcomes
      3. Compute deterministic hash chain
      4. Persist immutable snapshot

    Any failure in sealing MUST invalidate the epoch for replay purposes.

  consequences:
    positive:
      - Enables fully immutable system snapshots per epoch
      - Provides cryptographic auditability
      - Strengthens replay determinism guarantees
      - Anchors all governance and execution layers into verifiable history

    negative:
      - Adds overhead at epoch boundaries
      - Requires strict coordination between state, guards, and epoch systems
      - Seal failure blocks epoch finalization

  links:
    dependencies:
      - ADR-0001
      - ADR-0002
      - ADR-0003
      - ADR-0004

    epochs:
      - EPOCH_0005

===== ./afritech/governance/adr/ADR-0006.yaml =====
schema: afritech.governance.adr.v1

adr:
  id: ADR-0006
  title: Runtime Surface Refinement and Introduction of Proof Layer
  status: APPROVED
  type: CONSTITUTIONAL_SURFACE_REFINEMENT

  epoch: 6

  approved_at: "2026-05-07T00:00:00Z"

  context: >
    The AfriTech system required a refinement of the runtime layer
    to improve separation of concerns between activation control
    and execution logic. Additionally, the system lacked a formalized
    proof surface for verifiable execution outcomes.

    Prior to this change, runtime execution and activation control
    were tightly coupled, limiting clarity, traceability, and
    enforceability of execution boundaries.

  decision: >
    The runtime layer is split into two explicit sub-surfaces:
      - runtime.activation
      - runtime.engine

    The runtime.activation surface is responsible for:
      - admission control
      - authority validation
      - execution readiness

    The runtime.engine surface is responsible for:
      - deterministic execution
      - state transition orchestration
      - integration with the state machine

    A new proof surface is introduced to capture execution proof
    artifacts, and an evaluation surface is introduced to support
    validation, scoring, and verification of execution outcomes.

    These surfaces MUST be:
      - deterministic
      - replay-verifiable
      - registry-attested

  implementation:
    surfaces_added:
      - proof
      - evaluation

    surfaces_refined:
      - runtime.activation
      - runtime.engine

    breaking_changes: false

  invariants:
    - runtime_surface_is_partitioned
    - runtime_activation_controls_admission
    - runtime_engine_executes_deterministically
    - proof_artifacts_are_deterministic
    - evaluation_surface_does_not_modify_state
    - all_surfaces_must_be_registry_attested
    - all_surfaces_must_be_replay_verifiable

  validation:
    replay_required: true
    guard_coverage_required: true
    registry_reseal_required: true

  dependencies:
    - ADR-0001
    - ADR-0002
    - ADR-0003
    - ADR-0004
    - ADR-0005

  required_by:
    - ADR-0007
    - ADR-0008
    - ADR-0009

  implementation_notes: >
    Runtime refinement is implemented across:
      - afritech.runtime.activation
      - afritech.runtime.engine

    Proof and evaluation surfaces are implemented in:
      - afritech.proof
      - afritech.evaluation

    The system MUST enforce:
      1. runtime.activation executes before runtime.engine
      2. all execution passes guard validation before engine execution
      3. proof artifacts are generated after execution
      4. evaluation does not alter system state

    Replay validation MUST:
      - include proof artifacts
      - validate execution consistency
      - ensure evaluation output does not affect deterministic state

  consequences:
    positive:
      - Improves separation of runtime responsibilities
      - Enables deterministic and auditable execution flow
      - Introduces formal execution proof generation
      - Enables post-execution validation and scoring
      - Strengthens replay verification fidelity

    negative:
      - Increases architectural complexity
      - Requires updates to registry attestation surfaces
      - Requires replay system awareness of new layers
      - Introduces additional validation overhead

  links:
    epochs:
      - EPOCH_0006

    surfaces:
      - runtime.activation
      - runtime.engine
      - proof
      - evaluation

  traceability:
    related_files:
      - afritech/runtime/activation.py
      - afritech/runtime/engine.py
      - afritech/proof/
      - afritech/evaluation/
      - afritech/guards/

  integrity:
    immutable: true
    replay_protected: true
    registry_included: true

===== ./afritech/governance/adr/ADR-0007.yaml =====
schema: afritech.governance.adr.v1

adr:
  id: ADR-0007
  title: Integration of Proof and Evaluation into Execution Lifecycle
  status: APPROVED
  type: CONSTITUTIONAL_EXECUTION_INTEGRATION

  epoch: 6

  approved_at: "2026-05-07T00:00:00Z"

  context: >
    Following the introduction of proof and evaluation surfaces
    in ADR-0006, the AfriTech system required formal integration
    of these surfaces into the execution lifecycle to ensure that
    every state transition produces verifiable artifacts and can
    be deterministically evaluated.

    Prior to this ADR, execution produced results without a unified
    guarantee of proof generation and evaluation consistency.

  decision: >
    The execution lifecycle is extended to mandate the generation
    of proof artifacts and evaluation outputs for every transition.

    Execution flow is defined as:

      state → transition → result → proof → evaluation

    This ensures:
      - every execution is provable
      - every result is evaluable
      - replay can verify correctness end-to-end

    Proof generation and evaluation are REQUIRED stages of execution,
    not optional extensions.

  implementation:
    execution_pipeline_extended: true

    lifecycle:
      - state
      - transition
      - result
      - proof
      - evaluation

    surfaces_affected:
      - runtime.engine
      - proof
      - evaluation

    breaking_changes: false

  invariants:
    - proof_generation_is_mandatory
    - evaluation_is_mandatory
    - execution_pipeline_is_fully_deterministic
    - proof_outputs_are_replay_verifiable
    - evaluation_outputs_do_not_modify_state
    - every_transition_produces_proof_and_evaluation

  validation:
    replay_required: true
    proof_required: true
    evaluation_required: true
    guard_coverage_required: true
    registry_reseal_required: true

  dependencies:
    - ADR-0001
    - ADR-0002
    - ADR-0003
    - ADR-0004
    - ADR-0005
    - ADR-0006

  required_by:
    - ADR-0008
    - ADR-0009

  implementation_notes: >
    The extended execution lifecycle is implemented across:
      - afritech.runtime.engine
      - afritech.proof
      - afritech.evaluation

    The system MUST enforce:
      1. Proof artifacts are generated immediately after execution
      2. Evaluation follows proof generation
      3. Neither proof nor evaluation may alter system state
      4. Guard enforcement applies before execution
      5. Replay MUST validate proof and evaluation deterministically

    Any execution missing proof or evaluation MUST be rejected.

  consequences:
    positive:
      - Guarantees proof generation for all executions
      - Enables deterministic verification during replay
      - Introduces measurable evaluation layer
      - Strengthens audit and traceability capabilities
      - Ensures execution lifecycle completeness

    negative:
      - Introduces additional processing overhead
      - Requires strict schema enforcement for proof and evaluation
      - Increases coupling between runtime and validation layers

  links:
    epochs:
      - EPOCH_0006

    surfaces:
      - runtime.engine
      - proof
      - evaluation

    related_adrs:
      - ADR-0006

  traceability:
    related_files:
      - afritech/runtime/engine.py
      - afritech/proof/
      - afritech/evaluation/
      - afritech/guards/invariant_guard.py
      - afritech/guards/schema.py

  integrity:
    immutable: true
    replay_protected: true
    registry_included: true

===== ./afritech/governance/adr/ADR-0008.yaml =====
schema: afritech.governance.adr.v1

adr:
  id: ADR-0008
  title: Introduction of Admission Control and Execution Orchestration Layer
  status: APPROVED
  type: CONSTITUTIONAL_EXECUTION_CONTROL

  epoch: 6

  approved_at: "2026-05-07T00:00:00Z"

  context: >
    Following the integration of proof and evaluation into the execution
    lifecycle (ADR-0007), the system requires a mechanism to control
    which operations are allowed to execute and how they are scheduled.

    Without admission control and orchestration, the system risks:
      - unauthorized execution
      - inconsistent evaluation ordering
      - violation of guard enforcement sequencing

  decision: >
    Introduce a formal admission and orchestration layer responsible for:

      - validating execution requests before runtime execution
      - enforcing deterministic guard sequencing
      - coordinating execution flow across all subsystems

    The execution lifecycle is updated to:

      admission → orchestration → state → transition → result → proof → evaluation

    Admission and orchestration are REQUIRED stages of execution and
    MUST enforce deterministic and replay-consistent control of execution.

  implementation:
    new_layers:
      - runtime.admission
      - runtime.orchestration

    execution_pipeline_updated: true

    lifecycle:
      - admission
      - orchestration
      - state
      - transition
      - result
      - proof
      - evaluation

    surfaces_affected:
      - runtime.activation
      - runtime.engine
      - runtime.admission
      - runtime.orchestration
      - guards
      - schema_validation

    breaking_changes: false

  invariants:
    - admission_is_mandatory_before_execution
    - orchestration_controls_execution_order
    - execution_pipeline_is_deterministic_and_replayable
    - guard_sequencing_is_enforced
    - unauthorized_execution_is_rejected
    - orchestration_does_not_modify_state
    - admission_and_orchestration_are_replay_verifiable

  validation:
    replay_required: true
    admission_required: true
    orchestration_required: true
    guard_execution_order_enforced: true
    registry_reseal_required: true

  dependencies:
    - ADR-0001
    - ADR-0002
    - ADR-0003
    - ADR-0004
    - ADR-0005
    - ADR-0006
    - ADR-0007

  required_by:
    - ADR-0009

  implementation_notes: >
    Admission and orchestration layers are implemented in:
      - afritech.runtime.admission
      - afritech.runtime.orchestration

    The system MUST enforce:
      1. All execution requests pass admission validation
      2. Orchestration defines deterministic execution ordering
      3. Guard checks occur before state transition
      4. Execution continues only if admission and guards succeed
      5. Orchestration MUST NOT alter system state

    Replay MUST:
      - reconstruct admission decisions
      - reconstruct orchestration ordering
      - verify identical execution sequencing

  consequences:
    positive:
      - Prevents unauthorized or invalid execution
      - Ensures deterministic ordering of operations
      - Centralizes execution control
      - Strengthens enforcement of guard system
      - Improves replay fidelity

    negative:
      - Adds additional layer to execution pipeline
      - Requires strict integration with guard and state systems
      - Introduces orchestration overhead

  links:
    epochs:
      - EPOCH_0006

    surfaces:
      - runtime.admission
      - runtime.orchestration
      - runtime.engine
      - proof
      - evaluation

    related_adrs:
      - ADR-0006
      - ADR-0007

  traceability:
    related_files:
      - afritech/runtime/admission/
      - afritech/runtime/orchestration/
      - afritech/guards/
      - afritech/state/
      - afritech/proof/
      - afritech/evaluation/

  integrity:
    immutable: true
    replay_protected: true
    registry_included: true

===== ./afritech/governance/adr/ADR-0009.yaml =====
schema: afritech.governance.adr.v1

adr:
  id: ADR-0009
  title: Replay Validity and Temporal Sovereignty Enforcement
  status: APPROVED
  type: CONSTITUTIONAL_VALIDITY_GUARANTEE

  epoch: 6

  approved_at: "2026-05-07T00:00:00Z"

  context: >
    Following the introduction of runtime refinement (ADR-0006),
    proof and evaluation enforcement (ADR-0007), and admission and
    orchestration control (ADR-0008), the system required a final
    guarantee that every execution and evolution step is reproducible,
    verifiable, and temporally consistent.

    Without a formal replay validity constraint, the system could:
      - diverge between runtime and registry
      - allow non-reproducible states
      - permit invalid temporal evolution

  decision: >
    A constitutional requirement is established:

      "All system states and epochs MUST be replayable from history."

    The system MUST enforce:

      - replay must reconstruct the full execution history
      - replay must reach the current registry epoch
      - runtime state MUST match replay result
      - epoch history is the single source of temporal truth
      - no declared epoch is valid unless fully reconstructible

    The execution and evolution model is finalized as:

      admission → orchestration → state → transition → result
      → proof → evaluation → epoch → replay_verification

    Replay validation is the final authority gate for system truth.

  implementation:
    enforcement_layers:
      - replay_verification
      - epoch_sync_guard
      - epoch_validator
      - invariant_guard

    runtime_requirements:
      replay_must_succeed: true
      terminal_epoch_must_match_registry: true
      history_chain_must_be_complete: true

    breaking_changes: false

  invariants:
    - replay_is_required_for_validity
    - runtime_state_must_match_replay
    - history_is_single_source_of_truth
    - no_unreplayable_state_is_allowed
    - epoch_lineage_must_be_complete
    - registry_and_runtime_must_be_consistent

  validation:
    replay_required: true
    epoch_consistency_required: true
    registry_history_alignment_required: true
    proof_chain_verification_required: true
    guard_enforcement_required: true

  dependencies:
    - ADR-0001
    - ADR-0002
    - ADR-0003
    - ADR-0004
    - ADR-0005
    - ADR-0006
    - ADR-0007
    - ADR-0008

  implementation_notes: >
    Replay validation is implemented in:
      - afritech.verify.replay
      - afritech.epoch.epoch_manager
      - afritech.epoch.epoch_transition
      - afritech.epoch.epoch_validator
      - afritech.guards.epoch_sync_guard
      - afritech.guards.invariant_guard

    The system MUST enforce:
      1. Full reconstruction of execution history
      2. Validation of epoch chain integrity
      3. Validation of proof and evaluation outputs
      4. Alignment between runtime and replay-derived state
      5. Rejection of any inconsistent or incomplete history

    Any failure in replay MUST invalidate system state.

  consequences:
    positive:
      - Guarantees full system reproducibility
      - Prevents hidden or unverifiable state transitions
      - Enforces strict alignment between runtime and registry
      - Establishes deterministic temporal consistency
      - Enables complete auditability
      - Finalizes computational authority model

    negative:
      - Requires strict maintenance of history chain
      - Rejects any incomplete or inconsistent evolution
      - Introduces hard failure on temporal divergence
      - Increases validation overhead for replay enforcement

  links:
    epochs:
      - EPOCH_0006

    surfaces:
      - runtime.admission
      - runtime.orchestration
      - runtime.engine
      - proof
      - evaluation
      - replay_verification

    related_adrs:
      - ADR-0006
      - ADR-0007
      - ADR-0008

  traceability:
    related_files:
      - afritech/verify/replay.py
      - afritech/guards/epoch_sync_guard.py
      - afritech/epoch/epoch_manager.py
      - afritech/epoch/epoch_transition.py
      - afritech/registry/history/
      - afritech/proof/

  integrity:
    immutable: true
    replay_protected: true
    registry_included: true

===== ./afritech/governance/adr/ADR-0010-afriride-v0-2.yaml =====
# afritech/governance/adr/ADR-000X-afriride-v0-2.yaml

schema: afritech.governance.adr.v1

adr:
  id: ADR-0010
  title: AfriRide v0.2 Proof-of-Continuity Expansion
  status: PROPOSED
  type: CONSTITUTIONAL_EVOLUTION
  proposed_epoch: 7
  date: 2026-05-13

  authors:
    - AfriTech Governance

  related_artifacts:
    - ecosystems/afriride/v0_2/
    - ecosystems/afriride/AFRIRIDE_V0_FREEZE.md

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ CONTEXT
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  context: >
    AfriRide v0.1 established deterministic, replay-verifiable
    coordination under a single controlled failure scenario.
    That version was constitutionally frozen under Epoch 6
    as immutable Proof-of-Continuity evidence.

    AfriRide v0.2 extends this proof to a bounded and explicitly
    declared failure space, demonstrating that deterministic,
    authority-governed coordination remains replay-sound across
    multiple failure modes without mutating or weakening v0.1.

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ DECISION
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  decision: >
    Introduce AfriRide v0.2 as a new Proof-of-Continuity surface
    that expands the validated failure space while preserving
    all AfriRide v0.1 guarantees.

    AfriRide v0.2 is introduced as an additive, layered system
    operating under a new determinism envelope and execution
    runtime, without modification of the frozen constitutional
    core.

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ SCOPE
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  scope:

    added:
      - DRIVER_DROPOUT deterministic failure scenario
      - DRIVER_REJECTION_CHAIN deterministic failure scenario
      - TIMEOUT_EXCEEDED deterministic failure scenario
      - v0.2 deterministic failure taxonomy
      - v0.2 determinism envelope
      - multi-scenario continuity metrics:
          - Continuity Coverage (CC)
          - Deterministic Refusal Rate (DRR)
      - v0.2 execution handlers and runtime wrapper

    preserved:
      - AfriRide v0.1 (constitutionally frozen)
      - v0.1 determinism guarantees
      - v0.1 replay identity guarantees
      - v0.1 authority model and execution law

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ INVARIANTS
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  invariants:
    - v0.1 artifacts MUST NOT be modified
    - v0.2 execution MUST be layered externally
    - replay hash identity is mandatory
    - deterministic refusal is required on exhaustion or timeout
    - all failures MUST be declared in the failure taxonomy
    - no nondeterministic behavior is permitted
    - determinism envelope violations invalidate proof

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ EVIDENCE
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  evidence:
    executable:
      - ecosystems/afriride/v0_2/run_multi_scenario_demo.py

    scenarios:
      - ecosystems/afriride/v0_2/scenarios/driver_dropout.yaml
      - ecosystems/afriride/v0_2/scenarios/rejection_chain.yaml
      - ecosystems/afriride/v0_2/scenarios/timeout.yaml

    metrics:
      - Decision Determinism Rate (DDR): 1.0 (all scenarios)
      - Continuity Coverage (CC): 1.0
      - Deterministic Refusal Rate (DRR): 1.0

    replay:
      - identical execution and replay hashes verified
      - replay verifier status: VALID

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ CONSEQUENCES
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  consequences:

    positive:
      - expands AfriRide continuity proof to multiple failure modes
      - strengthens AfriTech institutional credibility
      - demonstrates scalable governance without historical mutation
      - preserves replay-verifiable lineage across epochs

    negative:
      - requires new constitutional epoch (Epoch 7)
      - increases governance surface area
      - introduces additional audit responsibilities

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ STATUS & NEXT STEPS
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  status_notes:
    - This ADR authorizes advancement to Epoch 7
    - AfriRide v0.2 may be frozen after ratification
    - No product, optimization, or performance claims are authorized

  approval_requirements:
    - governance review
    - replay verifier confirmation
    - epoch registry update


===== ./afritech/governance/adr/ADR-0011-afriride-deterministic-retry.yaml =====
schema: afritech.governance.adr.v1

adr:
  id: ADR-0011

  title: AfriRide Deterministic Retry Observation Formalization

  status: PROPOSED

  type: CONSTITUTIONAL_EVOLUTION

  proposed_epoch: 7

  date: 2026-05-14

  authors:
    - AfriTech Governance

  related_artifacts:
    - ecosystems/afriride/tests/test_retry_idempotence.py
    - ecosystems/afriride/tests/test_observational_replay.py
    - ecosystems/afriride/runtime/replay.py
    - ecosystems/afriride/runtime/deterministic_executor.py

  supersedes: []

  depends_on:
    - ADR-0001
    - ADR-0002
    - ADR-0003
    - ADR-0004
    - ADR-0005
    - ADR-0006
    - ADR-0007
    - ADR-0008
    - ADR-0009

# =====================================================
# CONTEXT
# =====================================================

  context: >

    AfriRide Phase 1 established a deterministic execution model
    where identical RuntimeContext produces identical ExecutionResult,
    including replay-stable execution traces and deterministic
    result hashes.

    During Phase 2 observational analysis, an empirical runtime
    behavior was consistently observed:

      - re-submission of an identical intent (retry)
        deterministically results in refusal

    Replay verification confirmed that:

      - refusal behavior is deterministic
      - replay traces remain stable
      - refusal hashes remain reproducible
      - no hidden mutation occurs
      - no semantic interpretation is required

    This behavior already exists within the lawful runtime
    execution surface and does not require additional runtime
    capability.

    However, the behavior is not presently declared within
    AfriRide’s formal failure taxonomy.

    This creates a constitutional ambiguity between:

      - empirically observed deterministic runtime behavior
      - formally declared proof-valid failure semantics

    The absence of explicit declaration risks:

      - replay interpretation inconsistency
      - undocumented observational refusal semantics
      - incomplete proof-of-continuity classification

# =====================================================
# PROBLEM STATEMENT
# =====================================================

  problem_statement: >

    AfriRide currently lacks a formally declared classification
    for deterministic refusal behavior arising from identical
    retry observation.

    Although runtime and replay behavior remain deterministic,
    the failure taxonomy does not explicitly acknowledge this
    observational refusal category.

    Without formal declaration:

      - replay auditors may treat refusal as undefined behavior
      - proof surfaces remain semantically incomplete
      - deterministic observational outcomes remain undocumented

# =====================================================
# DECISION
# =====================================================

  decision: >

    Formally recognize deterministic refusal under duplicate
    intent replay as part of AfriRide’s declared constitutional
    failure surface.

    This ADR does NOT:

      - introduce new runtime logic
      - modify deterministic executor behavior
      - define intent equivalence
      - introduce retry normalization
      - implement semantic deduplication
      - alter replay admissibility rules
      - expand execution surfaces
      - modify orchestration semantics
      - change Phase 1 determinism guarantees

    This ADR ONLY:

      - elevates observed deterministic behavior into
        declared constitutional taxonomy

      - aligns replay-confirmed empirical evidence with
        AfriRide’s proof-of-continuity surface

      - formalizes observational refusal as a lawful
        deterministic outcome

# =====================================================
# CLASSIFICATION
# =====================================================

  classification:

    mutation_type: DECLARATIVE_ALIGNMENT

    constitutional_scope: FAILURE_TAXONOMY_ALIGNMENT

    runtime_effect: NONE

    determinism_effect: NONE

    replay_effect: NONE

    semantic_effect: NONE

    authority_effect: NONE

    execution_surface_effect: NONE

    mutation_visibility: EXPLICIT

# =====================================================
# OBSERVATIONAL BASIS
# =====================================================

  observational_basis:

    evidence_type: EMPIRICAL_RUNTIME_OBSERVATION

    validation_pipeline:
      - deterministic_execution_verification
      - replay_consistency_verification
      - transcript_hash_validation
      - refusal_stability_confirmation

    observed_properties:
      deterministic: true
      replay_stable: true
      hash_stable: true
      observer_independent: true
      non_mutating: true

# =====================================================
# INVARIANTS (PRESERVED)
# =====================================================

  invariants_preserved:

    - I3_NO_SILENT_MUTATION
    - I4_DETERMINISTIC_EXECUTION
    - I5_REPLAY_REQUIRED
    - I6_AUTHORITY_DECLARATION
    - I7_NO_AUTHORITY_ESCALATION
    - I8_CLOSED_WORLD
    - I14_ADR_REQUIRED

  invariant_assertions:

    - identical inputs MUST produce identical outputs

    - replay MUST yield identical traces and hashes

    - deterministic refusal MUST remain replay-stable

    - no runtime mutation is introduced

    - no semantic equivalence is defined

    - duplicate intent MUST NOT trigger normalization

    - duplicate retry MUST NOT imply canonical identity

    - deterministic refusal remains invariant-preserving

# =====================================================
# FAILURE SURFACE ALIGNMENT
# =====================================================

  failure_surface:

    added_case:

      id: DUPLICATE_INTENT_REFUSAL

      failure_kind: OBSERVATIONAL_REFUSAL

      classification: DETERMINISTIC_RUNTIME_REFUSAL

      description: >

        Deterministic refusal observed under replay-stable
        re-execution of identical intent conditions.

      trigger_condition: >

        Runtime observes retry execution under identical
        deterministic RuntimeContext conditions.

      properties:

        deterministic: true

        replay_stable: true

        hash_stable: true

        observer_independent: true

        non_semantic: true

        non_normalizing: true

        non_equivalence_bound: true

        non_inferential: true

        runtime_existing_behavior: true

        replay_verified: true

      prohibited_interpretations:

        - semantic_equivalence
        - retry_identity_inference
        - canonicalization
        - request_normalization
        - deduplication_semantics
        - behavioral_generalization

# =====================================================
# NON-GOALS
# =====================================================

  non_goals:

    - defining intent equivalence

    - introducing retry idempotence guarantees

    - collapsing duplicate detection into runtime logic

    - modifying executor or orchestration layers

    - enabling semantic deduplication

    - introducing canonical request identity

    - creating retry normalization semantics

    - enabling runtime inference expansion

    - introducing observational-to-semantic promotion

# =====================================================
# CONSTITUTIONAL JUSTIFICATION
# =====================================================

  justification: >

    This ADR satisfies constitutional constraints because
    it introduces no executable behavioral mutation and
    preserves all deterministic replay guarantees.

    Constitutional preservation includes:

      - No silent mutation occurs (I3 preserved)

      - Deterministic execution remains unchanged
        (I4 preserved)

      - Replay validity remains unchanged
        (I5 preserved)

      - No authority expansion occurs
        (I6 and I7 preserved)

      - No new execution surface is introduced
        (I8 preserved)

      - Mutation remains ADR-governed
        (I14 satisfied)

    The mutation is strictly declarative and exists solely
    to align replay-confirmed observational behavior with
    formal constitutional taxonomy.

# =====================================================
# REPLAY ALIGNMENT
# =====================================================

  replay_alignment:

    replay_behavior_changed: false

    replay_hash_changed: false

    transcript_structure_changed: false

    replay_admissibility_changed: false

    deterministic_refusal_preexisting: true

    replay_interpretation_clarified: true

# =====================================================
# CLOSED-WORLD COMPLIANCE
# =====================================================

  closed_world_compliance:

    new_execution_surfaces_introduced: false

    undeclared_runtime_access: false

    semantic_runtime_extension: false

    dynamic_interpretation_introduced: false

    equivalence_resolution_added: false
    epistemic_status: OBSERVED_FACT
    semantic_commitment: NONE
    interpretation_required: false

# =====================================================
# CONSEQUENCES
# =====================================================

  consequences:

    positive:

      - aligns empirical behavior with declared failure taxonomy

      - improves replay auditability

      - strengthens proof-of-continuity semantics

      - removes ambiguity from deterministic refusal interpretation

      - formalizes observational refusal ontology

      - preserves Phase-2b semantic boundary integrity

    negative:

      - expands declarative constitutional taxonomy surface

      - introduces future taxonomy governance obligations

      - requires continued observational/semantic separation discipline

# =====================================================
# PHASE-2 BOUNDARY ASSERTION
# =====================================================

  phase_boundary_assertion: >

    This ADR does not activate Phase-2b equivalence-space logic.

    No semantic equivalence model is introduced.

    No retry identity semantics are defined.

    No normalization or canonicalization behavior exists.

    The ADR remains strictly observational and declarative.

# =====================================================
# STATUS & NEXT STEPS
# =====================================================

  status_notes:

    - No executor changes are required

    - No runtime deployment is triggered

    - No replay engine changes are required

    - No orchestration changes are required

    - May be incorporated into AfriRide v0.2 taxonomy

  approval_requirements:

    - replay verification confirmation

    - transcript hash consistency validation

    - taxonomy alignment review

    - constitutional replay audit

    - epoch registry update if ratified

# =====================================================
# FUTURE GOVERNANCE CONSTRAINTS
# =====================================================

  future_constraints:

    observational_refusal_must_not_imply_equivalence: true

    replay_observation_must_not_enable_normalization: true

    deterministic_refusal_must_remain_non_semantic: true

    future_semantic_promotion_requires_new_adr: true

    runtime_behavior_expansion_requires_epoch_transition: true

# =====================================================
# CANONICAL INTERPRETATION
# =====================================================

  canonical_interpretation: >

    This ADR does not introduce new behavior.

    It formally declares already-existing deterministic
    observational refusal as part of AfriRide’s constitutional
    proof surface.

    Replay remains authoritative.

    Runtime behavior remains unchanged.

    No execution semantics are modified.

    No invariants are weakened.

    No equivalence logic is introduced.

# =====================================================
# FINAL ASSERTION
# =====================================================

  assertion: >

    AfriRide does not reason about retry equivalence.

    It merely declares that when replay-observed identical
    deterministic conditions occur, deterministic refusal
    is itself part of the lawful constitutional proof surface.

    Observe → Prove → Replay → Declare.

    No semantic interpretation is activated.

      - expands AfriRide continuity proof to multiple failure modes
      - strengthens AfriTech institutional credibility
      - demonstrates scalable governance without historical mutation
      - preserves replay-verifiable lineage across epochs

    negative:
      - requires new constitutional epoch (Epoch 7)
      - increases governance surface area
      - introduces additional audit responsibilities

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ STATUS & NEXT STEPS
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  status_notes:
    - This ADR authorizes advancement to Epoch 7
    - AfriRide v0.2 may be frozen after ratification
    - No product, optimization, or performance claims are authorized

  approval_requirements:
    - governance review
    - replay verifier confirmation
    - epoch registry update


===== ./afritech/governance/anti_entropy.yaml =====
schema: afritech.governance.anti_entropy.v1

anti_entropy:

  description: >
    Defines risk classes that introduce implementation entropy.
    These must never occur in the system.

  risks:

    semantic_drift:
      forbidden: true

    implicit_runtime_semantics:
      forbidden: true

    proof_bypass:
      forbidden: true

    non_determinism:
      forbidden: true

    layer_contamination:
      forbidden: true

    optimization_semantic_shortcuts:
      forbidden: true

  enforcement:

    runtime: REQUIRED
    ci: REQUIRED
    code_review: REQUIRED
    architecture_freeze: REQUIRED

  executable_boundary:

    runtime_code_may:
      - execute_declared_semantics
      - normalize_declared_semantics
      - hash_normalized_semantics
      - evaluate_normalized_semantics
      - generate_proofs

    runtime_code_must_not:
      - define_semantics
      - infer_semantic_authority
      - bypass_normalization
      - evaluate_raw_expressions
      - introduce_new_operators_without_constitutional_declaration

  frozen_surfaces:
    constitution: FROZEN
    semantic_calculus: FROZEN
    meta_semantics: FROZEN

  allowed_changes_after_freeze:
    - bug_fixes
    - contradiction_resolution
    - implementation_required_clarifications

  failure:

    block_execution: true
    block_merge: true
    severity: CRITICAL


===== ./afritech/governance/autonomous_constitution.yaml =====
schema: afritech.governance.autonomous_constitution.v1

autonomous_constitution:

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # PURPOSE
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  description: >
    Defines a self-evolving constitutional system capable of:
      - detecting structural inefficiencies
      - generating governance improvements
      - validating upgrades via consensus
      - applying safe constitutional mutations

  model: SELF_UPGRADING_CONSTITUTIONAL_SYSTEM

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # CORE PRINCIPLES
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  principles:

    - constitution_is_mutable_but_controlled
    - all_changes_must_be_deterministically_justified
    - evolution_requires_consensus
    - replay_validity_must_be_preserved
    - backward_compatibility_must_be_enforced

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # EVOLUTION TRIGGERS
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  triggers:

    - repeated_consensus_failures
    - performance_degradation
    - governance_rule_conflicts
    - security_violations
    - persistent_node_disagreements
    - drift_pattern_detection

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # PROPOSAL GENERATION
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  proposal_engine:

    description: >
      Automatically generates constitutional amendments.

    inputs:

      - system_metrics
      - failure_patterns
      - node_reputation_history
      - replay_inconsistencies

    output:

      proposal:

        id: "ADR-AUTO-XXXX"

        type: GOVERNANCE_CHANGE

        changes:

          - modify_rule
          - adjust_threshold
          - introduce_new_constraint
          - deprecate_existing_rule

    invariant:

      - proposals_must_be_deterministic
      - proposals_must_be_replayable

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # SIMULATION LAYER
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  simulation:

    description: >
      Proposed changes are executed in a simulated environment.

    requirements:

      - deterministic_re-execution
      - replay_verification
      - historical_data_testing

    validation:

      must_pass:

        - all_previous_replay_cases
        - current_execution_paths
        - consensus_verification

      failure_effect: proposal_rejected

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # CONSENSUS APPROVAL
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  approval:

    model: MULTI_NODE_CONSENSUS

    requirements:

      - 2/3 quorum agreement
      - no critical replay regression
      - no security degradation

    voting:

      unit: node

      process:

        - evaluate_proposal
        - simulate_execution
        - submit_vote

    rejection_conditions:

      - replay_failure
      - increased divergence
      - invariant_violation

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # SAFE APPLICATION
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  application:

    description: >
      Approved changes are applied in a controlled manner.

    steps:

      - create_new_epoch
      - update_registry
      - regenerate_attestation
      - issue_new_certificate

    constraints:

      - atomic_change_application
      - rollback_possible
      - version_history_preserved

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # VERSIONING SYSTEM
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  versioning:

    version_scheme: SEMANTIC_CONSTITUTION

    components:

      - MAJOR: breaking governance change
      - MINOR: additive rule
      - PATCH: adjustment

    invariant:

      - version_must_increase_monotonically

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # SELF-VALIDATION LOOP
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  evolution_loop:

    cycle:

      - observe_system
      - detect_patterns
      - generate_proposal
      - simulate_proposal
      - consensus_vote
      - apply_or_reject

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # CONSTRAINTS (CRITICAL)
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  constraints:

    - no_change_may_break_replay
    - no_change_may_introduce_nondeterminism
    - no_change_may_bypass_authority_rules
    - no_change_may alter surface_registry without validation

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # FAIL-SAFE MECHANISMS
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  fail_safe:

    rollback:

      description: >
        If post-upgrade failure is detected,
        system reverts to previous version.

      trigger:

        - consensus_failure_post_upgrade
        - replay_regression

    freeze:

      description: >
        Evolution disabled if instability threshold exceeded.

      condition:

        - repeated_failed_proposals > threshold

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # GOVERNANCE MEMORY (ADR AUTO-GENERATION)
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  adr_generation:

    enabled: true

    description: >
      Every accepted proposal becomes an ADR.

    structure:

      - id
      - change_summary
      - justification
      - simulation_results
      - consensus_result

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # FINAL ASSERTION
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  final_assertion: >
    The constitution evolves itself.

    It observes its own behavior,
    improves its own rules,
    validates its own changes,
    and applies them without human intervention.

    No evolution without proof.
    No change without consensus.
    No regression without rollback.

===== ./afritech/governance/binding_schema.yaml =====
schema: afritech.binding.v1

binding_manifest:

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # SOURCE ARTIFACT ANCHORING (CRITICAL ROOT INPUTS)
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  source_artifacts:

    genesis_hash: sha256
    trace_schema_hash: sha256
    state_schema_hash: sha256
    invariants_hash: sha256

    # OPTIONAL EXTENSIONS
    proof_system_hash: sha256
    runtime_surface_hash: sha256

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # DERIVED BINDINGS (NO MANUAL DEFINITIONS)
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  bindings:

    - id: string

      type:
        enum:
          - TRACE_BINDING
          - STATE_BINDING
          - AUTHORITY_BINDING
          - PROOF_BINDING
          - RUNTIME_BINDING

      target: string
      constraint: string

      derived_from:
        - string

      # -------------------------------------------------------------
      # CRYPTOGRAPHIC IDENTITY
      # -------------------------------------------------------------

      binding_hash: sha256
      binding_version: string

      # -------------------------------------------------------------
      # EXECUTION CONTEXT
      # -------------------------------------------------------------

      scope:

        applies_to:
          - TRACE
          - STATE
          - EXECUTION
          - VALIDATION

        enforcement_level:
          enum:
            - STRICT
            - MANDATORY
            - OPTIONAL

      # -------------------------------------------------------------
      # VALIDATION RULE
      # -------------------------------------------------------------

      validation:

        required: true
        failure_policy:

          type: HARD_FAILURE
          effect: SYSTEM_REJECTION

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # ROOT BINDING COMMITMENT
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  root_binding_hash: sha256

  # sha256 over:
  #   ordered list of binding_hash values

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # DETERMINISM + REPLAY GUARANTEE
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  determinism:

    canonical_serialization: json_sorted_compact
    hashing_algorithm: sha256

    replay:

      expected:

        - identical_binding_list
        - identical_binding_hashes
        - identical_root_binding_hash

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # SYSTEM INVARIANTS (AUTHORITY CLOSURE)
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  invariants:

    - I21_BINDING_DERIVATION
      # all bindings MUST be machine-generated

    - I21_1_NO_MANUAL_BINDINGS
      # no human-authored bindings allowed

    - I21_2_CANONICAL_DERIVATION
      # identical inputs MUST produce identical bindings

    - I21_3_BINDING_HASH_INTEGRITY
      # each binding_hash MUST match canonical recomputation

    - I21_4_ROOT_HASH_CORRECT
      # root_binding_hash MUST match recomputed value

    - I21_5_AUTHORITY_DERIVED_FROM_GENESIS
      # authority MUST trace back to genesis_hash

    - I21_6_NO_ORPHAN_BINDINGS
      # every binding MUST derive from source artifacts

    - I21_7_REPLAY_EQUALITY
      # replay MUST regenerate identical manifest

    - I21_8_BINDING_ENUM_EXHAUSTIVENESS
      # all system layers MUST be covered by bindings

    - I21_9_IMMUTABILITY
      # bindings MUST NOT change after generation

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # VALIDATION CONTRACT
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  validation:

    required_at_system_boot: true
    required_for_runtime_execution: true
    required_for_proof_verification: true

    enforce_hash_integrity: true
    enforce_derivation: true
    enforce_total_binding_coverage: true

    failure_policy:

      type: HARD_FAILURE
      effect: SYSTEM_NON_EXISTENCE

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # TRACE + STATE INTEGRATION
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  integration:

    trace:

      requirement:
        trace.event.step MUST map to binding.target

    state_machine:

      requirement:
        transitions MUST comply with binding constraints

    proof:

      requirement:
        all proofs MUST validate against binding constraints

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # SECURITY MODEL
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  security:

    authority_model: DERIVED_ONLY
    tamper_resistance: CRYPTOGRAPHIC

    guarantees:

      - no hidden authority paths
      - no privilege escalation
      - no drift in derived bindings
      - no manual override possible

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # METADATA (NON-AUTHORITATIVE)
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  metadata:

    version: v1
    environment: production

    description: >
      Binding manifest schema defining the deterministic derivation
      of all authority relationships within AfriTech.

    notes: >
      This artifact MUST be generated automatically. Any manual
      modification invalidates the entire system.

rules:

  D1_NO_SHORTCUT:
    statement: >
      If correctness depends on a shortcut, the implementation must be rejected.

  D2_EXPLAINABILITY:
    statement: >
      Every evaluation must be traceable, normalized, and provable.

  D3_REPRODUCIBILITY:
    statement: >
      Any result must be reproducible across environments and runs.

  D4_NO_MAGIC:
    statement: >
      No hidden behavior, implicit logic, or silent inference is allowed.

review_requirements:

  - "Does this introduce semantic meaning in code?"
  - "Can this be expressed in S-IR?"
  - "Is this deterministic?"
  - "Are proofs preserved?"
  - "Is normalization enforced?"

===== ./afritech/governance/roles.yaml =====
schema: afritech.governance.roles.v1

# =====================================================================
# GOVERNANCE ROLES & QUORUM SEMANTICS (DECLARATIVE, NON-AUTHORITATIVE)
# =====================================================================
# This file defines GOVERNANCE INTENT ONLY.
#
# It:
#   - Grants NO authority
#   - Enforces NO rules
#   - Triggers NO behavior
#   - Is NOT consulted by runtime or guards
#
# Authority remains exclusively with:
#   - registry.yaml
#   - epoch mechanics
#   - ADR approval records
#
# This document exists to enable future institutional scalability
# without retroactively redefining legitimacy.
# =====================================================================

purpose: >
  Declarative description of governance roles and approval semantics
  for AfriTech constitutional evolution.
  This file documents how authority may be exercised by humans,
  but does not enforce or grant that authority.

# ---------------------------------------------------------------------
# Governance roles
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------

governance_roles:

  proposer:
    description: >
      Proposes Architectural Decision Records (ADRs).
      May author and submit changes for consideration.
    permissions:
      - draft_adr
      - submit_adr
    restrictions:
      - may_not_approve
      - may_not_reseal
      - may_not_advance_epoch

  verifier:
    description: >
      Reviews proposed ADRs for constitutional correctness,
      completeness, and invariant preservation.
    permissions:
      - review_adr
      - request_changes
    restrictions:
      - may_not_approve
      - may_not_execute
      - may_not_override

  approver:
    description: >
      Approves ADRs according to quorum rules.
      Approval authorizes epoch advancement but does not execute it.
    permissions:
      - approve_adr
    restrictions:
      - may_not_execute
      - may_not_override_runtime

  attestor:
    description: >
      Attests that governance procedures were followed correctly.
      Provides institutional confirmation only.
    permissions:
      - attest_process
    restrictions:
      - may_not_block
      - may_not_execute
      - may_not_override

# ---------------------------------------------------------------------
# Quorum semantics (declarative)
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------

quorum_rules:

  adr_approval:
    description: >
      Rules defining how many approvers are required
      to approve an ADR for constitutional evolution.
    model: SIMPLE_MAJORITY
    parameters:
      minimum_approvers: 1
      fraction_required: 0.50

  epoch_advance_authorization:
    description: >
      An epoch may advance only after a valid ADR approval quorum
      has been satisfied.
    depends_on:
      - adr_approval

# ---------------------------------------------------------------------
# Governance invariants (non-enforcing)
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------

governance_invariants:
  - no_single_actor_may_hold_all_roles
  - approval_and_execution_are_separate
  - governance_does_not_override_runtime
  - governance_never_bypasses_registry

# ---------------------------------------------------------------------
# Current operational mode
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------

operational_mode:
  governance_model: CENTRALIZED
  reason: >
    Current governance is intentionally centralized.
    These role definitions exist to support future
    scaling without ambiguity.

# ---------------------------------------------------------------------
# Authority disclaimer
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------

authority_disclaimer: >
  This file is documentary and non-authoritative.
  It does not grant power, enforce behavior,
  or supersede the registry, epochs, or runtime guards.
  In any conflict, registry.yaml and epoch history prevail.

# ---------------------------------------------------------------------
# Status
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------

status: ACTIVE
mutable: true

surface_registry:

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

    and governance status.

      - which surfaces are executable
      - which surfaces are included in hash binding
      - which surfaces are governed
      - which surfaces are strictly informational

      authority_scope: NONE

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
