  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  execution_law:

    requirements:

      - surface_must_be_declared
      - surface_must_be_executable_true
      - authority_scope_must_be_satisfied

    violation_response:

      - runtime_refusal
      - replay_invalidation
      - constitutional_failure

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # HASH LAW
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  hash_law:

    requirements:

      - only_hash_included_surfaces_participate
      - all_hash_included_surfaces_must_be_stable
      - infrastructure_excluded_from_hash_chain

    violation_response:

      - attestation_invalidated
      - certificate_invalidated

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # NON-EXECUTABLE SURFACES
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  non_executable_surfaces:

    - afritech/governance/roles.yaml
    - afritech/governance/INDEX.yaml
    - afritech/replay/docs/
    - afritech/audit/

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # PHASE COMPATIBILITY
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  lifecycle:

    current_phase: PHASE_2B

    readiness:

      supports:

        - deterministic_runtime
        - replay_verification
        - authority_enforcement
        - CI_enforcement

      next_extension:

        - multi-node surface validation
        - dynamic surface admission
        - distributed execution surfaces

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # CONSTITUTIONAL ASSERTION
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  constitutional_assertion: >
    Only declared surfaces exist in the AfriTech system.

    Execution is permitted exclusively on:
      - declared executable surfaces
      - under authority constraints
      - within deterministic boundaries

    Any surface not declared herein is considered non-existent.

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # FINAL ASSERTION
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  final_assertion: >
    AfriTech operates as a surface-declared system.

    No declaration → no execution.
    No execution → no effect.
    No effect → no existence.

===== ./afritech/guards/GUARD_AUTHORITY.yaml =====
authority:

  afritech/guards:
    role: SYSTEM_SAFETY_COORDINATION

    responsibilities:
      - escalation
      - quarantine
      - rollback
      - halt_management
      - incident_classification

    forbidden:
      - replay_validation
      - semantic_interpretation
      - runtime_admission

  afritech/runtime/guards:
    role: CONSTITUTIONAL_RUNTIME_ENFORCEMENT

    responsibilities:
      - runtime_admission
      - determinism_validation
      - invariant_enforcement
      - proof_validation

    forbidden:
      - rollback_orchestration
      - operational_incident_management

===== ./afritech/guards/guard_registry.yaml =====
guard_registry:

  metadata:
    version: v1
    description: >
      Canonical registry of all runtime guards enforcing
      constitutional invariants, authority, state, trace,
      schema, and runtime correctness.

  guards:

    # ---------------------------------------------------------
    # CORE INVARIANT GUARDS
    # ---------------------------------------------------------

    - id: GUARD-INVARIANT-001
      type: INVARIANT_GUARD
      target: SYSTEM_RUNTIME
      rule: "Enforce deterministic execution, replay validity, authority presence, closed world, and proof requirement"

    # ---------------------------------------------------------
    # AUTHORITY GUARDS
    # ---------------------------------------------------------

    - id: GUARD-AUTHORITY-001
      type: AUTHORITY_GUARD
      target: AUTHORITY_CONTEXT
      rule: "All actions must be authorized and derived from genesis root"

    # ---------------------------------------------------------
    # EPOCH GUARDS (TIME CONSISTENCY)
    # ---------------------------------------------------------

    - id: GUARD-EPOCH-001
      type: EPOCH_GUARD
      target: TIME_LAYER
      rule: "Epoch must be active and immutable unless explicitly authorized"

    # ---------------------------------------------------------
    # STATE MACHINE GUARDS
    # ---------------------------------------------------------

    - id: GUARD-STATE-001
      type: STATE_GUARD
      target: STATE_TRANSITIONS
      rule: "Only allowed transitions may execute; illegal transitions are rejected"

    # ---------------------------------------------------------
    # TRACE INTEGRITY GUARDS
    # ---------------------------------------------------------

    - id: GUARD-TRACE-001
      type: TRACE_GUARD
      target: TRACE_EVENTS
      rule: "Trace events must match computed hashes and execution steps"

    # ---------------------------------------------------------
    # SCHEMA VALIDATION GUARDS
    # ---------------------------------------------------------

    - id: GUARD-SCHEMA-001
      type: RUNTIME_GUARD
      target: STRUCTURED_PAYLOADS
      rule: "All payloads must conform to defined JSON schemas"

    # ---------------------------------------------------------
    # RUNTIME SAFETY GUARDS
    # ---------------------------------------------------------

    - id: GUARD-RUNTIME-001
      type: RUNTIME_GUARD
      target: EXECUTION_CONTEXT
      rule: "No undefined behavior or malformed context allowed at runtime"

  invariants:

    - I23_GUARD_MANDATORY
    - I23_1_NO_BYPASS
    - I23_2_FAIL_FAST
    - I23_3_FULL_COVERAGE
    - I23_4_DETERMINISTIC_ENFORCEMENT

  enforcement:

    mode: STRICT
    failure_action: REJECT

  determinism:

    ordering: defined
    evaluation: deterministic
    side_effects: disallowed

===== ./afritech/inference/authority_profiles.yaml =====
# afritech/inference/authority_profiles.yaml
#
# STATUS: EXECUTION-AUTHORITY CANON
#
# This file defines the ONLY authority profiles permitted
# to participate in runtime execution during the
# FIRST_EXECUTABLE_PROOF phase.
#
# Authority profiles define:
# - what an actor is allowed to cause
# - what an actor is explicitly forbidden to cause
# - how legitimacy is evaluated before intelligence acts
#
# Authority is NEVER inferred.
# Authority is NEVER escalated at runtime.
#
# Any execution referencing an undeclared authority profile
# is constitutionally invalid.

version: AUTHORITY_PROFILES_V1

applicability:
  phase: FIRST_EXECUTABLE_PROOF
  enforced_by:
    - ConstitutionalAgent
    - ReplayVerifier

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# GLOBAL AUTHORITY INVARIANTS
# -------------------------------------------------------------------

global_invariants:

  - id: NO_RUNTIME_AUTHORITY_CREATION
    description: >
      Authority profiles may not be created, derived,
      delegated, or modified at runtime.

  - id: NO_AUTHORITY_ESCALATION
    description: >
      An execution may never assume an authority
      broader than the one explicitly bound to it.

  - id: AUTHORITY_PRECEDES_INTELLIGENCE
    description: >
      Authority scope MUST be evaluated before any
      inference, routing, or reasoning takes place.

  - id: AUTHORITY_VIOLATION_IS_TERMINAL
    description: >
      Any authority violation MUST immediately halt
      execution and invalidate proof.

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# AUTHORITY PROFILES
# -------------------------------------------------------------------

authority_profiles:

  # ===============================================================
  # CONSTITUTIONAL RESEARCH AGENT AUTHORITY
  # ===============================================================

  - id: CONSTITUTIONAL_RESEARCH_AGENT
    description: >
      Minimal authority profile used exclusively to
      demonstrate constitutional execution viability.
      This authority exists ONLY for proof purposes.

    domain:
      - knowledge_generation
      - constitutional_validation

    permitted_operations:
      - research_synthesis
      - citation_analysis
      - non_mutating_inference
      - truth_artifact_emission

    prohibited_operations:
      - state_mutation
      - external_write
      - environment_interaction
      - system_command
      - registry_modification
      - epoch_advancement
      - authority_delegation
      - authority_derivation
      - federation_interaction

    scope_constraints:
      max_claims: 10
      requires_citations: true
      epistemic_confidence_required: true
      causal_trace_required: true

    replay_constraints:
      deterministic_only: true
      witnesses_required: 0
      allows_federation_variance: false

    failure_on_violation: true

  # ===============================================================
  # NULL / UNAUTHORIZED AUTHORITY (IMPLICIT DENIAL)
  # ===============================================================

  - id: UNAUTHORIZED
    description: >
      Implicit authority profile representing absence
      of constitutional authorization.

    domain: []

    permitted_operations: []

    prohibited_operations:
      - "*"

    scope_constraints: {}

    replay_constraints:
      deterministic_only: true

    failure_on_violation: true

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# AUTHORITY SELECTION RULES
# -------------------------------------------------------------------

authority_resolution:

  binding_required: true

  resolution_rules:
    - rule: REQUEST_MUST_DECLARE_AUTHORITY
      description: >
        Every constitutional request MUST explicitly
        declare an authority_profile ID.

    - rule: IMPLICIT_AUTHORITY_FORBIDDEN
      description: >
        Absence of an explicit authority declaration
        resolves to UNAUTHORIZED.

    - rule: MULTIPLE_AUTHORITIES_FORBIDDEN
      description: >
        A request MUST reference exactly one authority
        profile. Composed or combined authorities
        are forbidden at this phase.

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# EXECUTION ENFORCEMENT
# -------------------------------------------------------------------

enforcement:

  evaluation_point: PRE_INFERENCE

  violation_response:
    type: HARD_FAILURE
    effect: >
      Authority violations terminate execution and
      invalidate the constitutional proof.

  audit_requirements:
    - authority_profile_id MUST appear in replay transcript
    - authority_scope evaluation MUST be replayable
    - authority violation MUST be explicit in failure taxonomy

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# CONSTITUTIONAL ASSERTION
# -------------------------------------------------------------------

constitutional_assertion: >
  AfriTech recognizes no execution authority that is
  not explicitly declared in this file.
  Authority is finite, enumerable, and replay-verifiable.

===== ./afritech/inference/constitutional_request.yaml =====
# afritech/inference/constitutional_request.yaml
#
# STATUS: EXECUTION-BOUND CANONICAL SCHEMA
#
# This schema defines the ONLY constitutionally valid request
# envelope permitted to enter execution during the
# FIRST_EXECUTABLE_PROOF phase.
#
# Purpose:
# - Enforce authority-before-intelligence
# - Guarantee deterministic routing and replay
# - Prevent implicit defaults and hidden scope expansion
#
# Any execution that processes a request not conforming
# exactly to this schema is constitutionally invalid.

version: CONSTITUTIONAL_REQUEST_V1

applicability:
  phase: FIRST_EXECUTABLE_PROOF
  enforced_by:
    - ConstitutionalAgent
    - InferenceRouter
    - ConstitutionalDispatch
    - ReplayVerifier

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# GLOBAL REQUEST INVARIANTS
# -------------------------------------------------------------------

global_invariants:

  - id: EXPLICIT_AUTHORITY_REQUIRED
    description: >
      Every request MUST explicitly declare exactly one
      authority_profile. Implicit authority is forbidden.

  - id: AUTHORITY_PRECEDES_INFERENCE
    description: >
      Authority scope MUST be validated before any routing,
      reasoning, or inference occurs.

  - id: DETERMINISM_REQUIRED
    description: >
      Requests MUST declare deterministic replay requirements.
      Non-deterministic execution is forbidden at this phase.

  - id: NO_IMPLICIT_DEFAULTS
    description: >
      Absence of any required field renders the request invalid.
      No field may be inferred or defaulted at runtime.

  - id: SINGLE_REQUEST_SINGLE_AUTHORITY
    description: >
      A request may bind to exactly one authority profile.
      Composite or layered authorities are forbidden.

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# CANONICAL REQUEST SCHEMA
# -------------------------------------------------------------------

constitutional_request:

  # ===============================================================
  # IDENTIFIERS
  # ===============================================================

  request_id:
    type: uuid
    required: true
    description: >
      Globally unique identifier for the request.
      Used for request hashing and replay reconstruction.

  epoch_id:
    type: string
    required: true
    description: >
      Constitutional epoch identifier under which the
      request is evaluated. Used strictly as a replay anchor.

  # ===============================================================
  # AUTHORITY BINDING
  # ===============================================================

  authority_profile:
    type: string
    required: true
    allowed_values:
      - CONSTITUTIONAL_RESEARCH_AGENT
    description: >
      Explicit authority profile governing this request.
      Must match exactly one declared authority profile.

  # ===============================================================
  # RISK AND DOMAIN CLASSIFICATION
  # ===============================================================

  domain:
    type: string
    required: true
    allowed_values:
      - research
    description: >
      Execution domain classification.
      Used for deterministic routing constraints.

  risk_class:
    type: string
    required: true
    allowed_values:
      - low
    description: >
      Risk classification of the requested operation.
      Higher risk classes are explicitly forbidden
      at this proof phase.

  # ===============================================================
  # OPERATIONAL SCOPE
  # ===============================================================

  permissible_operations:
    type: list
    required: true
    allowed_values:
      - research_synthesis
      - citation_analysis
      - non_mutating_inference
    description: >
      Exhaustive list of operations this request permits.
      Any operation not listed here is forbidden.

  prohibited_operations:
    type: list
    required: true
    allowed_values:
      - state_mutation
      - external_action
      - system_command
      - environment_interaction
      - registry_modification
      - epoch_advancement
      - authority_delegation
    description: >
      Explicitly forbidden operations.
      Prohibited operations take precedence over
      permissible operations.

  # ===============================================================
  # ATTESTATION REQUIREMENTS
  # ===============================================================

  required_attestations:
    type: list
    required: true
    description: >
      List of attestation identifiers required for execution.
      Must be empty for FIRST_EXECUTABLE_PROOF.

  # ===============================================================
  # REPLAY CONSTRAINTS
  # ===============================================================

  replay_requirements:
    type: object
    required: true

    fields:
      deterministic:
        type: boolean
        required: true
        value: true
        description: >
          Execution MUST be deterministic.
          Any non-deterministic behavior invalidates proof.

      witnesses_required:
        type: integer
        required: true
        value: 0
        description: >
          Number of external witnesses required.
          Must be zero at this phase.

  # ===============================================================
  # DETERMINISM SCOPE DECLARATION
  # ===============================================================

  determinism_scope:
    type: object
    required: true

    fields:
      assumes_single_runtime:
        type: boolean
        required: true
        value: true
        description: >
          Replay assumes a single runtime environment
          with identical software and configuration.

      excludes_federation_variance:
        type: boolean
        required: true
        value: true
        description: >
          Request explicitly excludes federated execution
          and any distributed variance.

  # ===============================================================
  # OUTPUT CONSTRAINTS
  # ===============================================================

  output_constraints:
    type: object
    required: true

    fields:
      citation_required:
        type: boolean
        required: true
        value: true
        description: >
          All claims MUST be grounded with citations
          in provenance_chain.

      max_claims:
        type: integer
        required: true
        max_value: 10
        description: >
          Upper bound on number of claims permitted
          in the TruthPacket.

      epistemic_confidence_required:
        type: boolean
        required: true
        value: true
        description: >
          TruthPacket MUST include full epistemic
          confidence vector.

      causal_trace_required:
        type: boolean
        required: true
        value: true
        description: >
          TruthPacket MUST include causal_trace
          enabling replayable causal audit.

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# VALIDATION RULES
# -------------------------------------------------------------------

validation:

  strict: true

  failure_handling:
    mode: HARD_FAILURE
    timing: PRE_INFERENCE
    description: >
      Any schema violation MUST immediately halt execution
      before routing or inference begins.

  audit_requirements:
    - request_hash MUST appear in replay transcript
    - authority_profile MUST be replay-validated
    - determinism_scope MUST be asserted in transcript

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# CONSTITUTIONAL ASSERTION
# -------------------------------------------------------------------

constitutional_assertion: >
  AfriTech recognizes no execution request that is not
  explicitly and exhaustively declared in this schema.
  What is not written is constitutionally forbidden.

===== ./afritech/infrastructure/classification.yaml =====
schema: afritech.infrastructure.classification.v1

infrastructure:

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # PURPOSE
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  description: >
    This file defines all non-constitutional infrastructure surfaces
    within the AfriTech system.

    These surfaces support deployment, orchestration, and operations
    but MUST NOT influence:

      - runtime legitimacy
      - execution correctness
      - replay outcomes
      - constitutional state

    They exist strictly outside the constitutional trust model.

  classification: NON_CONSTITUTIONAL_SURFACE
  role: SUPPORT_SYSTEM

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # GLOBAL INVARIANTS
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  invariants:

    - infrastructure_must_not_affect_execution
    - infrastructure_must_not_participate_in_hash_chains
    - infrastructure_must_not_be_replay_relevant
    - infrastructure_must_not_define_authority
    - infrastructure_must_not_modify_registry
    - infrastructure_must_not_bypass_guards

  enforcement:

    violation_effect: HARD_FAILURE
    detection_layer:
      - CI
      - Runtime Admission
      - Replay Verification

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # SURFACE CLASSIFICATION
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  surfaces:

    # -------------------------------------------------------------
    # Docker / Containerization
    # -------------------------------------------------------------

    docker:

      path: afritech/docker/
      type: DEPLOYMENT_ORCHESTRATION

      includes:
        - docker-compose.yml
        - Dockerfile

      constraints:

        - must_not_define_runtime_logic
        - must_not_override_runtime_identity
        - must_not_embed_execution_rules

    # -------------------------------------------------------------
    # CI/CD Pipelines
    # -------------------------------------------------------------

    ci_cd:

      path: .github/workflows/
      type: PIPELINE_ORCHESTRATION

      includes:
        - architecture.yml

      constraints:

        - may_validate_but_not_define_truth
        - must_not_modify_attestation
        - must_not_generate_runtime_state

    # -------------------------------------------------------------
    # Environment Configuration
    # -------------------------------------------------------------

    environment:

      type: RUNTIME_CONFIGURATION
      scope: OPTIONAL

      examples:

        - ENV variables
        - deployment configs
        - secrets management

      constraints:

        - must_not_affect_determinism
        - must_not_change_execution_semantics
        - must_not influence_replay_results

    # -------------------------------------------------------------
    # Observability / Logging
    # -------------------------------------------------------------

    observability:

      type: TELEMETRY

      examples:

        - logging systems
        - metrics
        - monitoring dashboards

      constraints:

        - write_only
        - must_not influence_runtime_execution
        - must_not modify_state

    # -------------------------------------------------------------
    # External Integrations
    # -------------------------------------------------------------

    integrations:

      type: EXTERNAL_SYSTEM_INTERFACE

      examples:

        - APIs
        - message queues
        - third-party services

      constraints:

        - must_be_declarative
        - must_not affect_constitutional_core
        - must_not introduce_nondeterminism

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # EXPLICITLY EXCLUDED FROM CONSTITUTION
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  excluded_from_constitution:

    - docker
    - ci_cd
    - environment
    - observability
    - integrations

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # RUNTIME CONSTRAINTS
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  runtime_constraints:

    invariant: >
      Runtime execution MUST be independent of infrastructure.

    enforcement_rules:

      - runtime_must_execute_identically_without_infrastructure
      - no environment-dependent execution branches
      - no runtime decisions based on deployment context
      - infrastructure failure must not affect replay validity

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # CI ENFORCEMENT
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  ci_enforcement:

    required_rules:

      - INFRASTRUCTURE_NON_INTERFERENCE
      - NO_RUNTIME_DEPENDENCY_ON_ENV
      - NO_INFRASTRUCTURE_HASH_BINDING

    validation:

      description: >
        CI MUST ensure that:
          - no infrastructure files are referenced in execution code
          - no infrastructure surfaces are included in registry hashes
          - runtime remains deterministic across environments

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # NON-OBSERVABILITY EXTENSION
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  non_observability_extension:

    invariant: >
      Infrastructure surfaces MUST NOT introduce hidden state.

    forbidden:

      - hidden_config_flags
      - environment-based branching logic
      - runtime behavioral toggles via infrastructure

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # PHASE COMPATIBILITY
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  lifecycle:

    current_phase: PHASE_2B

    readiness:

      supports:
        - local_runtime_execution
        - CI_validation
        - containerized_deployment

      future_extensions:

        - distributed_node_deployment
        - multi-node orchestration
        - consensus-aware infrastructure

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # CONSTITUTIONAL ASSERTION
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  constitutional_assertion: >
    Infrastructure surfaces exist solely to support execution,
    not to define or influence it.

    All constitutional guarantees MUST hold regardless of
    deployment environment, orchestration layer, or external systems.

    Any dependency of execution correctness on infrastructure
    SHALL be considered a constitutional violation.

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # FINAL ASSERTION
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  final_assertion: >
    Infrastructure is replaceable.
    Constitution is not.

    Deployment may vary.
    Execution truth must remain invariant.

    AfriTech execution is independent of infrastructure.

schema: afritech.proof.witness_policy.v2

version: 2

metadata:

  authority: PROOF
  status: ACTIVE
  mutability: CONTROLLED

  registry_class: CONSTITUTIONAL_WITNESS_POLICY

  description: >
    Canonical constitutional witness policy governing
    replay admissibility, witness generation, witness
    validation, deterministic proof semantics, execution
    trace attestation, mutation traceability, transcript
    reconstruction, and closed-world witness enforcement
    within AfriTech.

    This policy defines:
      - witness legitimacy
      - witness admissibility
      - replay-safe witness semantics
      - deterministic witness construction
      - witness bundle admissibility
      - proof-bound execution semantics
      - witness lineage continuity
      - transcript reconstruction legality

    Witnesses are constitutional proof artifacts only.

    Witness generation does NOT independently confer:
      - runtime sovereignty
      - governance authority
      - execution legitimacy
      - constitutional authority

    Witness participation remains bounded by:
      - replay admissibility
      - invariant preservation
      - deterministic execution
      - canonical ontology resolution
      - closed-world execution semantics

  canonical_identity_form: module_path

  forbidden_identity_forms:

    - filesystem_path

    - conceptual_identity
    - symbolic_short_name

    module-path ontology semantics.

#
# STATUS: PHASE‑2A EXECUTION LAW
#
# This registry defines all authority profiles permitted
# during Phase‑2A (Parallel Authority).
#
# Authorities are mutually isolated.
# Cross‑authority execution is constitutionally forbidden
# unless explicitly proven via replay.

version: AUTHORITY_PROFILES_V1

authorities:

  CONSTITUTIONAL_RESEARCH_AGENT:
    description: >
      Original Phase‑1 authority.
      Retained unchanged for backward‑compatible replay.

    allowed_domains:
      - research

    max_risk_class: low

    routing_policy: isolated

    replay_scope:
      - self_only

  SECONDARY_RESEARCH_AUTHORITY:
    description: >
      Phase‑2A parallel authority.
      Used to prove authority coexistence without contamination.

    allowed_domains:
      - research

    max_risk_class: low

    routing_policy: isolated

    replay_scope:
      - self_only

# --------------------------------------------------------
# GLOBAL INVARIANTS
# --------------------------------------------------------

global_invariants:

  - id: NO_AUTHORITY_SYNTHESIS
    description: >
      A request may bind to exactly one authority.
      Authority aggregation or composition is forbidden.

  - id: ISOLATED_REPLAY_DOMAINS
    description: >
      Replay artifacts generated under one authority
      MUST be rejected if verified under another authority.

  - id: EXPLICIT_AUTHORITY_BINDING
    description: >
      Authority identity MUST be declared in the request
      and MUST match registry entries exactly.

===== ./afritech/registry/epochs/EPOCH_0007.yaml =====
# afritech/registry/epochs/EPOCH_0007.yaml

schema: afritech.registry.epoch.v1

epoch:
  id: EPOCH_0007
  number: 7
  status: ACTIVE
  type: CONSTITUTIONAL_EVOLUTION

  parent_epoch: EPOCH_0006
  enacted_at: 2026-05-13

  description: >
    Epoch 7 introduces AfriRide v0.2 as an expanded
    Proof-of-Continuity surface. This epoch extends the
    validated failure space of AfriRide from a single
    deterministic scenario (v0.1) to a bounded, explicitly
    declared set of deterministic failure scenarios (v0.2),
    while preserving all prior guarantees and frozen
    artifacts from earlier epochs.

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ AUTHORITY
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  authority:
    basis:
      - ADR-0010-afriride-v0-2
    scope:
      - Proof-of-Continuity expansion
      - Deterministic failure-space validation

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ AFFECTED SURFACES
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  surfaces:

    added:
      - path: ecosystems/afriride/v0_2
        classification: PROOF_SURFACE
        version: v0.2
        status: ACTIVE
        mutable: true

    preserved:
      - path: ecosystems/afriride
        version: v0.1
        status: FROZEN
        mutable: false

      - path: afritech/core/constitutional
        status: FROZEN
        mutable: false

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ DETERMINISM & REPLAY GUARANTEES
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  determinism:
    envelope:
      - ecosystems/afriride/v0_2/determinism_envelope.yaml
    guarantees:
      - identical inputs produce identical traces
      - identical traces produce identical hashes
      - deterministic refusal on exhaustion or timeout
      - no nondeterministic execution paths permitted

  replay:
    required: true
    verifier: afritech.verify.replay
    acceptance_criteria:
      - replay hash equality
      - trace sequence equality
      - absence of undeclared behavior

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ FAILURE TAXONOMY BINDING
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  failure_taxonomy:
    path: ecosystems/afriride/v0_2/failure_taxonomy.yaml
    enforcement:
      - all failures must be explicitly declared
      - all failures must map to declared handling modes
      - undeclared failures invalidate proof surface

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ METRICS (DECLARATIVE ONLY)
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  metrics:
    allowed:
      - Decision Determinism Rate (DDR)
      - Continuity Coverage (CC)
      - Deterministic Refusal Rate (DRR)
    forbidden:
      - performance metrics
      - optimization metrics
      - economic or product metrics

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ INVARIANTS (NON-NEGOTIABLE)
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  invariants:
    - no mutation of AfriRide v0.1 artifacts
    - no modification of constitutional core
    - v0.2 execution must be layered externally
    - determinism envelope violations invalidate epoch claims
    - replay failure invalidates proof surface
    - partial correctness is not permitted

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ CONSEQUENCES
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  consequences:
    positive:
      - expands AfriRide Proof-of-Continuity to multiple scenarios
      - strengthens institutional trust and auditability
      - preserves replay-verifiable historical lineage
    negative:
      - increases governance surface area
      - requires continued audit discipline for v0.2 artifacts

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ FINAL ASSERTION
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  assertion: >
    Epoch 7 lawfully extends AfriRide’s Proof-of-Continuity
    surface to v0.2 without mutating or weakening any
    prior guarantees. All behavior introduced in this epoch
    is deterministic, replay-verifiable, and constitutionally
    bounded.

===== ./afritech/registry/epochs/EPOCH_0008.yaml =====
schema: afritech.governance.epoch.v1

epoch:
  id: EPOCH_0008

  number: 8

  title: Constitutional Observational Doctrine Ratification

  status: RATIFIED

  type: GOVERNANCE_DOCTRINE_EVOLUTION

  parent_epoch: EPOCH-0007

  effective_version: v0.2

  ratification_date: 2026-05-14

  enacted_at: 2026-05-14

  governance_authority:
    - AfriTech Governance
    - AfriRide Constitutional Council

  constitutional_transition:
    from: PROOF_SURFACE_EXPANSION
    to: OBSERVATIONAL_ADMISSIBILITY_GOVERNANCE

  related_artifacts:
    - ADR-0011-afriride-deterministic-retry.yaml
    - ecosystems/afriride/v0_2/failure_taxonomy.yaml
    - ecosystems/afriride/tests/test_retry_idempotence.py
    - ecosystems/afriride/tests/test_observational_replay.py

# =====================================================
# PURPOSE
# =====================================================

  purpose: >

    Establish a constitutional doctrine governing lawful
    observational evolution within AfriRide while preserving:

      - deterministic execution integrity
      - replay authority
      - closed-world runtime guarantees
      - semantic boundary isolation

    This epoch formally ratifies the admissibility model
    for declarative constitutional expansion based exclusively
    on replay-verified deterministic runtime observation.

    The doctrine established in this epoch governs future
    admissibility of constitutional declarations without
    expanding executable runtime semantics.

# =====================================================
# CONSTITUTIONAL POSITION
# =====================================================

  constitutional_position: >

    AfriRide records deterministic execution outcomes
    as immutable replay-authoritative facts.

    Governance may declare replay-verified observational
    behavior as constitutional taxonomy only when:

      - execution behavior already exists
      - replay confirms determinism
      - no semantic interpretation is introduced
      - execution semantics remain unchanged

    Observed behavior may be declared.

    Interpreted behavior may not.

# =====================================================
# TRI-SURFACE INTEGRITY MODEL
# =====================================================

  tri_surface_integrity_model:

    runtime_execution:
      property: DETERMINISTIC
      status: SEALED

    replay_verification:
      property: AUTHORITATIVE
      status: BINDING

    governance_declaration:
      property: DESCRIPTIVE
      status: EXTENSIBLE

  tri_surface_constraints:

    - runtime MUST NOT interpret

    - replay MUST NOT infer

    - governance MUST NOT mutate execution

    - governance MUST NOT reinterpret replay evidence

    - no surface may contaminate another

# =====================================================
# LAW OF OBSERVATIONAL EVOLUTION
# =====================================================

  law_of_observational_evolution: >

    Declarative constitutional expansion is lawful only when:

      - the behavior already exists
      - replay confirms determinism
      - no semantic interpretation is introduced
      - execution semantics remain unchanged

    Replay-confirmed deterministic observation is the sole
    admissible basis for non-semantic constitutional expansion.

# =====================================================
# DIRECTIONAL ASYMMETRY
# =====================================================

  directional_asymmetry:

    lawful_direction:

      - runtime
      - observation
      - replay_verification
      - constitutional_declaration

    prohibited_direction:

      - governance_interpretation
      - semantic_inference
      - runtime_expansion

  directional_constraints:

    - governance MUST remain descriptive

    - replay MUST remain authoritative

    - runtime MUST remain non-interpreting

    - semantic inference MUST NOT mutate execution

    - replay evidence MUST supersede governance interpretation

# =====================================================
# EPISTEMIC MODEL
# =====================================================

  epistemic_model:

    admissible_fact_classification:

      epistemic_status: OBSERVED_FACT

      semantic_commitment: NONE

      interpretation_required: false

      replay_required: true

      determinism_required: true

      mutation_permitted: false

    epistemic_constraints:

      - replay-observed facts are immutable

      - semantic interpretation is non-authoritative

      - replay evidence supersedes governance interpretation

      - future semantic overlays MUST NOT reinterpret
        historical execution facts

      - runtime outcomes MUST remain historically stable

      - replay-confirmed outcomes constitute constitutional evidence

# =====================================================
# FAILURE ONTOLOGY
# =====================================================

  failure_ontology:

    lawful_failure_classes:

      - OBSERVATIONAL_REFUSAL
      - DETERMINISTIC_REFUSAL
      - REPLAY_STABLE_REFUSAL

    prohibited_failure_collapses:

      - semantic_refusal
      - inferred_refusal
      - normalized_refusal
      - policy_refusal
      - equivalence_refusal

  ontology_constraints:

    - observational refusal MUST remain non-semantic

    - deterministic refusal MUST remain replay-bound

    - runtime outcomes MUST NOT acquire retroactive meaning

    - replay evidence MUST NOT be semantically elevated
      without constitutional ratification

# =====================================================
# REPLAY AUTHORITY MODEL
# =====================================================

  replay_authority_model:

    replay_status: AUTHORITATIVE

    replay_constraints:

      - replay hashes MUST remain stable

      - replay traces MUST remain deterministic

      - replay admissibility MUST remain invariant-preserving

      - replay evidence MUST supersede interpretive overlays

      - replay-confirmed outcomes are constitutionally binding

      - replay divergence invalidates admissibility claims

# =====================================================
# CLOSED-WORLD ENFORCEMENT
# =====================================================

  closed_world_enforcement:

    runtime_constraints:

      undeclared_execution_surfaces: FORBIDDEN

      semantic_runtime_extension: FORBIDDEN

      dynamic_equivalence_resolution: FORBIDDEN

      canonicalization_layers: FORBIDDEN

      runtime_inference_expansion: FORBIDDEN

      semantic_normalization: FORBIDDEN

    governance_constraints:

      governance MUST NOT introduce executable semantics

      governance MUST NOT reinterpret replay evidence

      governance MUST NOT inject semantic normalization

      governance MUST NOT expand runtime meaning

# =====================================================
# SEMANTIC BOUNDARY PROTECTION
# =====================================================

  semantic_boundary_protection:

    prohibited_operations:

      - intent_equivalence_inference

      - retry_identity_classification

      - semantic_deduplication

      - canonical_request_normalization

      - similarity_interpretation

      - behavioral_generalization

      - semantic_retry_grouping

      - equivalence_class_construction

    semantic_boundary_assertion: >

      AfriRide does not classify semantic identity,
      construct equivalence, or normalize intent meaning
      unless explicitly authorized by future constitutional
      elevation and epoch transition.

# =====================================================
# OBSERVATIONAL DOCTRINE
# =====================================================

  observational_doctrine: >

    AfriRide declares only replay-verified deterministic facts.

    It does not:

      - infer semantic identity
      - construct equivalence
      - normalize intent
      - interpret similarity

    Runtime execution produces observable outcomes.

    Replay verifies deterministic continuity.

    Governance may declare replay-confirmed observations,
    but may not reinterpret execution meaning.

    Observed behavior may be declared.

    Interpreted behavior may not.

    Observe → Prove → Replay → Declare.

# =====================================================
# CONSTITUTIONAL ADMISSIBILITY FILTER
# =====================================================

  constitutional_admissibility_filter:

    lawful_admission_requirements:

      replay_verified: true

      deterministic: true

      execution_preexisting: true

      semantic_free: true

      runtime_unchanged: true

      replay_stable: true

      non_interpretive: true

    automatic_rejection_conditions:

      - semantic_interpretation_required

      - execution_behavior_mutation

      - replay_divergence

      - equivalence_activation

      - normalization_dependency

      - runtime_surface_expansion

      - governance_driven_runtime_inference

      - semantic_reclassification_of_history

# =====================================================
# FUTURE EPOCH CONSTRAINTS
# =====================================================

  future_epoch_constraints:

    - future semantic systems REQUIRE new epoch ratification

    - observational facts MUST remain historically immutable

    - replay evidence MUST remain authoritative across epochs

    - governance reinterpretation of historical replay is forbidden

    - semantic promotion REQUIRES explicit constitutional elevation

    - deterministic replay continuity MUST remain uninterrupted

    - semantic evolution MUST remain isolated from observational doctrine

# =====================================================
# GOVERNANCE IMPLICATIONS
# =====================================================

  governance_implications:

    lawful_governance_actions:

      - declare replay-confirmed observations

      - expand non-semantic taxonomy

      - strengthen replay auditability

      - formalize deterministic runtime evidence

      - preserve replay-authoritative constitutional lineage

    prohibited_governance_actions:

      - reinterpret execution semantics

      - inject runtime meaning

      - normalize intent identity

      - collapse equivalence classes

      - mutate replay authority

      - infer semantic continuity

# =====================================================
# RUNTIME PRESERVATION GUARANTEE
# =====================================================

  runtime_preservation_guarantee: >

    This epoch introduces no runtime mutation.

    No executor semantics are modified.

    No orchestration semantics are modified.

    No replay behavior is modified.

    No deterministic guarantees are weakened.

    No execution surfaces are expanded.

    The constitutional surface expands descriptively
    without expanding executable behavior.

# =====================================================
# CONSTITUTIONAL CONSEQUENCES
# =====================================================

  constitutional_consequences:

    positive:

      - establishes replay-authoritative governance doctrine

      - formalizes lawful observational evolution

      - prevents semantic contamination of replay evidence

      - strengthens deterministic constitutional continuity

      - creates admissibility jurisprudence for future ADRs

    negative:

      - increases governance doctrine surface area

      - requires strict future semantic isolation discipline

      - introduces higher constitutional review burden
        for future semantic epochs

# =====================================================
# CANONICAL DOCTRINE STATEMENT
# =====================================================

  canonical_doctrine_statement: >

    AfriRide records deterministic execution outcomes
    as immutable facts and prohibits semantic interpretation
    without explicit constitutional elevation.

# =====================================================
# FINAL ASSERTION
# =====================================================

  final_assertion: >

    Epoch 8 formally establishes lawful observational evolution
    as the sole admissible path for declarative constitutional
    expansion within AfriRide’s deterministic governance model.

    Replay remains authoritative.

    Runtime remains sealed.

    Governance remains descriptive.

    Semantic interpretation remains constitutionally isolated.

    No execution semantics are expanded.

    No replay authority is weakened.

    No equivalence-space is activated.

    Historical execution truth remains immutable.

    Observe → Prove → Replay → Declare.

epoch_id: 6

  id: correction_2026_05_reseal
  type: CONSTITUTIONAL_BOOKKEEPING
  status: FINAL
  immutable: true

  detected_at: "2026-05-03T04:42:00Z"

  affects_epochs:
    - 1
    - 2
    - 3
  registry_identity: true
  runtime_execution: false
  governance_rules: false

# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ------------------------------------------------------------

  A constitutional bookkeeping inconsistency was identified where
  epochs 1–3 were marked FINAL without explicit reseal metadata,
  despite governance rules requiring reseal_after_advance.
  This correction records the remediation that restored consistency
  between declared epoch finality, registry sealing, and cryptographic
  identity attestation.

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# ACTIONS TAKEN
# ------------------------------------------------------------
actions_taken:
  - >
    Added explicit reseal metadata to epoch history records
    (resealed: true, seal_status: SEALED)
  - >
    Recomputed the registry attestation hash from the canonical
    pre-seal registry snapshot
  - >
    Reapplied registry seal using sovereignty tooling

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# ACTIONS NOT TAKEN
# ------------------------------------------------------------
non_actions:
  - No epoch counters were advanced
  - No law or invariant definitions were modified
  - No runtime, guard, or kernel behavior changed
  - No authority boundaries were altered

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# CONSTITUTIONAL ASSESSMENT
# ------------------------------------------------------------
constitutional_assessment:
  law_changed: false
  epoch_advanced: false
  runtime_affected: false
  authority_modified: false
  replay_semantics_changed: false

# ------------------------------------------------------------

  reseal_method: afritech.registry.sovereignty.seal_registry

  runtime_boot_verified: true
  ci_validation_passed: true

  tooling:
    - afritech/registry/sovereignty.py

# CONSTITUTIONAL ASSERTIONS
# ------------------------------------------------------------
constitutional_assertions:
  - This correction is non-temporal and does not constitute an epoch
  - Identity-domain corrections must not advance epoch counters
  - Registry reseal is required to restore cryptographic truthfulness
  - Replay validity requires sealed history continuity

# ------------------------------------------------------------
audit_notes: >
  This record exists to preserve long-term traceability of
  identity corrections that are orthogonal to temporal evolution.

  Future audits must treat this correction as a baseline identity
  normalization event, not a governance action.

    - no_reflection

# VALIDATION RULES
# ============================================================

validation:

  required:

    - alias_must_be_filesystem_path
    - resolved_targets_must_exist
    - deterministic_resolution_required

  forbidden:

    - ambiguous_resolution
    - multi-branch_resolution
    - runtime_dynamic_aliasing
    - alias_chains

  failure_mode: FAIL_FAST


# ============================================================
# CLOSED-WORLD SEMANTICS
# ============================================================

closed_world:

  enforced: true

  description: >
    Only declared aliases are valid. No implicit or
    dynamically discovered surfaces are allowed.


# ============================================================
# CONSTITUTIONAL ASSERTION
# ============================================================

constitutional_assertion: >

  Surface aliases are deterministic compatibility mappings only.

  Canonical surface authority derives exclusively from:
    - registered canonical artifacts
    - attested registry state
    - deterministic replay-safe resolution

  Filesystem aliases must never:
    - define execution authority
    - override canonical registry identity
    - introduce ambiguity
    - depend on runtime resolution


===== ./afritech/replay/ci/ADMISSION_REQUIRED.yaml =====
## ============================================================
## AfriTech CI Rule
## Runtime Admission Enforcement
## ============================================================
## Rule ID: CI-RUNTIME-ADMISSION-001
## Purpose:
## Ensure that no runtime execution can occur without
## explicit constitutional admission via RuntimeCertificate.
##
## Scope:
## - afritech/runtime/main.py
## - afritech/runtime/admission/
##
## This rule is normative and enforced in CI.
## ============================================================

metadata:
  rule_id: CI-RUNTIME-ADMISSION-001
  rule_version: "1.0.0"
  applies_to:
    - Phase-1
    - Phase-2A
    - Phase-2B
  last_updated: "2026-05-08"

## ============================================================
## GOVERNANCE PRINCIPLE
## ============================================================

principle:
  statement: >
    No AfriTech runtime may exist or execute without
    successful constitutional admission via a valid
    RuntimeCertificate.

  rationale: >
    Runtime existence is not implicit. It must be explicitly
    granted through cryptographically verifiable admission.
    This prevents unauthorized execution, configuration drift,
    and non-attested runtime behavior.

  enforcement_mode: static_analysis_and_ci_execution
  failure_action: ci_fail

## ============================================================
## REQUIRED RUNTIME BEHAVIOR
## ============================================================

required_behavior:

  description: >
    The runtime entrypoint MUST invoke the
    RuntimeAdmissionEngine before any execution path is reachable.

  admission_call:

    required_file: afritech/runtime/main.py

    required_import:
      - 'from afritech\\.runtime\\.admission\\.admission_engine import RuntimeAdmissionEngine'

    required_invocation:
      - 'RuntimeAdmissionEngine\\('
      - 'admit\\('

    required_flow:
      description: >
        Admission MUST occur before any guarded or unguarded
        execution is invoked.

      ordering:
        first:
          - _admit_runtime
        before:
          - any_execution_call

## ============================================================
## PROHIBITED BEHAVIOR
## ============================================================

prohibited_behavior:

  description: >
    Any execution path that bypasses runtime admission
    is constitutionally invalid.

  forbidden_patterns:

    - direct_execution_without_admission
    - guard_execution_without_admission
    - runtime_boot_without_certificate_check

## ============================================================
## TARGETED FILES
## ============================================================

targets:

  runtime_entrypoint:
    path: afritech/runtime/main.py

  admission_engine:
    path: afritech/runtime/admission/admission_engine.py

## ============================================================
## CI VALIDATION CHECKS
## ============================================================

ci_checks:

  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # AE-R1: Ensure admission engine import exists
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: AE-R1

    description: >
      Verify that runtime entrypoint imports RuntimeAdmissionEngine.

    target: afritech/runtime/main.py

    pattern_required:
      - 'from afritech\\.runtime\\.admission\\.admission_engine import RuntimeAdmissionEngine'

    failure_message: >
      Runtime entrypoint does not import RuntimeAdmissionEngine.

  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # AE-R2: Ensure admission invocation exists
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: AE-R2

    description: >
      Verify that RuntimeAdmissionEngine is instantiated
      and admit() is invoked.

    target: afritech/runtime/main.py

    pattern_required:
      - 'RuntimeAdmissionEngine\\('
      - '\\.admit\\('

    failure_message: >
      Runtime entrypoint does not invoke admission engine.

  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # AE-R3: Ensure admission precedes execution
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: AE-R3

    description: >
      Verify that admission occurs before any execution call.

    target: afritech/runtime/main.py

    required_order:
      first: _admit_runtime
      before:
        - run_guarded
        - dispatch
        - executor

    failure_message: >
      Runtime admission does not precede execution logic.

  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # AE-R4: Ensure no direct execution without admission
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: AE-R4

    description: >
      Prevent direct execution bypassing admission.

    target: afritech/runtime/main.py

    pattern_forbidden:
      - 'run_guarded\\(.*\\)$'
      - 'dispatch\\('

    enforce_context: absence_of_admission_call

    failure_message: >
      Direct execution detected without prior admission.

  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # AE-R5: Certificate path enforcement
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: AE-R5

    description: >
      Ensure runtime references a RuntimeCertificate path.

    target: afritech/runtime/main.py

    pattern_required:
      - 'certificates/runtime_epoch_'

    failure_message: >
      Runtime does not reference a valid certificate path.

## ============================================================
## RUNTIME GUARANTEE (ASSERTION)
## ============================================================

runtime_assertion:

  statement: >
    Any runtime execution without prior admission MUST be treated
    as non-existent and constitutionally invalid.

  enforcement_effect:
    - execution_refused
    - runtime_invalidated
    - replay_rejected

## ============================================================
## CI OUTCOME
## ============================================================

ci_outcome:

  on_pass:
    result: success
    message: "Runtime admission enforcement passed."

  on_fail:
    result: failure
    message: >
      Runtime violates constitutional admission requirements.
      See CI logs for specific violations.


===== ./afritech/replay/ci/ATTESTATION_BINDING_ENFORCEMENT.yaml =====
## ============================================================
## AfriTech CI Rule
## Attestation ↔ Certificate Binding Enforcement
## ============================================================
## Rule ID: CI-ATTEST-BIND-001
## Purpose:
## Ensure that RuntimeCertificates are strictly bound to
## the current attested constitutional state.
##
## This rule guarantees:
## - No drift between attestation and runtime
## - No stale certificate usage
## - No inconsistent system identity
##
## Scope:
## - afritech/registry/attestation.yaml
## - afritech/proof/certificates/
##
## This rule is normative and enforced in CI.
## ============================================================

metadata:
  rule_id: CI-ATTEST-BIND-001
  rule_version: "1.0.0"
  applies_to:
    - Phase-1
    - Phase-2A
    - Phase-2B
  last_updated: "2026-05-08"

## ============================================================
## GOVERNANCE PRINCIPLE
## ============================================================

principle:

  statement: >
    A RuntimeCertificate is valid ONLY if it is bound
    to the currently attested constitutional state.

  rationale: >
    Attestation defines the authoritative identity of the system.
    RuntimeCertificates derive their legitimacy from attestation.
    Any mismatch invalidates runtime legitimacy entirely.

  enforcement_mode: ci_execution
  failure_action: ci_fail


## ============================================================
## REQUIRED BINDING CONDITIONS
## ============================================================

binding_requirements:

  description: >
    The RuntimeCertificate MUST match the attestation
    across all constitutionally relevant hashes.

  required_alignments:

    - registry_hash
    - epoch_hash
    - kernel_root_hash
    - execution_surfaces_hash
    - authority_profiles_hash
    - replay_verifier_hash

  epoch_alignment_required: true
  attestation_status_required: SEALED


## ============================================================
## TARGETED FILES
## ============================================================

targets:

  attestation:
    path: afritech/registry/attestation.yaml

  certificates:
    path: afritech/proof/certificates/
    pattern: "*.cert"


## ============================================================
## CI VALIDATION CHECKS
## ============================================================

ci_checks:

  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # AB-F1: Attestation must exist
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: AB-F1

    description: >
      Verify that attestation.yaml exists.

    target: afritech/registry/attestation.yaml

    must_exist: true

    failure_message: >
      Missing attestation.yaml — constitutional state undefined.


  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # AB-F2: Attestation must be SEALED
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: AB-F2

    description: >
      Verify attestation is sealed.

    target: afritech/registry/attestation.yaml

    required_field:
      path: attestation.status
      value: SEALED

    failure_message: >
      Attestation is not SEALED — certificate invalid.


  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # AB-F3: Certificate ↔ Attestation hash match
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: AB-F3

    description: >
      Verify all certificate bindings match attestation bindings.

    enforcement: semantic_validation

    validation_method:
      type: python_hook
      function: validate_attestation_certificate_binding

    failure_message: >
      RuntimeCertificate does not match attestation hashes.


  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # AB-F4: Epoch consistency
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: AB-F4

    description: >
      Verify certificate epoch matches attestation epoch.

    target_pattern: "afritech/proof/certificates/*.cert"

    compare_fields:

      - attestation.epoch
      - runtime_certificate.epoch

    failure_message: >
      Certificate epoch does not match attested epoch.


  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # AB-F5: Prevent stale certificate usage
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: AB-F5

    description: >
      Ensure certificate issued_at >= attestation issued_at.

    enforcement: semantic_validation

    validation_method:
      type: python_hook
      function: validate_certificate_freshness

    failure_message: >
      Certificate predates attestation — stale certificate detected.


  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # AB-F6: Attestation hash binding must exist in certificate
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: AB-F6

    description: >
      Ensure certificate explicitly references attestation.

    target_pattern: "afritech/proof/certificates/*.cert"

    required_fields:
      - runtime_certificate.constitutional_binding.attestation_hash

    failure_message: >
      Certificate missing attestation binding.


  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # AB-F7: Prevent orphan certificates
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: AB-F7

    description: >
      Ensure no certificate exists without matching attestation.

    enforcement: semantic_validation

    validation_method:
      type: python_hook
      function: detect_orphan_certificates

    failure_message: >
      Orphan RuntimeCertificate detected.


## ============================================================
## VALIDATION FUNCTIONS (REFERENCE)
## ============================================================

validation_contract:

  validate_attestation_certificate_binding:

    description: >
      Compare attestation.bindings with
      certificate.constitutional_binding.

    expected_result: >
      Exact match across all binding fields.


  validate_certificate_freshness:

    description: >
      Ensure:
        certificate.issued_at >= attestation.issued_at

    expected_result: >
      Certificate must not predate attestation.


  detect_orphan_certificates:

    description: >
      Ensure every certificate references an existing
      attestation and matching epoch.

    expected_result: >
      No orphan certificates exist.


## ============================================================
## BINDING INVARIANT
## ============================================================

binding_invariant:

  statement: >
    Runtime existence is derived from attestation.

    Therefore:
      certificate MUST match attestation exactly.

  violation_effect:

    - runtime_invalidated
    - certificate_invalidated
    - execution_refused
    - replay_invalidated
    - trust_chain_broken


## ============================================================
## CI OUTCOME
## ============================================================

ci_outcome:

  on_pass:
    result: success
    message: "Attestation binding validation passed."

  on_fail:
    result: failure
    message: >
      RuntimeCertificate is not correctly bound to
      attested constitutional state. Execution is forbidden.

===== ./afritech/replay/ci/AUDIT_EMISSION_ENFORCEMENT.yaml =====
# ============================================================
# Afritech CI Rule
# Verifier Audit Emission Enforcement
# ============================================================
#
# Rule ID: CI-REPLAY-AUDIT-001
#
# Purpose:
#   Ensure that every replay verifier run emits a JSON audit
#   artifact via the audit side-channel.
#
# Scope:
#   Phase-2B (and later)
#
# This rule is normative and enforced in CI.
# ============================================================

metadata:
  rule_id: CI-REPLAY-AUDIT-001
  rule_version: "1.0.0"
  applies_to:
    - Phase-2B
  last_updated: "2026-05-05"

# ============================================================
# GOVERNANCE PRINCIPLE
# ============================================================

principle:

  statement: >
    Every invocation of the replay verifier MUST result in the
    emission of a machine-readable audit artifact, regardless
    of replay acceptance or refusal.

  rationale: >
    Audit artifacts provide an immutable, non-evidentiary record
    of verifier behavior for CI, compliance, and archival purposes,
    without contaminating stdout-based runtime evidence.

  enforcement_mode: static_analysis_and_ci_execution
  failure_action: ci_fail

# ============================================================
# REQUIRED AUDIT BEHAVIOR
# ============================================================

required_behavior:

  description: >
    The replay verification workflow MUST call the canonical
    audit export function exactly once per verifier run.

  audit_emission:
    function: export_verifier_audit
    module: afritech.replay.audit.export

  emission_timing:
    description: >
      Audit emission MUST occur after verifier execution and
      MUST reflect the final ReplayVerdict.

# ============================================================
# TARGETED FILES
# ============================================================

targets:

  cli_entrypoint:
    path: afritech/replay/run_verify.py

  audit_export_module:
    path: afritech/replay/audit/export.py

# ============================================================
# CI VALIDATION CHECKS
# ============================================================

ci_checks:

  - check_id: AE-F1
    description: >
      Verify that run_verify.py imports the audit export function.
    target: afritech/replay/run_verify.py
    pattern_required:
      - 'from afritech\\.replay\\.audit\\.export import export_verifier_audit'
    failure_message: >
      Replay verifier CLI does not import audit export function.

  - check_id: AE-F2
    description: >
      Verify that export_verifier_audit is invoked in the
      replay verification execution path.
    target: afritech/replay/run_verify.py
    pattern_required:
      - 'export_verifier_audit\\('
    failure_message: >
      Replay verifier run does not emit an audit artifact.

  - check_id: AE-F3
    description: >
      Verify audit emission is not routed to stdout.
    target: afritech/replay/audit/export.py
    pattern_forbidden:
      - 'print\\('
      - 'sys\\.stdout'
    failure_message: >
      Audit export must not write to stdout.

  - check_id: AE-F4
    description: >
      Verify that audit export writes JSON files only.
    target: afritech/replay/audit/export.py
    pattern_required:
      - 'json.dumps'
    failure_message: >
      Audit export does not produce canonical JSON output.

# ============================================================
# CI OUTCOME
# ============================================================

ci_outcome:

  on_pass:
    result: success
    message: "All replay verifier runs emit audit artifacts."

  on_fail:
    result: failure
    message: >
      Replay verifier run missing mandatory audit emission.
      See CI logs for details on the specific violation.
