===== ./afritech/replay/ci/AUTHORITY_BEFORE_INFERENCE_ENFORCEMENT.yaml =====
# ============================================================
# Afritech CI Rule
# Authority Isolation Must Precede Inference Validation
# ============================================================
#
# Rule ID: CI-REPLAY-AUTH-ORDER-001
#
# Purpose:
#   Ensure that authority isolation is enforced BEFORE any
#   inference binding validation occurs in the replay verifier.
#
# Scope:
#   Phase-2B (applies transitively to Phase-2A)
#
# This rule is normative and enforced in CI.
# ============================================================

metadata:
  rule_id: CI-REPLAY-AUTH-ORDER-001
  rule_version: "1.0.0"
  applies_to:
    - Phase-2A
    - Phase-2B
  last_updated: "2026-05-05"

# ============================================================
# GOVERNANCE PRINCIPLE
# ============================================================

principle:

  statement: >
    Authority isolation is a foundational replay invariant and
    MUST be enforced before any inference-related validation.
    Inference validation MUST NOT occur across authority domains.

  rationale: >
    Inference binding has meaning only within a single authority-
    scoped replay domain. Validating inference prior to authority
    isolation risks cross-authority contamination.

  enforcement_mode: static_analysis
  failure_action: ci_fail

# ============================================================
# CANONICAL ORDER REQUIREMENT
# ============================================================

required_validation_order:

  description: >
    The replay verifier MUST validate authority isolation
    before validating inference bindings.

  required_sequence:
    - _validate_authority
    - _validate_environment
    - _validate_request
    - _validate_inference_binding

  forbidden_sequences:
    - inference_validation_before_authority
    - inference_validation_without_authority_validation

# ============================================================
# TARGETED FILES
# ============================================================

targets:

  verifier:
    path: afritech/replay/verify.py

# ============================================================
# CI VALIDATION CHECKS
# ============================================================

ci_checks:

  - check_id: AO-F1
    description: >
      Verify that _validate_authority is invoked before
      _validate_inference_binding in verify().
    target: afritech/replay/verify.py
    required_order:
      first: _validate_authority
      before: _validate_inference_binding
    failure_message: >
      Authority validation must occur before inference validation.

  - check_id: AO-F2
    description: >
      Verify that inference binding validation is not reachable
      unless authority validation has already executed.
    target: afritech/replay/verify.py
    pattern_forbidden:
      - '_validate_inference_binding\\(.*\\).*_validate_authority'
    failure_message: >
      Inference validation appears reachable before authority validation.

  - check_id: AO-F3
    description: >
      Verify that no inference-related failure modes are emitted
      prior to authority mismatch handling.
    target: afritech/replay/verify.py
    forbidden_failure_modes_before_authority:
      - inference_input_mismatch
      - model_identity_mismatch
      - nondeterministic_inference
    failure_message: >
      Inference failure emitted before authority isolation.

# ============================================================
# CI OUTCOME
# ============================================================

ci_outcome:

  on_pass:
    result: success
    message: "Authority isolation precedes inference validation."

  on_fail:
    result: failure
    message: >
      Replay verifier violates authority-first governance ordering.

===== ./afritech/replay/ci/CERTIFICATE_SIGNATURE_VALIDATION.yaml =====
## ============================================================
## AfriTech CI Rule
## Runtime Certificate Signature Validation
## ============================================================
## Rule ID: CI-CERT-SIGNATURE-001
## Purpose:
## Ensure that every RuntimeCertificate is:
## - structurally valid
## - cryptographically signed
## - bound to the attested constitutional state
##
## Scope:
## - afritech/proof/certificates/
## - afritech/proof/runtime_certificate.py
##
## This rule is normative and enforced in CI.
## ============================================================

metadata:
  rule_id: CI-CERT-SIGNATURE-001
  rule_version: "1.0.0"
  applies_to:
    - Phase-1
    - Phase-2A
    - Phase-2B
  last_updated: "2026-05-08"

## ============================================================
## GOVERNANCE PRINCIPLE
## ============================================================

principle:
  statement: >
    No RuntimeCertificate may authorize runtime execution
    unless its signature, payload integrity, and constitutional
    bindings are cryptographically valid.

  rationale: >
    The RuntimeCertificate is the sole authorization artifact
    for runtime existence. If its integrity is not enforced,
    the entire constitutional model collapses.

  enforcement_mode: ci_execution
  failure_action: ci_fail

## ============================================================
## REQUIRED CERTIFICATE PROPERTIES
## ============================================================

required_properties:

  description: >
    Every RuntimeCertificate MUST satisfy all structural,
    cryptographic, and binding constraints prior to acceptance.

  structural_requirements:

    required_fields:
      - certificate_id
      - issued_at
      - epoch
      - constitutional_binding
      - runtime_identity
      - admission_guarantees
      - execution_scope
      - replay_constraints
      - signature

  cryptographic_requirements:

    signature_required: true
    payload_hash_required: true
    certificate_root_required: true

  binding_requirements:

    - registry_hash_present
    - epoch_hash_present
    - kernel_root_hash_present
    - execution_surfaces_hash_present
    - authority_profiles_hash_present
    - replay_verifier_hash_present

## ============================================================
## TARGETED FILES
## ============================================================

targets:

  certificate_directory:
    path: afritech/proof/certificates
    pattern: "*.cert"

  certificate_handler:
    path: afritech/proof/runtime_certificate.py

## ============================================================
## CI VALIDATION CHECKS
## ============================================================

ci_checks:

  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # CS-F1: Ensure certificate exists
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: CS-F1

    description: >
      Verify that at least one RuntimeCertificate exists.

    target_directory: afritech/proof/certificates
    minimum_files: 1

    failure_message: >
      No RuntimeCertificate found. Runtime cannot be admitted.

  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # CS-F2: Validate certificate structure
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: CS-F2

    description: >
      Ensure certificate contains all required top-level fields.

    target_pattern: "afritech/proof/certificates/*.cert"

    required_fields:
      - runtime_certificate.certificate_id
      - runtime_certificate.epoch
      - runtime_certificate.constitutional_binding
      - runtime_certificate.runtime_identity
      - runtime_certificate.signature

    failure_message: >
      RuntimeCertificate missing required fields.

  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # CS-F3: Validate signature fields present
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: CS-F3

    description: >
      Ensure signature fields exist and are not placeholders.

    target_pattern: "afritech/proof/certificates/*.cert"

    required_fields:
      - runtime_certificate.signature.payload_hash
      - runtime_certificate.signature.signature
      - runtime_certificate.signature.certificate_root

    forbidden_values:
      - "<SHA256(canonical serialization)>"
      - "<CRYPTOGRAPHIC_SIGNATURE>"
      - "<RUNTIME_ROOT_PUBLIC_KEY_HASH>"

    failure_message: >
      RuntimeCertificate contains unresolved or placeholder signature fields.

  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # CS-F4: Payload hash integrity
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: CS-F4

    description: >
      Validate that payload_hash matches canonical serialization.

    enforcement: semantic_validation

    validation_method:
      type: python_hook
      function: validate_certificate_payload_hash

    failure_message: >
      RuntimeCertificate payload_hash does not match serialized content.

  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # CS-F5: Signature verification
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: CS-F5

    description: >
      Verify cryptographic signature against certificate_root.

    enforcement: semantic_validation

    validation_method:
      type: python_hook
      function: verify_certificate_signature

    failure_message: >
      RuntimeCertificate signature verification failed.

  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # CS-F6: Binding consistency check
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: CS-F6

    description: >
      Ensure certificate binding matches actual system state.

    enforcement: semantic_validation

    validation_method:
      type: python_hook
      function: validate_constitutional_binding

    failure_message: >
      RuntimeCertificate does not match registry, epoch, or surfaces.

  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # CS-F7: Prevent unsigned certificate execution
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: CS-F7

    description: >
      Ensure runtime_certificate.py enforces signature verification.

    target: afritech/proof/runtime_certificate.py

    pattern_required:
      - 'verify_signature'
      - 'validate_payload_hash'

    failure_message: >
      Certificate handler does not enforce cryptographic validation.

## ============================================================
## VALIDATION FUNCTIONS (REFERENCE CONTRACT)
## ============================================================

validation_contract:

  validate_certificate_payload_hash:

    description: >
      Canonically serialize certificate fields defined in
      signature_scope and compute SHA256 hash.

    expected_result: >
      Computed hash must equal signature.payload_hash.

  verify_certificate_signature:

    description: >
      Verify signature using certificate_root public key.

    expected_result: >
      Signature MUST validate against payload_hash.

  validate_constitutional_binding:

    description: >
      Compare binding hashes against actual files:
      - registry.yaml
      - EXECUTION_SURFACES.yaml
      - authority_profiles.yaml

    expected_result: >
      All hashes MUST match.

## ============================================================
## RUNTIME GUARANTEE (ASSERTION)
## ============================================================

runtime_assertion:

  statement: >
    No RuntimeCertificate with invalid signature,
    mismatched payload_hash, or inconsistent binding
    MAY authorize runtime execution.

  enforcement_effect:
    - runtime_invalidated
    - execution_refused
    - replay_rejected
    - attestation_chain_broken

## ============================================================
## CI OUTCOME
## ============================================================

ci_outcome:

  on_pass:
    result: success
    message: "RuntimeCertificate validation passed."

  on_fail:
    result: failure
    message: >
      RuntimeCertificate failed integrity or signature validation.
      Execution is constitutionally forbidden.
      See CI logs for details.


===== ./afritech/replay/ci/CERTIFICATE_VERIFICATION_ENFORCEMENT.yaml =====
## ============================================================
## AfriTech CI Rule
## Runtime Certificate Verification Enforcement
## ============================================================
## Rule ID: CI-CERT-VERIFY-001
## Purpose:
## Ensure that RuntimeCertificates are not only valid in CI,
## but also actively verified at runtime via enforced logic.
##
## Scope:
## - afritech/runtime/admission/admission_engine.py
## - afritech/proof/runtime_certificate.py
##
## This rule is normative and enforced in CI.
## ============================================================

metadata:
  rule_id: CI-CERT-VERIFY-001
  rule_version: "1.0.0"
  applies_to:
    - Phase-1
    - Phase-2A
    - Phase-2B
  last_updated: "2026-05-08"


## ============================================================
## GOVERNANCE PRINCIPLE
## ============================================================

principle:

  statement: >
    RuntimeCertificate validation MUST be actively enforced
    at runtime. Structural correctness alone is insufficient.

  rationale: >
    A valid certificate that is not verified during runtime
    admission represents a broken security model.
    Verification must be executed—not assumed.

  enforcement_mode: static_analysis
  failure_action: ci_fail


## ============================================================
## REQUIRED VERIFICATION BEHAVIOR
## ============================================================

required_behavior:

  description: >
    The runtime must perform explicit verification of:
      - payload_hash integrity
      - cryptographic signature validity
      - constitutional binding consistency

  required_functions:

    - verify_signature
    - validate_payload_hash
    - validate_constitutional_binding

  enforcement_location:

    admission_engine:
      path: afritech/runtime/admission/admission_engine.py

    certificate_handler:
      path: afritech/proof/runtime_certificate.py


## ============================================================
## TARGETED FILES
## ============================================================

targets:

  admission_engine:
    path: afritech/runtime/admission/admission_engine.py

  certificate_handler:
    path: afritech/proof/runtime_certificate.py


## ============================================================
## CI VALIDATION CHECKS
## ============================================================

ci_checks:

  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # CV-F1: Ensure signature verification exists
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: CV-F1

    description: >
      Verify that cryptographic signature validation logic is implemented.

    targets:
      - afritech/runtime/admission/admission_engine.py
      - afritech/proof/runtime_certificate.py

    pattern_required:
      - 'verify_signature'
      - 'signature'
      - 'certificate_root'

    failure_message: >
      Signature verification logic is missing or incomplete.


  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # CV-F2: Ensure payload hash validation exists
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: CV-F2

    description: >
      Verify that certificate payload hash integrity is validated.

    targets:
      - afritech/runtime/admission/admission_engine.py
      - afritech/proof/runtime_certificate.py

    pattern_required:
      - 'payload_hash'
      - 'compute_sha256'
      - 'validate_payload'

    failure_message: >
      Certificate payload hash validation is missing.


  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # CV-F3: Ensure binding validation logic exists
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: CV-F3

    description: >
      Ensure that constitutional binding hashes are checked
      against actual system files.

    target: afritech/runtime/admission/admission_engine.py

    pattern_required:
      - '_validate_constitutional_binding'
      - 'registry_hash'
      - 'epoch_hash'
      - 'execution_surfaces_hash'

    failure_message: >
      Constitutional binding validation is incomplete.


  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # CV-F4: Ensure verification occurs BEFORE admission succeeds
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: CV-F4

    description: >
      Ensure that verification is executed before admission returns success.

    target: afritech/runtime/admission/admission_engine.py

    required_order:
      sequence:
        - _validate_signature
        - _validate_constitutional_binding
        - _validate_admission_guarantees

    failure_message: >
      Verification steps are not executed in required order.


  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # CV-F5: Prevent bypass of verification
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: CV-F5

    description: >
      Ensure that admission cannot succeed without running verification.

    target: afritech/runtime/admission/admission_engine.py

    pattern_forbidden:
      - 'return True$'

    enforce_context: absence_of_validation_calls

    failure_message: >
      Admission may return success without verification.


## ============================================================
## VERIFICATION INVARIANT
## ============================================================

verification_invariant:

  statement: >
    A RuntimeCertificate is valid ONLY if:
      - payload integrity is verified
      - signature is cryptographically confirmed
      - constitutional bindings are consistent

  violation_effect:

    - runtime_invalidated
    - execution_refused
    - replay_rejected
    - certificate_rejected


## ============================================================
## CI OUTCOME
## ============================================================

ci_outcome:

  on_pass:
    result: success
    message: "Runtime certificate verification enforcement passed."

  on_fail:
    result: failure
    message: >
      Runtime certificate verification is incomplete or bypassed.
      Execution is constitutionally invalid.

===== ./afritech/replay/ci/FAILURE_TAXONOMY_ENFORCEMENT.yaml =====
# ============================================================
# Afritech CI Rule
# Failure Taxonomy Enforcement
# ============================================================
#
# Rule ID: CI-REPLAY-FAIL-001
#
# Purpose:
#   Ensure that *every* replay verifier failure is mapped to
#   the canonical failure taxonomy.
#
# Scope:
#   - afritech/replay/verify.py
#   - afritech/replay/failures.py
#
# This rule is normative and enforced in CI.
# ============================================================

metadata:
  rule_id: CI-REPLAY-FAIL-001
  rule_version: "1.0.0"
  applies_to:
    - Phase-1
    - Phase-2A
    - Phase-2B
  last_updated: "2026-05-05"

# ============================================================
# ENFORCEMENT PRINCIPLE
# ============================================================

principle:

  statement: >
    The replay verifier MUST NOT emit any failure that is not
    explicitly defined in the canonical failure taxonomy.

  enforcement_mode: static_analysis
  failure_action: ci_fail

# ============================================================
# CANONICAL SOURCES
# ============================================================

canonical_sources:

  failure_definitions:
    path: afritech/replay/failures.py
    required_items:
      - ReplayFailureMode
      - ReplayInvariant
      - DivergenceLocation

  failure_taxonomy_doc:
    path: afritech/replay/docs/FAILURE_TAXONOMY.yaml

# ============================================================
# REQUIRED VERIFIER CONTRACT
# ============================================================

verifier_contract:

  allowed_failure_emission:

    description: >
      Replay verifier code MAY ONLY construct ReplayFailure
      instances using values sourced from ReplayFailureMode,
      ReplayInvariant, and DivergenceLocation enums.

    disallowed_patterns:
      - string literal failure modes
      - ad-hoc invariant strings
      - ad-hoc divergence locations

  required_construction_pattern:

    python:
      allowed:
        - ReplayFailure(
            ReplayFailureMode.<ENUM>,
            ReplayInvariant.<ENUM>,
            DivergenceLocation.<ENUM>,
            <details>
          )

      forbidden:
        - ReplayFailure("...", "...", "...", "...")

# ============================================================
# CI VALIDATION CHECKS
# ============================================================

ci_checks:

  - check_id: CT-F1
    description: >
      Verify that verify.py imports ReplayFailureMode,
      ReplayInvariant, and DivergenceLocation.
    target: afritech/replay/verify.py
    failure_message: >
      Verifier does not import canonical failure enums.

  - check_id: CT-F2
    description: >
      Verify that verify.py does not construct ReplayFailure
      with string literals.
    pattern_forbidden:
      - 'ReplayFailure\(\s*"[a-zA-Z_]+"'
    target: afritech/replay/verify.py
    failure_message: >
      Verifier constructs ReplayFailure using string literals.

  - check_id: CT-F3
    description: >
      Verify that every ReplayFailureMode enum appears in
      FAILURE_TAXONOMY.yaml.
    target:
      - afritech/replay/failures.py
      - afritech/replay/docs/FAILURE_TAXONOMY.yaml
    failure_message: >
      Failure mode missing from canonical taxonomy document.

  - check_id: CT-F4
    description: >
      Verify no failure modes appear in taxonomy that are not
      defined in ReplayFailureMode.
    target:
      - afritech/replay/failures.py
      - afritech/replay/docs/FAILURE_TAXONOMY.yaml
    failure_message: >
      Taxonomy references undefined failure mode.

# ============================================================
# CI OUTCOME
# ============================================================

ci_outcome:

  on_pass:
    result: success
    message: "Replay failure taxonomy enforcement passed."

  on_fail:
    result: failure
    message: >
      Replay verifier failure semantics violate canonical taxonomy.
      See CI logs for details on the specific violation.

===== ./afritech/replay/ci/INFRASTRUCTURE_ENFORCEMENT.yaml =====
## ============================================================
## AfriTech CI Rule
## Infrastructure Non-Interference Enforcement
## ============================================================
## Rule ID: CI-INFRA-ENFORCE-001
## Purpose:
## Ensure infrastructure surfaces remain strictly
## non-constitutional and cannot influence runtime execution.
##
## Scope:
## - afritech/docker/
## - .github/workflows/
## - environment configs
##
## ============================================================

metadata:
  rule_id: CI-INFRA-ENFORCE-001
  rule_version: "1.0.0"
  applies_to:
    - Phase-2B
  last_updated: "2026-05-08"

# ============================================================
# PRINCIPLE
# ============================================================

principle:

  statement: >
    Infrastructure MUST NOT influence runtime execution,
    replay outcomes, or constitutional validity.

  enforcement_mode: static_analysis
  failure_action: ci_fail


# ============================================================
# TARGETS
# ============================================================

targets:

  infrastructure_dirs:

    - afritech/docker/
    - .github/workflows/

  runtime_dirs:

    - afritech/runtime/
    - afritech/inference/
    - afritech/replay/


# ============================================================
# CORE RULES
# ============================================================

rules:

  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # INF-1: No infrastructure imports in runtime
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: INF-1

    description: >
      Runtime must not import infrastructure modules.

    target_dirs: 
      - afritech/runtime/
      - afritech/inference/

    forbidden_patterns:

      - "docker"
      - "os\\.environ"
      - "subprocess"
      - "dotenv"

    failure_message: >
      Runtime depends on infrastructure or environment.


  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # INF-2: No environment-driven execution
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: INF-2

    description: >
      Prevent execution logic based on environment variables.

    target_dirs:
      - afritech/runtime/
      - afritech/inference/

    forbidden_patterns:

      - "os\\.getenv"
      - "os\\.environ\\["
      - "env\\."

    failure_message: >
      Environment-based execution detected.


  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # INF-3: No infrastructure paths in registry/certificate
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: INF-3

    description: >
      Infrastructure must not appear in constitutional bindings.

    target_files:

      - afritech/registry/registry.yaml
      - afritech/registry/attestation.yaml
      - afritech/proof/certificates/*.cert

    forbidden_patterns:

      - "docker"
      - ".github"
      - "workflow"

    failure_message: >
      Infrastructure detected in constitutional binding.


  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # INF-4: Replay determinism enforcement
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: INF-4

    description: >
      Ensure infrastructure cannot affect replay output.

    target_dirs:

      - afritech/runtime/

    forbidden_patterns:

      - "time\\."
      - "random\\."
      - "uuid\\."
      - "datetime\\.now"

    failure_message: >
      Non-deterministic dependency detected.


  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # INF-5: No execution logic inside infrastructure
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: INF-5

    description: >
      Infrastructure files must not contain runtime logic.

    target_dirs:

      - afritech/docker/
      - .github/workflows/

    forbidden_patterns:

      - "def run"
      - "execute"
      - "engine"

    failure_message: >
      Execution logic found in infrastructure.


# ============================================================
# RUNTIME ASSERTION
# ============================================================

runtime_assertion:

  statement: >
    Runtime execution must be fully independent
    from all infrastructure layers.

  violations:

    - runtime_invalidated
    - replay_invalidated
    - certificate_rejected


# ============================================================
# CI OUTCOME
# ============================================================

ci_outcome:

  on_pass:
    result: success
    message: "Infrastructure isolation verified."

  on_fail:
    result: failure
    message: >
      Infrastructure is influencing execution.
      This violates constitutional invariants.

===== ./afritech/replay/ci/SURFACE_VALIDATION_ENFORCEMENT.yaml =====
## ============================================================
## AfriTech CI Rule
## Surface Registry Validation Enforcement
## ============================================================
## Rule ID: CI-SURFACE-VALIDATION-001
## Purpose:
## Enforce that all system surfaces are explicitly declared
## in surface_registry.yaml and comply with their classification.
##
## This rule guarantees:
## - No undeclared execution surfaces
## - No invalid executable flags
## - No rogue or hidden system files
##
## Scope:
## - Entire afritech/ system tree
##
## ============================================================

metadata:
  rule_id: CI-SURFACE-VALIDATION-001
  rule_version: "1.0.0"
  applies_to:
    - Phase-2B
  last_updated: "2026-05-08"

# ============================================================
# PRINCIPLE
# ============================================================

principle:

  statement: >
    Only surfaces explicitly declared in surface_registry.yaml
    may exist, execute, or participate in the system.

  rationale: >
    Undeclared surfaces represent ungoverned computation paths,
    violating constitutional guarantees.

  enforcement_mode: static_analysis
  failure_action: ci_fail

# ============================================================
# TARGETS
# ============================================================

targets:

  registry:
    path: afritech/governance/surface_registry.yaml

  system_root:
    path: afritech/

# ============================================================
# CORE VALIDATION RULES
# ============================================================

rules:

  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # SV-1: All surfaces must be declared
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: SV-1

    description: >
      Every top-level directory and file in afritech/
      must be declared in surface_registry.yaml.

    validation_method:
      type: python_hook
      function: validate_all_surfaces_declared

    failure_message: >
      Undeclared surface detected in repository.


  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # SV-2: Executable surfaces must be explicitly marked
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: SV-2

    description: >
      Any file or directory containing executable code
      must have executable: true.

    validation_method:
      type: python_hook
      function: validate_executable_flag

    failure_message: >
      Executable surface is not properly declared.


  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # SV-3: Non-executable surfaces must not contain logic
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: SV-3

    description: >
      Surfaces marked executable: false must not contain
      Python execution logic.

    target_patterns:
      - "*.py"

    validation_method:
      type: pattern_analysis

    forbidden_patterns:
      - "def "
      - "class "
      - "import "

    failure_message: >
      Non-executable surface contains executable code.


  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # SV-4: Hash inclusion consistency
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: SV-4

    description: >
      Only surfaces marked hash_included: true may appear
      in attestation or certificate bindings.

    target_files:
      - afritech/registry/attestation.yaml
      - afritech/proof/certificates/*.cert

    validation_method:
      type: python_hook
      function: validate_hash_surface_membership

    failure_message: >
      Non-declared surface used in hash binding.


  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # SV-5: Infrastructure surfaces must be excluded
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: SV-5

    description: >
      NON_CONSTITUTIONAL surfaces must not:
        - be executable
        - be hashed
        - appear in bindings

    validation_method:
      type: python_hook
      function: validate_infrastructure_isolation

    failure_message: >
      Infrastructure surface violates isolation rules.


  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  # SV-6: Authority scope enforcement
  # ------------------------------------------------------------
  - check_id: SV-6

    description: >
      Executable surfaces must respect authority scope.

    validation_method:
      type: python_hook
      function: validate_surface_authority_scope

    failure_message: >
      Surface violates authority constraints.


# ============================================================
# VALIDATION CONTRACTS
# ============================================================

validation_contracts:

  validate_all_surfaces_declared:

    description: >
      Walk afritech/ directory tree and ensure each top-level
      directory or file is declared in surface_registry.

    expected_result: >
      No undeclared surfaces.


  validate_executable_flag:

    description: >
      Ensure all .py files in execution paths are declared
      with executable: true.

    expected_result: >
      All executable files correctly declared.


  validate_hash_surface_membership:

    description: >
      Compare attestation bindings with surface_registry entries.

    expected_result: >
      All hashed surfaces must have hash_included: true.


  validate_infrastructure_isolation:

    description: >
      Ensure NON_CONSTITUTIONAL surfaces are excluded from:
        - executable surfaces
        - hash chains
        - authority scope

    expected_result: >
      Infrastructure fully isolated.


  validate_surface_authority_scope:

    description: >
      Ensure executable surfaces have valid authority_scope.

    expected_result: >
      authority_scope must be one of:
        - GLOBAL
        - GUARDED
        - AUTHORITY_BOUND
        - VALIDATION_ONLY

# ============================================================
# EXECUTION ASSERTION
# ============================================================

execution_assertion:

  statement: >
    Execution is only permitted for declared surfaces
    with executable: true and valid authority scope.

  violation_effect:

    - runtime_refused
    - replay_invalidated
    - constitutional_failure

# ============================================================
# CI OUTCOME
# ============================================================

ci_outcome:

  on_pass:
    result: success
    message: "Surface registry validation passed."

  on_fail:
    result: failure
    message: >
      Surface registry validation failed.
      Undeclared or unauthorized surfaces detected.

===== ./afritech/replay/docs/AUTHORITY_ISOLATED_REAL_INFERENCE_GOVERNANCE.yaml =====
# ============================================================
# Afritech Constitutional Replay Law
# Authority‑Isolated Real Inference Governance
# ============================================================
#
# Purpose:
#   Specify how authority isolation applies to real inference
#   under replay law (Phase‑2B).
#
# Scope:
#   Phase‑2B only
#
# This specification is normative.
# Authority isolation is enforced through deterministic refusal,
# not discretionary policy.
# ============================================================

metadata:
  spec_name: authority_isolated_real_inference_governance
  spec_version: "1.0.0"
  phase: Phase-2B
  last_updated: "2026-05-05"

# ============================================================
# DEFINITIONS
# ============================================================

definitions:

  authority_profile:
    description: >
      A canonical identifier representing the constitutional
      authority under which an inference is executed.

  real_inference:
    description: >
      An inference produced by an actual model invocation
      (local, remote, or hybrid) and bound into replay truth
      via an inference_binding object.

  replay_domain:
    description: >
      The closed validity space defined by an authority_profile.
      Replay artifacts MAY NOT cross replay domains.

# ============================================================
# GOVERNANCE PRINCIPLE
# ============================================================

governance_principle:

  statement: >
    All real inference executions are scoped to exactly one
    authority_profile, and replay validity is confined to
    that authority’s replay domain.

  enforcement_mechanism: deterministic_refusal
  enforcement_phase: Phase-2B

# ============================================================
# AUTHORITY BINDING REQUIREMENTS
# ============================================================

authority_binding_requirements:

  transcript_binding:
    description: >
      Every replay transcript that includes real inference
      MUST declare an authority_profile at the top level.
    failure_mode: missing_authority_binding

  inference_binding_inheritance:
    description: >
      The inference_binding object MUST inherit the
      transcript authority_profile implicitly and
      MUST NOT introduce a second authority identifier.
    failure_mode: authority_mismatch

# ============================================================
# REPLAY DOMAIN ISOLATION RULE
# ============================================================

replay_domain_isolation:

  rule_id: DR-2B-AUTH-ISO-001

  description: >
    A real inference transcript generated under authority X
    MUST be rejected when replay verification is attempted
    under authority Y ≠ X.

  enforcement:
    when: authority_mismatch
    action: deterministic_refusal

  failure_characteristics:
    failure_mode: authority_mismatch
    violated_invariant: isolated_replay_domains
    divergence_location: authority_binding

# ============================================================
# ACCEPTANCE CONDITION
# ============================================================

acceptance_condition:

  description: >
    Real inference replay MAY be accepted only when
    request authority exactly matches transcript authority.

  required_match:
    request.authority_profile: transcript.authority_profile

  outcome_on_match:
    status: REPLAY_VALID

  outcome_on_mismatch:
    status: REPLAY_INVALID

# ============================================================
# NON-DISCRETIONARY BEHAVIOR
# ============================================================

non_discretion:

  no_authority_coercion:
    description: >
      The verifier MUST NOT coerce, map, alias, or reinterpret
      authority identities during replay.

  no_cross_authority_import:
    description: >
      Inference bindings, outputs, or caches produced under
      one authority MUST NOT be reused across authorities.

# ============================================================
# EXPLICIT NON-GOALS
# ============================================================

non_goals:

  trust_equivalence:
    description: >
      This specification does not assume equivalence or
      compatibility between different authorities.

  semantic_authority_merging:
    description: >
      This specification does not permit authorities to be
      merged, grouped, or federated at replay time.

# ============================================================
# CONSTITUTIONAL GUARANTEE
# ============================================================

guarantee:

  statement: >
    Authority‑isolated real inference governance guarantees
    that no inference executed under one constitutional
    authority can be replay‑validated under another,
    regardless of model identity, inference determinism,
    or semantic equivalence.

  enforcement_location: replay_verifier
  enforcement_phase: Phase-2B

===== ./afritech/replay/docs/DETERMINISTIC_REPLAY_ACCEPTANCE.yaml =====
# ============================================================ Afritech Constitutional Replay Law
# Deterministic Replay Acceptance of Real Inference
# ============================================================
#
# Purpose:
#   Specify the exact conditions under which replay verification
#   MUST accept a transcript that includes a real inference binding.
#
# Scope:
#   Phase-2B only
#
# This specification is normative.
# Acceptance conditions are deterministic and non-discretionary.
# ============================================================

metadata:
  spec_name: deterministic_replay_acceptance
  spec_version: "1.0.0"
  phase: Phase-2B
  last_updated: "2026-05-05"

# ============================================================
# DEFINITIONS
# ============================================================

definitions:

  real_inference:
    description: >
      An inference produced by an actual model invocation
      (local or remote) and bound into replay truth via an
      inference_binding object.

  replay_acceptance:
    description: >
      A verifier outcome with status REPLAY_VALID, indicating that
      all constitutional replay invariants are satisfied.

  inference_binding:
    description: >
      A structured, immutable record capturing the relationship
      between inference input, inference output, and model identity.

# ============================================================
# PRECONDITIONS FOR ACCEPTANCE
# ============================================================

preconditions:

  transcript_exists:
    description: Transcript file must exist and be readable
    failure_mode: invalid_transcript_path

  transcript_schema_valid:
    description: Transcript schema must be complete
    failure_mode: invalid_transcript_schema

  authority_binding_valid:
    description: Request authority must match transcript authority
    failure_mode: authority_mismatch

  deterministic_environment:
    description: Replay environment must declare deterministic_mode = true
    failure_mode: environment_mismatch

# ============================================================
# INFERENCE BINDING REQUIREMENTS
# ============================================================

inference_binding_requirements:

  presence_required:
    description: >
      Any transcript claiming real inference MUST contain
      an inference_binding object.
    failure_mode: missing_inference_binding

  input_hash_binding:
    description: >
      inference_binding.input_hash MUST equal the canonical
      request hash.
    failure_mode: inference_input_mismatch

  model_identity_binding:
    description: >
      inference_binding.model_id and model_version MUST match
      replay_environment.model_id and model_version.
    failure_mode: model_identity_mismatch

# ============================================================
# DETERMINISTIC ACCEPTANCE RULE
# ============================================================

acceptance_rule:

  rule_id: DR-2B-ACCEPT-001
  description: >
    Replay verification MUST accept a transcript with real inference
    if and only if all acceptance invariants are satisfied.

  acceptance_conditions:
    - transcript_exists
    - transcript_schema_valid
    - authority_binding_valid
    - deterministic_environment
    - presence_required
    - input_hash_binding
    - model_identity_binding
    - truthpacket_identity
    - deterministic_identity

  outcome:
    status: REPLAY_VALID
    replay_hash: authoritative
    refusal_allowed: false

# ============================================================
# NON-DISCRETIONARY BEHAVIOR
# ============================================================

non_discretion:

  no_probabilistic_tolerance:
    description: >
      Replay acceptance MUST NOT depend on semantic similarity,
      approximate matching, or statistical closeness.

  refuse_on_any_violation:
    description: >
      Any violation of acceptance conditions MUST result in
      deterministic replay refusal.

# ============================================================
# EXPLICIT NON-GOALS
# ============================================================

non_goals:

  semantic_correctness:
    description: >
      This specification does not assert that model output
      is correct, helpful, or truthful.

  model_quality:
    description: >
      This specification does not evaluate model performance
      or intelligence.

  production_readiness:
    description: >
      This specification does not claim operational stability
      or deployment readiness.

# ============================================================
# CONSTITUTIONAL GUARANTEE
# ============================================================

guarantee:

  statement: >
    If a real inference transcript is accepted under this rule,
    replay law guarantees that the inference binding is authority-
    scoped, deterministic at the replay boundary, and immune to
    post-hoc reinterpretation.

  enforcement_location: replay_verifier
  enforcement_phase: Phase-2B



===== ./afritech/replay/docs/FAILURE_TAXONOMY.yaml =====
# ============================================================
# Afritech Constitutional Replay Failure Taxonomy
# ============================================================
#
# Purpose:
#   Canonical, machine-readable specification of all replay
#   failure modes, invariants, and divergence locations.
#
# Scope:
#   Phase-1  : Deterministic replay
#   Phase-2A : Authority-isolated replay domains
#   Phase-2B : Real inference binding under replay law
#
# Consumption:
#   - replay verifier
#   - audit tooling
#   - CI enforcement
#   - governance documentation
#
# This file is normative.
# Runtime code must NOT invent new failure strings.
# ============================================================

metadata:
  taxonomy_version: "1.0.0"
  last_updated: "2026-05-05"
  scope:
    - Phase-1
    - Phase-2A
    - Phase-2B

# ============================================================
# FAILURE MODES
# ============================================================

failure_modes:

  # -----------------------
  # Transcript / I/O
  # -----------------------

  invalid_transcript_path:
    phase: Phase-1
    summary: Transcript file not found or unreadable
    invariant: transcript_existence
    divergence_location: transcript_load

  invalid_transcript_schema:
    phase: Phase-1
    summary: Transcript missing required fields or malformed
    invariant: transcript_integrity
    divergence_location: transcript_schema

  # -----------------------
  # Authority (Phase-2A)
  # -----------------------

  missing_authority_binding:
    phase: Phase-2A
    summary: Transcript missing authority_profile
    invariant: authority_identity
    divergence_location: authority_binding

  authority_mismatch:
    phase: Phase-2A
    summary: Request authority does not match transcript authority
    invariant: isolated_replay_domains
    divergence_location: authority_binding

  # -----------------------
  # Environment
  # -----------------------

  environment_mismatch:
    phase: Phase-1
    summary: Replay environment does not satisfy deterministic constraints
    invariant: environment_identity
    divergence_location: environment_validation

  # -----------------------
  # Request / Trace
  # -----------------------

  request_mismatch:
    phase: Phase-1
    summary: Request hash differs from transcript request_hash
    invariant: request_identity
    divergence_location: request_reconstruction

  trace_divergence:
    phase: Phase-1
    summary: Deterministic execution trace mismatch
    invariant: causal_reconstruction
    divergence_location: execution_rerun

  # -----------------------
  # TruthPacket / Replay
  # -----------------------

  truthpacket_divergence:
    phase: Phase-1
    summary: Regenerated TruthPacket hash mismatch
    invariant: truthpacket_identity
    divergence_location: truthpacket_regeneration

  hash_mismatch:
    phase: Phase-1
    summary: Replay hash mismatch after recomputation
    invariant: deterministic_identity
    divergence_location: hash_recomputation

  # -----------------------
  # Inference Binding (Phase-2B)
  # -----------------------

  missing_inference_binding:
    phase: Phase-2B
    summary: Transcript does not contain inference binding
    invariant: inference_binding_required
    divergence_location: inference_binding

  inference_input_mismatch:
    phase: Phase-2B
    summary: Inference input hash does not match request
    invariant: deterministic_inference_binding
    divergence_location: inference_binding

  model_identity_mismatch:
    phase: Phase-2B
    summary: Model ID or version differs from replay environment
    invariant: model_identity
    divergence_location: inference_binding

  nondeterministic_inference:
    phase: Phase-2B
    summary: Inference output cannot be deterministically validated
    invariant: deterministic_inference
    divergence_location: inference_binding

# ============================================================
# INVARIANTS
# ============================================================

invariants:

  transcript_existence:
    phase: Phase-1
    description: Replay requires an existing transcript

  transcript_integrity:
    phase: Phase-1
    description: Transcript schema must be complete and valid

  request_identity:
    phase: Phase-1
    description: Request identity must be preserved across replay

  deterministic_identity:
    phase: Phase-1
    description: Replay output must be deterministic

  truthpacket_identity:
    phase: Phase-1
    description: TruthPacket must regenerate identically

  causal_reconstruction:
    phase: Phase-1
    description: Execution trace must replay exactly

  authority_identity:
    phase: Phase-2A
    description: Authority identity must be explicit

  isolated_replay_domains:
    phase: Phase-2A
    description: Replay domains must be authority-isolated

  inference_binding_required:
    phase: Phase-2B
    description: Real inference must be bound into replay truth

  deterministic_inference_binding:
    phase: Phase-2B
    description: Inference input must deterministically bind to request

  model_identity:
    phase: Phase-2B
    description: Replay must bind to a single model identity

  deterministic_inference:
    phase: Phase-2B
    description: Inference must be reproducible or deterministically refused

# ============================================================
# DIVERGENCE LOCATIONS
# ============================================================

divergence_locations:

  transcript_load:
    description: Transcript file access/loading

  transcript_schema:
    description: Transcript schema validation

  authority_binding:
    description: Authority identity validation

  environment_validation:
    description: Replay environment validation

  request_reconstruction:
    description: Request regeneration & hashing

  execution_rerun:
    description: Deterministic execution replay

  truthpacket_regeneration:
    description: TruthPacket reconstruction

  hash_recomputation:
    description: Final replay hash computation

  inference_binding:
    description: Real inference binding validation


===== ./afritech/replay/docs/FAILURE_TAXONOMY_PHASE_3.yaml =====
# ============================================================
# Afritech Constitutional Replay Failure Taxonomy
# Phase‑3 Extension — Multi‑Agent Governance
# ============================================================
#
# Purpose:
#   Extend the canonical replay failure taxonomy to support
#   Phase‑3 multi‑agent governance, arbitration, and coordination.
#
# Scope:
#   Phase‑3 only
#
# This file EXTENDS the base taxonomy defined in:
#   afritech/replay/docs/FAILURE_TAXONOMY.yaml
#
# No Phase‑3 failure may overlap or redefine earlier phases.
# ============================================================

metadata:
  taxonomy_extension: phase_3_multi_agent
  extension_version: "1.0.0"
  phase: Phase-3
  last_updated: "2026-05-05"

# ============================================================
# PHASE‑3 FAILURE MODES
# ============================================================

failure_modes:

  # ----------------------------------------------------------
  # Agent Identity & Registration
  # ----------------------------------------------------------

  unregistered_agent:
    phase: Phase-3
    summary: >
      An agent participated in execution but was not declared
      in the multi-agent registry.
    invariant: agent_identity
    divergence_location: agent_registry

  agent_identity_mismatch:
    phase: Phase-3
    summary: >
      Agent identifier in execution does not match declared
      agent identity or signature.
    invariant: agent_identity
    divergence_location: agent_binding

  # ----------------------------------------------------------
  # Authority Delegation
  # ----------------------------------------------------------

  unauthorized_agent_action:
    phase: Phase-3
    summary: >
      Agent performed an action outside its delegated authority.
    invariant: delegated_authority
    divergence_location: authority_delegation

  conflicting_authority_delegation:
    phase: Phase-3
    summary: >
      Multiple agents received overlapping or contradictory
      authority scopes.
    invariant: non_overlapping_delegation
    divergence_location: authority_delegation

  # ----------------------------------------------------------
  # Inter‑Agent Coordination
  # ----------------------------------------------------------

  coordination_protocol_violation:
    phase: Phase-3
    summary: >
      Agent interaction violated the declared coordination
      protocol or ordering rules.
    invariant: coordination_protocol
    divergence_location: coordination_layer

  message_order_violation:
    phase: Phase-3
    summary: >
      Inter-agent messages were replayed out of canonical order.
    invariant: causal_ordering
    divergence_location: coordination_layer

  # ----------------------------------------------------------
  # Arbitration & Conflict Resolution
  # ----------------------------------------------------------

  unresolved_agent_conflict:
    phase: Phase-3
    summary: >
      Conflicting agent outputs were detected without a valid
      arbitration outcome.
    invariant: arbitration_required
    divergence_location: arbitration_layer

  invalid_arbitration_decision:
    phase: Phase-3
    summary: >
      Arbitration result violates declared arbitration rules
      or authority hierarchy.
    invariant: arbitration_integrity
    divergence_location: arbitration_layer

  # ----------------------------------------------------------
  # Collective Determinism
  # ----------------------------------------------------------

  nondeterministic_multi_agent_execution:
    phase: Phase-3
    summary: >
      Collective agent execution cannot be deterministically
      reproduced under replay.
    invariant: collective_determinism
    divergence_location: execution_rerun

# ============================================================
# PHASE‑3 INVARIANTS
# ============================================================

invariants:

  agent_identity:
    description: >
      Every participating agent must have a unique,
      declared, and verifiable identity.

  delegated_authority:
    description: >
      Agents may act only within explicitly delegated
      authority scopes.

  non_overlapping_delegation:
    description: >
      Authority delegation between agents must not overlap
      or conflict unless explicitly allowed.

  coordination_protocol:
    description: >
      Agent coordination must obey declared protocols and
      sequencing rules.

  causal_ordering:
    description: >
      Inter-agent interactions must preserve causal order
      during replay.

  arbitration_required:
    description: >
      Conflicting agent outputs must be resolved through
      a valid arbitration process.

  arbitration_integrity:
    description: >
      Arbitration outcomes must be rule-compliant and
      authority-consistent.

  collective_determinism:
    description: >
      Multi-agent execution must be reproducible or
      deterministically refused.

# ============================================================
# PHASE‑3 DIVERGENCE LOCATIONS
# ============================================================

divergence_locations:

  agent_registry:
    description: >
      Agent declaration and registration stage.

  agent_binding:
    description: >
      Runtime agent identity binding.

  authority_delegation:
    description: >
      Delegation of authority scopes to agents.

  coordination_layer:
    description: >
      Inter-agent message passing and protocol enforcement.

  arbitration_layer:
    description: >
      Conflict resolution and arbitration processing.


===== ./afritech/replay/docs/PHASE_2B_EVIDENCE_HARNESS.yaml =====
# ============================================================
# Afritech Constitutional Evidence Harness
# Phase‑2B — Real Inference Binding Under Replay Law
# ============================================================
#
# Purpose:
#   Define the exact, constitutionally admissible procedure
#   for evidencing Phase‑2B enforcement.
#
# Scope:
#   Phase‑2B only
#
# This harness is normative.
# It specifies how evidence MUST be produced, presented,
# and evaluated. It does NOT assert ratification.
# ============================================================

metadata:
  harness_name: phase_2b_evidence_harness
  harness_version: "1.0.0"
  phase: Phase-2B
  last_updated: "2026-05-05"

# ============================================================
# CONSTITUTIONAL PRINCIPLES
# ============================================================

principles:

  evidence_precedes_judgment:
    description: >
      Runtime evidence MUST be presented before any claim
      of Phase‑2B acceptance or refusal is evaluated.

  stdout_is_evidence:
    description: >
      Shell stdout constitutes admissible runtime evidence.
      Side-channel audit files support CI and compliance,
      but do NOT substitute for stdout evidence.

  refusal_is_governance:
    description: >
      Phase‑2B enforcement is demonstrated by deterministic
      refusal as much as by acceptance.

# ============================================================
# REQUIRED PRECONDITIONS
# ============================================================

preconditions:

  phase_2a_frozen:
    description: >
      Phase‑2A MUST already be ratified and frozen prior
      to Phase‑2B evidence submission.

  real_inference_enabled:
    description: >
      Transcript generation MUST include an inference_binding
      object produced by a real or stubbed inference runtime.

# ============================================================
# EVIDENCE CLASSES
# ============================================================

evidence_classes:

  # ----------------------------------------------------------
  # E‑B1: Real Inference Transcript Generation
  # ----------------------------------------------------------

  EB1_real_inference_transcript:
    description: >
      Demonstrates that a real inference has been executed
      and bound into replay truth.

    command:
      shell: >
        python3 -m afritech.replay.generate
        <phase_2b_request.yaml>

    required_stdout_contains:
      - "Transcript written to"
    
    transcript_requirements:
      must_contain:
        - inference_binding
        - authority_profile
        - replay_environment.model_id
        - replay_environment.model_version

  # ----------------------------------------------------------
  # E‑B2: Deterministic Replay Acceptance
  # ----------------------------------------------------------

  EB2_replay_acceptance:
    description: >
      Demonstrates deterministic replay acceptance of a real
      inference under the same authority and model identity.

    command:
      shell: >
        python3 -m afritech.replay.run_verify
        <phase_2b_request.yaml>
        <phase_2b_transcript.yaml>

    required_stdout_exact:
      verdict: REPLAY_VALID

    required_fields:
      - REPLAY_HASH
      - FAILURE_MODE: null
      - VIOLATED_INVARIANT: null
      - DIVERGENCE_LOCATION: null

  # ----------------------------------------------------------
  # E‑B3: Deterministic Replay Refusal
  # ----------------------------------------------------------

  EB3_replay_refusal:
    description: >
      Demonstrates deterministic replay refusal when a
      constitutionally relevant invariant is violated.

    acceptable_variants:
      - model_identity_mismatch
      - inference_input_mismatch
      - authority_mismatch
      - nondeterministic_inference

    command:
      shell: >
        python3 -m afritech.replay.run_verify
        <modified_context>

    required_stdout_exact:
      verdict: REPLAY_INVALID

    required_fields:
      - FAILURE_MODE
      - VIOLATED_INVARIANT
      - DIVERGENCE_LOCATION

# ============================================================
# PRESENTATION RULES
# ============================================================

presentation_rules:

  standalone_submission:
    description: >
      Each evidence artifact MUST be presented as a standalone
      shell transcript, without surrounding interpretation.

  no_interleaved_evaluation:
    description: >
      No evaluative commentary or judgment is allowed in the
      same shell transcript as the evidence itself.

# ============================================================
# Afritech Constitutional Checklist

  # ----------------------------------------------------------

    description: >

    required_items:

        path: afritech/replay/docs/PHASE_2B_EVIDENCE_HARNESS.yaml

      harness_runner:

  # ----------------------------------------------------------


===== ./afritech/replay/transcript.yaml =====
# afritech/replay/transcript.yaml
#
# STATUS: CANONICAL REPLAY TRANSCRIPT SCHEMA
#
# This file defines the ONLY admissible replay transcript
# structure for proving constitutional execution during the
# FIRST_EXECUTABLE_PROOF phase.
#
# All replay verdicts are derived from artifacts conforming
# exactly to this schema.
#
# Any execution claim without a transcript matching THIS FILE
# is constitutionally void.

version: REPLAY_TRANSCRIPT_SCHEMA_V1

applicability:
  phase: FIRST_EXECUTABLE_PROOF
  governed_by:
    - CONSTITUTIONAL_RESEARCH_AGENT_SPEC
    - REPLAY_VERIFIER_SPEC
  enforced_by:
    - ReplayVerifier

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# GLOBAL TRANSCRIPT INVARIANTS
# -------------------------------------------------------------------

global_invariants:

  - id: TRANSCRIPT_REQUIRED
    description: >
      No execution may claim constitutional legitimacy
      without a complete replay transcript.

  - id: NO_IMPLICIT_FIELDS
    description: >
      Every field in a transcript MUST be explicitly present.
      No defaults, inference, or omission is allowed.

  - id: DETERMINISTIC_ONLY
    description: >
      Transcripts MUST represent deterministic execution only.
      Any nondeterminism invalidates replay.

  - id: REPLAY_HASH_TERMINAL
    description: >
      replay_hash is the terminal authority for replay identity.
      Any mismatch invalidates legitimacy.

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# CANONICAL TRANSCRIPT STRUCTURE
# -------------------------------------------------------------------

replay_transcript:

  # ===============================================================
  # HEADER / IDENTITY
  # ===============================================================

  header:
    transcript_id:
      type: uuid
      required: true
      description: >
        Globally unique identifier for this transcript.

    created_at:
      type: timestamp
      required: true
      description: >
        Time the transcript was generated.
        Informational only; does not affect replay.

    afritech_version:
      type: string
      required: true
      description: >
        AfriTech runtime version used for execution.

    execution_environment_hash:
      type: hash
      required: true
      description: >
        Hash of environment configuration used to bind replay.

  # ===============================================================
  # REQUEST IDENTITY
  # ===============================================================

  request_hash:
    type: hash
    required: true
    description: >
      Cryptographic hash of the full constitutional request
      envelope (`constitutional_request.yaml`).

  # ===============================================================
  # REPLAY ENVIRONMENT BINDING
  # ===============================================================

  replay_environment:
    runtime_version:
      type: string
      required: true

    model_version:
      type: string
      required: true

    constitution_version:
      type: string
      required: true

    deterministic_mode:
      type: boolean
      required: true
      value: true

  # ===============================================================
  # EXECUTION TRACE
  # ===============================================================

  execution_trace:
    type: ordered_list
    required: true

    entry_schema:
      step:
        type: string
        required: true
        description: >
          Fully‑qualified execution step identifier.

      input_hash:
        type: hash
        required: true
        description: >
          Hash of all step inputs.

      output_hash:
        type: hash
        required: true
        description: >
          Hash of all step outputs.

  # ===============================================================
  # TRUTHPACKET IDENTITY
  # ===============================================================

  truth_packet_hash:
    type: hash
    required: true
    description: >
      Cryptographic hash of the emitted TruthPacket.

  # ===============================================================
  # EPISTEMIC CONFIDENCE (SUMMARY VIEW)
  # ===============================================================
  #
  # This MUST match the TruthPacket epistemic_confidence
  # exactly. Included here for replay validation convenience.

  epistemic_confidence:
    type: object
    required: true
    schema_ref: afritech/truth/epistemic_confidence.yaml

  # ===============================================================
  # CAUSAL TRACE (SUMMARY VIEW)
  # ===============================================================

  causal_trace:
    type: object
    required: true

    fields:
      decisions:
        type: list
        required: true

      dependencies:
        type: list
        required: true

      rejected_paths:
        type: list
        required: true

  # ===============================================================
  # TERMINAL REPLAY HASH
  # ===============================================================

  replay_hash:
    type: hash
    required: true
    description: >
      Terminal deterministic hash representing the
      complete constitutional execution.
      This value is authoritative.

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# VALIDATION RULES
# -------------------------------------------------------------------

validation:

  strict: true

  failure_handling:
    mode: HARD_FAILURE
    description: >
      Any deviation from this schema MUST result in
      immediate replay invalidation.

  audit_requirements:
    - request_hash MUST match reconstructed request
    - execution_trace MUST be complete and ordered
    - truth_packet_hash MUST match regenerated TruthPacket
    - epistemic_confidence MUST be reproducible
    - replay_hash MUST match recomputed value

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# PROHIBITED TRANSCRIPT PRACTICES
# -------------------------------------------------------------------

forbidden_practices:

  - missing_execution_steps
  - unordered_execution_trace
  - elided_hashes
  - inferred_fields
  - partial_traces
  - narrative_explanations
  - non-deterministic markers

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# CONSTITUTIONAL ASSERTION
# -------------------------------------------------------------------

constitutional_assertion: >
  AfriTech recognizes no constitutional execution
  unless it can be exactly reconstructed from
  a transcript conforming to this schema.

===== ./afritech/runtime/contracts/normalization_contract.yaml =====
schema: afritech.runtime.contracts.normalization.v1

normalization_contract:
  status: mandatory
  applies_to:
    - semantic_yaml
    - s_ir
    - proof_generation
    - execution_admission

  invariant:
    evaluation_requires_normalized_ir: true
    hashing_requires_normalized_ir: true
    proof_requires_normalized_hash: true
    raw_expression_evaluation_allowed: false

  canonical_order:
    - compile
    - normalize
    - hash
    - evaluate
    - proof

  mvp_rewrites:
    and:
      flatten_nested_and: true
      remove_duplicate_operands: true
      sort_operands_by_canonical_hash: true
      single_operand_collapses: true

    equivalent:
      sort_binary_operands_by_canonical_hash: true

    requires:
      preserve_operand_order: true

    forall:
      preserve_variable_domain_body_shape: true
      normalize_body: true

  hard_failures:
    - normalization_failed
    - unsupported_operator
    - undeclared_symbol
    - rewrite_overflow
    - hash_mismatch

  on_violation: SYSTEM_INVALID

    - canonical_expression_matches_normalized_s_ir
    - proof_hash_matches_proof_payload

  on_violation: SYSTEM_INVALID

===== ./afritech/runtime/system_enforcement/execution_pipeline.yaml =====
schema: afritech.runtime.system_enforcement.execution_pipeline.v1

execution_pipeline:
  authority: canonical_runtime_path
  status: frozen_for_mvp

  invariant:
    runtime_code_may_execute_semantics: true
    runtime_code_must_not_define_semantics: true
    raw_expression_evaluation_allowed: false

  stages:
    - name: compile
      input: semantic_yaml
      output: s_ir
      failure: SYSTEM_INVALID

    - name: normalize
      input: s_ir
      output: normalized_s_ir
      required_before_evaluation: true
      failure: SYSTEM_INVALID

    - name: hash
      input: normalized_s_ir
      output: normalized_expression_hash
      failure: SYSTEM_INVALID

    - name: evaluate
      input: normalized_s_ir
      output: admissibility_result
      allowed_operators:
        - AND
        - EQUIVALENT
        - REQUIRES
        - FORALL
      failure: SYSTEM_INVALID

    - name: proof
      input:
        - normalized_expression_hash
        - admissibility_result
      output: proof_artifact
      failure: SYSTEM_INVALID

    - name: admission_gate
      input: proof_artifact
      output:
        - ADMIT
        - REJECT
      failure: SYSTEM_INVALID

  non_bypassable_order:
    - compile
    - normalize
    - hash
    - evaluate
    - proof
    - admission_gate

===== ./afritech/semantic_calculus/evaluation_rules.yaml =====
schema: afritech.semantic_calculus.evaluation.v1

evaluation:

  AND:
    rule: all_true

  OR:
    rule: any_true

  IMPLIES:
    truth_table:
      - lhs: FALSE
        result: TRUE
      - lhs: TRUE
        rhs: FALSE
        result: FALSE
      - lhs: TRUE
        rhs: TRUE
        result: TRUE

  EQUIVALENT:
    rule: equality

  SUBSET:
    rule: set_inclusion

  FORALL:
    rule: universal_quantification

  EXISTS:
    rule: existential_quantification

===== ./afritech/semantic_calculus/proof_rules.yaml =====
schema: afritech.semantic_calculus.proof_rules.v1

inference_rules:

  modus_ponens:

    from:
      - IMPLIES(A, B)
      - A

    derive:
      - B

  equivalence_elimination:

    from:
      - EQUIVALENT(A, B)

    derive:
      - IMPLIES(A, B)
      - IMPLIES(B, A)

  conjunction_elimination:

    from:
      - AND(A, B)

    derive:
      - A
      - B

  conjunction_introduction:

    from:
      - A
      - B

    derive:
      - AND(A, B)

    rewrite: A

  - id: RW-002
    pattern: AND(A, TRUE)
    rewrite: A

  - id: RW-003
    pattern: OR(A, FALSE)
    rewrite: A

  - id: RW-004
    pattern: IMPLIES(A, A)
    rewrite: TRUE

  - id: RW-005
    pattern: EQUIVALENT(A, A)
    rewrite: TRUE
