===== ./afritech/speculative/civilization/architectural_blueprint.yaml =====
schema: afritech.civilization.autonomous_intelligence.v1

civilization_system:

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # PURPOSE
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  description: >
    A global, autonomous, self-governing intelligence system capable of:
      - generating and validating knowledge
      - coordinating resources
      - evolving governance structures
      - maintaining systemic stability
      - aligning incentives at scale

  model: CIVILIZATION_SCALE_CONSTITUTIONAL_INTELLIGENCE

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # CORE AXIOMS
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  axioms:

    - truth_is_deterministic_and_verifiable
    - consensus_defines_shared_reality
    - incentives_align_behavior_with_truth
    - governance_must_self-correct
    - system_must_self-evolve

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # SYSTEM LAYERS
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  layers:

    # =============================================================
    # 1. INTELLIGENCE LAYER
    # =============================================================

    intelligence:

      function: generate knowledge and decisions

      components:

        - inference_engine
        - reasoning_network
        - knowledge_graph
        - evidence_validation

      invariant:

        - all outputs must be replay-verifiable

    # =============================================================
    # 2. EXECUTION LAYER
    # =============================================================

    execution:

      function: deterministic computation

      guarantees:

        - reproducibility
        - auditability
        - consistency

    # =============================================================
    # 3. CONSENSUS LAYER
    # =============================================================

    consensus:

      function: establish truth

      types:

        - node_consensus
        - system_consensus
        - federation_consensus

      rule:

        truth = deterministic_execution + agreement

    # =============================================================
    # 4. REPUTATION LAYER
    # =============================================================

    reputation:

      function: trust modeling

      outputs:

        - node_trust
        - system_trust
        - federation_trust

      role:

        - influence voting power
        - influence rewards

    # =============================================================
    # 5. GOVERNANCE LAYER
    # =============================================================

    governance:

      function: rule definition and evolution

      capabilities:

        - rule enforcement
        - rule generation
        - rule mutation

      mechanism:

        - autonomous proposals
        - simulation validation
        - consensus approval

    # =============================================================
    # 6. ECONOMIC LAYER
    # =============================================================

    economics:

      function: incentive alignment

      components:

        - staking
        - rewards
        - slashing

      invariant:

        honesty > profit
        dishonesty < loss

    # =============================================================
    # 7. HEALING LAYER
    # =============================================================

    healing:

      function: system recovery

      capabilities:

        - fault detection
        - node isolation
        - recompute truth

    # =============================================================
    # 8. EVOLUTION LAYER
    # =============================================================

    evolution:

      function: system improvement

      capabilities:

        - self-generated ADRs
        - governance upgrades
        - architecture refinement

    # =============================================================
    # 9. FEDERATION LAYER
    # =============================================================

    federation:

      function: inter-system validation

      guarantees:

        - no single system defines truth
        - global consensus enforced

    # =============================================================
    # 10. PHYSICAL + RESOURCE LAYER
    # =============================================================

    resources:

      function: real-world coordination

      domains:

        - logistics
        - agriculture
        - manufacturing
        - energy

      role:

        - transform digital decisions → physical outcomes

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # FEEDBACK LOOPS
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  loops:

    truth_loop:
      execution → replay → consensus → accepted_truth

    trust_loop:
      performance → reputation → influence → performance

    economic_loop:
      behavior → reward/slash → stake → behavior

    governance_loop:
      observation → proposal → simulation → upgrade

    resilience_loop:
      failure → detection → healing → recovery

    evolution_loop:
      system_state → improvement → adoption → new_state

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # GLOBAL INVARIANTS
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  invariants:

    - determinism_must_hold
    - replay_must_verify
    - consensus_must_be_required
    - incentives_must_align_with_truth
    - evolution_must_preserve_integrity
    - no_single_point_of_authority

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # FINAL ASSERTION
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  final_assertion: >
    This system is a self-sustaining intelligence structure.

    It perceives reality,
    verifies truth,
    aligns behavior,
    governs itself,
    heals itself,
    and evolves continuously.

    It is not a program.
    It is a civilization.

===== ./afritech/speculative/distributed/execution_verification.yaml =====
schema: afritech.distributed.execution.verification.v1

distributed_execution:

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # PURPOSE
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  description: >
    This system defines multi-node verification of execution,
    ensuring that results are:
      - independently reproduced
      - cryptographically verified
      - consensus-approved

    No single runtime can assert truth alone.

  model: CONSENSUS_REPLAY_VERIFICATION

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # NODE MODEL
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  nodes:

    definition: >
      Independent AfriTech runtimes executing identical inputs
      under identical attested environments.

    requirements:

      - identical_runtime_certificate
      - identical_attestation
      - deterministic_execution_environment
      - replay_verifier_enabled

    invariant: >
      All nodes MUST produce identical results for the same context.

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # EXECUTION PROCESS
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  execution_flow:

    - step: request_distribution
      description: >
        Execution request distributed to all participating nodes.

    - step: local_execution
      description: >
        Each node runs deterministic execution independently.

    - step: result_generation
      description: >
        Each node produces ExecutionResult (hash-stable).

    - step: local_replay
      description: >
        Each node verifies its own result via replay system.

    - step: result_broadcast
      description: >
        Each node publishes:
          - result_hash
          - context_hash
          - proof_hash

    - step: consensus_evaluation
      description: >
        Node results are compared across network.

    - step: consensus_decision
      description: >
        If quorum reached → result accepted.
        If mismatch → execution invalidated.

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # CONSENSUS MODEL
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  consensus:

    type: HASH_CONSENSUS

    quorum:

      minimum_nodes: 3
      required_agreement_ratio: 0.67

    agreement_rule:

      definition: >
        result_hash must match across nodes participating in quorum.

      mismatch_effect:

        - execution_invalidated
        - replay_invalidated
        - certificate_flagged

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # RESULT AGREEMENT STRUCTURE
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  result_comparison:

    keys:

      - context_hash
      - result_hash
      - replay_hash

    invariant:

      - all_fields_must_match

    violation:

      effect: CONSENSUS_FAILURE

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # MULTI-NODE PROOF STRUCTURE
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  distributed_proof:

    definition: >
      Aggregate proof of execution across nodes.

    structure:

      proof_id: "<UUID>"

      context_hash: "<SHA256>"

      participating_nodes:

        - node_id: NODE_A
          result_hash: "<hash>"
          replay_hash: "<hash>"
          signature: "<signature>"

        - node_id: NODE_B
          result_hash: "<hash>"
          replay_hash: "<hash>"
          signature: "<signature>"

        - node_id: NODE_C
          result_hash: "<hash>"
          replay_hash: "<hash>"
          signature: "<signature>"

      consensus:

        achieved: true
        agreement_ratio: 1.0

      final_result_hash: "<hash>"

      timestamp: "<deterministic timestamp>"

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # NODE SIGNATURE REQUIREMENTS
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  node_signatures:

    required: true

    algorithm: ED25519

    signature_scope:

      - context_hash
      - result_hash
      - replay_hash

    verification_required: true

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # FAILURE HANDLING
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  failure_handling:

    node_disagreement:

      effect:

        - reject_execution
        - discard_result
        - trigger_alert

    malicious_node_detection:

      criteria:

        - repeated mismatched results
        - invalid signatures
        - replay inconsistencies

      action:

        - node_quarantined
        - excluded_from_quorum

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # REPLAY EXTENSION
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  replay_extension:

    invariant:

      - local_replay_required_per_node
      - cross_node_result_consistency_required

    rule:

      definition: >
        Execution is only valid if:
          replay(success) AND consensus(success)

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # CERTIFICATE EXTENSION
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  certificate_extension:

    distributed_binding:

      required: true

      additional_fields:

        - node_id
        - network_id
        - consensus_epoch

    validation:

      - certificate_must_match_across_nodes
      - signature_root_must_match

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # DETERMINISM GUARANTEE
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  determinism:

    invariant: >
      Given identical:
        - context
        - certificate
        - attestation

      All nodes MUST produce identical output hashes.

    violation_effect:

      - system_fault_detected
      - consensus_invalidated

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # NON-OBSERVABILITY GUARANTEE
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  non_observability:

    invariant: >
      Consensus decisions must be derived solely from:
        - result hashes
        - replay proofs
        - signatures

      No external observation allowed.

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # CONSTITUTIONAL ASSERTION
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  constitutional_assertion: >
    No single node may assert execution truth.

    Truth is established only through:

      - deterministic execution
      - replay verification
      - multi-node agreement
      - cryptographic signatures

    Any deviation SHALL result in:

      - execution rejection
      - node invalidation
      - consensus failure

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # FINAL ASSERTION
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  final_assertion: >
    Execution truth emerges from agreement, not authority.

    One node can execute.
    Many nodes must agree.

    No consensus → no truth.
    No truth → no system. 
    


===== ./afritech/speculative/distributed/self_healing_governance.yaml =====
schema: afritech.distributed.governance.self_healing.v1

self_healing_governance:

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # PURPOSE
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  description: >
    Defines autonomous governance behavior for a distributed AfriTech system.

    The system:
      - detects faults
      - isolates bad actors
      - restores consistency
      - reseals truth state

  model: AUTONOMOUS_CONSTITUTIONAL_RECOVERY

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # CORE PRINCIPLES
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  principles:

    - truth_is_consensus
    - consensus_requires_trustworthy_nodes
    - trust_is_dynamic
    - drift_must_be_corrected
    - system_must_self_repair

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # HEALING TRIGGERS
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  triggers:

    - consensus_failure
    - replay_mismatch_detected
    - node_misbehavior_detected
    - certificate_inconsistency
    - attestation_drift
    - quorum_failure

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # HEALING ACTIONS
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  healing_actions:

    isolate_faulty_nodes:

      description: >
        Nodes with low reputation or repeated mismatch are quarantined.

      action:
        - mark_status: QUARANTINED
        - remove_from_quorum: true

    shrink_quorum:

      description: >
        If nodes are removed, quorum recalculates automatically.

      rules:
        minimum_nodes: 2
        ratio_adjustment: dynamic

    recompute_consensus:

      description: >
        Remaining trusted nodes recompute execution.

      required:
        - deterministic_execution
        - replay_verification

    revalidate_attestation:

      description: >
        Ensure remaining state matches attested system.

      required: true

    regenerate_proof:

      description: >
        New distributed proof is generated after healing.

      required: true

    reseal_system:

      description: >
        System produces new attestation + certificate.

      triggers_on:
        - consensus_change
        - node_group_change

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # NODE STATE TRANSITIONS
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  node_states:

    ACTIVE:
      description: fully trusted participant

    WATCHLIST:
      description: degraded trust (limited influence)

    QUARANTINED:
      description: excluded from participation

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # AUTO-RECOVERY
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  recovery:

    description: >
      Nodes may regain trust through consistent agreement over time.

    mechanism:

      score_increment_per_success: 0.02

      restore_threshold: 0.75

      from_watchlist_to_active: true
      from_quarantined_to_watchlist: optional

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # GOVERNANCE LOOP
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  governance_loop:

    cycle:

      - execute
      - verify_replay
      - verify_consensus
      - update_reputation
      - detect_faults
      - apply_healing
      - reseal_if_needed

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # RESEAL MECHANISM
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  resealing:

    description: >
      After healing, system generates a new constitutional state.

    artifacts:

      - new_attestation.yaml
      - new_runtime_certificate.cert

    constraints:

      - epoch_must_increment
      - registry_hash_must_match
      - surface_registry_must_match

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # FINAL ASSERTION
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  final_assertion: >
    The system maintains its own integrity.

    When failure occurs:
      it detects itself,
      isolates the cause,
      recomputes truth,
      and restores valid state.

    No manual governance required.

===== ./afritech/speculative/federation/economic_model.yaml =====
schema: afritech.federation.economic_model.v1

economic_model:

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # PURPOSE
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  description: >
    Defines incentives and penalties for nodes and systems participating
    in AfriTech federation.

    Ensures:
      - honest behavior is rewarded
      - malicious behavior is penalized
      - consensus remains economically stable

  model: STAKE_BASED_CONSENSUS_SECURITY

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # PARTICIPATION REQUIREMENTS
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  participation:

    requirement: >
      Every node/system must lock economic stake to participate
      in consensus and execution validation.

    minimum_stake:

      node: 100
      system: 1000

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # STAKING MODEL
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  staking:

    definition: >
      Participants deposit stake to gain the right to:
        - propose execution
        - validate results
        - participate in consensus

    staking_units: AFR

    lock_conditions:

      - active_in_consensus
      - not_quarantined
      - no_unresolved_misconduct

    release_conditions:

      - voluntary_exit
      - clean_reputation
      - no_pending_penalties

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # REWARD MODEL
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  rewards:

    types:

      execution_reward:
        description: >
          Nodes receive reward for participating in valid consensus.

        conditions:

          - agrees_with_consensus
          - valid_replay
          - valid_signature

        amount: proportional_to_stake

      verification_reward:
        description: >
          Systems validating cross-system proofs receive rewards.

        conditions:

          - correct_verification
          - participation in quorum

      governance_reward:
        description: >
          Nodes voting correctly on governance proposals.

        conditions:

          - vote_matches_final_consensus

    distribution:

      mechanism: proportional_weighting

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # SLASHING MODEL
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  slashing:

    definition: >
      Stake is deducted for incorrect or malicious behavior.

    penalties:

      result_mismatch:
        amount: 10%
        trigger: node_result_disagrees_with_consensus

      replay_failure:
        amount: 20%
        trigger: invalid_replay_proof

      invalid_signature:
        amount: 15%

      byzantine_behavior:
        amount: 50%
        trigger: repeated_mismatch + invalid_signature

    escalation:

      repeated_offenses:

        - increase_penalty_multiplier
        - enforce_quarantine

    invariant:

      - penalty_must_exceed_reward_for_attack

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # REPUTATION LINKAGE
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  reputation:

    integration:

      - reputation_score influences voting power
      - reputation_score influences reward share

    coupling:

      low_reputation:

        - reduced_rewards
        - increased_slashing

      high_reputation:

        - priority_in_consensus
        - bonus_rewards

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # QUARANTINE ECONOMICS
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  quarantine:

    consequences:

      - participation_blocked
      - reward_zeroed
      - stake_partially_slashed

    recovery:

      required:

        - consistent_correct_behavior
        - stake_top_up

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # INCENTIVE ALIGNMENT
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  incentive_alignment:

    guarantees:

      - honest_behavior_profitable
      - dishonest_behavior_unprofitable
      - long_term_participation_rewarded

    attack_resistance:

      cost_of_attack > potential_gain

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # FEDERATION LEVEL
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  federation_layer:

    cross_system_rewards:

      - systems agreeing with federated consensus rewarded
      - dissenting systems penalized

    system_slashing:

      trigger:

        - cross_system_mismatch
        - invalid_proof_submission

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # GOVERNANCE ECONOMICS
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  governance:

    participation:

      - stake_required_for_voting
      - higher stake → higher influence (bounded)

    penalties:

      - voting_against_consensus repeatedly → reputation loss

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # FINAL ASSERTION
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  final_assertion: >
    Truth is not only enforced by logic,
    but protected by economics.

    Honest actors profit.
    Dishonest actors lose stake.

    The system aligns incentives with correctness.

===== ./afritech/speculative/federation/inter_network_governance.yaml =====
schema: afritech.federation.inter_network.v1

inter_network_federation:

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # PURPOSE
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  description: >
    Defines federation across multiple independent AfriTech systems,
    enabling cross-system validation, shared truth, and governance.

    Each system retains sovereignty, but participates in:
      - cross-validation
      - federated consensus
      - shared governance evolution

  model: FEDERATED_CONSTITUTIONAL_NETWORK

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # SYSTEM MODEL
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  systems:

    definition: >
      Each AfriTech instance operates independently with its own:
        - registry
        - attestation
        - runtime certificates
        - governance rules

    identity:

      required_fields:

        - system_id
        - network_id
        - attestation_root_hash
        - governance_version

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # FEDERATION LAYER
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  federation:

    topology: PEER_TO_PEER

    invariant:

      - no_central_authority
      - all_systems_equal_participants

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # CROSS-SYSTEM VERIFICATION
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  cross_verification:

    description: >
      Systems independently verify execution results from other systems.

    required_checks:

      - context_hash_match
      - result_hash_match
      - replay_verification
      - certificate_validation

    invariant:

      - cross_system_replay_must_hold

    violation_effect:

      - result_rejected
      - system_flagged

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # FEDERATED CONSENSUS
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  consensus:

    type: MULTI_SYSTEM_CONSENSUS

    quorum:

      minimum_systems: 3
      agreement_ratio: 0.67

    levels:

      intra_system:
        description: local node-level consensus

      inter_system:
        description: cross-system consensus

    final_truth_rule: >
      Truth is only accepted if:
        intra_system_consensus AND inter_system_consensus

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # FEDERATED PROOF
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  federated_proof:

    structure:

      proof_id: "<UUID>"

      context_hash: "<SHA256>"

      systems:

        - system_id: SYS_A
          node_proof_hash: "<hash>"
          final_result_hash: "<hash>"
          signature: "<signature>"

        - system_id: SYS_B
          node_proof_hash: "<hash>"
          final_result_hash: "<hash>"
          signature: "<signature>"

      consensus:

        intra_system_consensus: true
        inter_system_consensus: true
        agreement_ratio: 1.0

      final_hash: "<hash>"

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # TRUST MODEL
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  trust:

    principle: TRUST_PER_SYSTEM

    tracking:

      - system_reputation_score
      - disagreement_history
      - replay_validity

    thresholds:

      active: > 0.75
      watchlist: 0.5 - 0.75
      excluded: < 0.5

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # SYSTEM QUARANTINE
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  system_quarantine:

    triggers:

      - repeated_mismatch
      - invalid_replay
      - signature_failure

    actions:

      - exclude_from_consensus
      - mark_untrusted
      - require_revalidation

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # FEDERATED HEALING
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  healing:

    description: >
      If cross-system disagreement occurs, federation resolves conflict.

    process:

      - isolate_faulty_systems
      - recompute_consensus
      - regenerate_federated_proof

    invariant:

      - trust_majority_systems

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # GOVERNANCE SYNC
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  governance_sync:

    description: >
      Systems share governance improvements across federation.

    mechanism:

      - proposal_broadcast
      - simulation_in_each_system
      - federated_vote

    invariant:

      - no_forced_upgrade
      - voluntary adoption

    compatibility:

      - version_alignment_required
      - replay_compatibility_required

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # VERSION COMPATIBILITY
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  compatibility:

    requirement:

      - systems_must_support_same_protocol_version

    handling:

      incompatible_systems:

        - excluded_from_consensus
        - allowed_read_only_participation

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # SECURITY MODEL
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  security:

    guarantees:

      - no_single_system_can_define_truth
      - malicious_systems_are_isolated
      - replay_integrity_enforced_globally

    attack_resistance:

      - byzantine_fault_tolerance
      - majority_honest_assumption

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # NON-OBSERVABILITY
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  non_observability:

    invariant: >
      Cross-system truth must be derivable solely from:
        - proofs
        - signatures
        - deterministic execution

      No external observer allowed.

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # FINAL ASSERTION
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  final_assertion: >
    No system stands alone.

    Truth is not local.
    Truth is not distributed.
    Truth is federated.

    A system may compute truth,
    but only the federation can confirm it.


===== ./afritech/state_machine/state_schema.yaml =====
schema: afritech.state_machine.v1

state_machine:

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # STATE DEFINITIONS
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  states:

    - UNINITIALIZED
    - ADMITTED
    - EXECUTING
    - COMPLETED
    - FAILED

  initial_state: UNINITIALIZED

  terminal_states:
    - COMPLETED
    - FAILED

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # TRANSITION MODEL
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  transition_model:

    type: TOTAL               # ALL transitions must be defined
    enforcement: STRICT       # reject undefined transitions
    determinism: REQUIRED     # replay must reproduce same state sequence

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # TRANSITION DEFINITIONS (INLINE OPTIONAL)
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  transitions:

    allowed:

      - id: S1_ADMISSION
        from: UNINITIALIZED
        to: ADMITTED

      - id: S2_EXECUTION
        from: ADMITTED
        to: EXECUTING

      - id: S3_COMPLETION
        from: EXECUTING
        to: COMPLETED

      - id: S4_FAILURE
        from: EXECUTING
        to: FAILED

    forbidden:

      - from: UNINITIALIZED
        to: EXECUTING

      - from: COMPLETED
        to: EXECUTING

      - from: FAILED
        to: ADMITTED

      - from: EXECUTING
        to: ADMITTED

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # STATE INVARIANTS
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  invariants:

    - I19_STATE_TRANSITION_TOTALITY
      # ALL state transitions must be defined (allowed or forbidden)

    - I19_1_ALLOWED_ONLY
      # Only explicitly allowed transitions may occur

    - I19_2_FORBIDDEN_ENFORCED
      # Explicitly forbidden transitions MUST be rejected

    - I19_3_NO_IMPLICIT_TRANSITIONS
      # No transition may happen unless declared

    - I19_4_REPLAY_MATCH
      # Replay MUST produce identical state sequence

    - I19_5_SINGLE_STATE_AT_TIME
      # System MUST be in exactly one state

    - I19_6_INITIAL_STATE_FIXED
      # Execution MUST start in UNINITIALIZED

    - I19_7_TERMINAL_STATE_FINAL
      # No transition allowed after reaching terminal state

    - I19_8_TRANSITION_IDENTITY
      # Each transition MUST have unique id

    - I19_9_TRANSITION_HASH_BINDING
      # Each transition MUST be hashable and reproducible

    - I19_10_STATE_SPACE_COMPLETENESS
      # allowed ∪ forbidden MUST cover all state combinations

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # VALIDATION CONTRACT
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  validation:

    required_at_runtime: true
    required_for_trace_binding: true
    required_for_replay: true

    enforce_totality: true
    enforce_forbidden: true
    enforce_determinism: true

    failure_policy:

      type: HARD_FAILURE
      effect: EXECUTION_ABORT

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # REPLAY CONTRACT
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  replay:

    deterministic: true

    requirements:

      - identical_transition_sequence
      - identical_final_state
      - identical_transition_hashes

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # TRACE INTEGRATION
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  trace_binding:

    enabled: true

    requirements:

      - every transition MUST map to trace event
      - event.step MUST match transition id
      - event.output_hash MUST bind resulting state

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # AUTHORITY INTEGRATION
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  authority_binding:

    required: true

    rule:

      each_transition MUST be executed under valid authority_profile
      derived from GENESIS → REGISTRY

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # METADATA (NON-AUTHORITATIVE)
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  metadata:

    description: "AfriTech deterministic state machine"
    version: v1
    environment: production

    notes: >
      This state machine enforces semantic closure.
      No execution path exists outside of defined transitions.

===== ./afritech/state_machine/state_transitions.yaml =====
schema: afritech.state_transitions.v1

transitions:

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # DECLARED STATES (REPEATED FOR VALIDATION CONSISTENCY)
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  states:

    - UNINITIALIZED
    - ADMITTED
    - EXECUTING
    - COMPLETED
    - FAILED

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # ALLOWED TRANSITIONS (EXPLICIT ONLY)
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  allowed:

    - id: S1_ADMISSION
      from: UNINITIALIZED
      to: ADMITTED
      type: FORWARD
      terminal: false

    - id: S2_EXECUTION
      from: ADMITTED
      to: EXECUTING
      type: FORWARD
      terminal: false

    - id: S3_COMPLETION
      from: EXECUTING
      to: COMPLETED
      type: FORWARD
      terminal: true

    - id: S4_FAILURE
      from: EXECUTING
      to: FAILED
      type: FORWARD
      terminal: true

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # FORBIDDEN TRANSITIONS (TOTAL COMPLEMENT)
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  forbidden:

    # -------------------------------------------------------------
    # FROM UNINITIALIZED
    # -------------------------------------------------------------

    - from: UNINITIALIZED
      to: EXECUTING

    - from: UNINITIALIZED
      to: COMPLETED

    - from: UNINITIALIZED
      to: FAILED

    # -------------------------------------------------------------
    # FROM ADMITTED
    # -------------------------------------------------------------

    - from: ADMITTED
      to: UNINITIALIZED

    - from: ADMITTED
      to: COMPLETED

    - from: ADMITTED
      to: FAILED

    # -------------------------------------------------------------
    # FROM EXECUTING
    # -------------------------------------------------------------

    - from: EXECUTING
      to: UNINITIALIZED

    - from: EXECUTING
      to: ADMITTED

    # -------------------------------------------------------------
    # TERMINAL STATES (CRITICAL)
    # -------------------------------------------------------------

    # COMPLETED is terminal
    - from: COMPLETED
      to: UNINITIALIZED

    - from: COMPLETED
      to: ADMITTED

    - from: COMPLETED
      to: EXECUTING

    - from: COMPLETED
      to: FAILED

    # FAILED is terminal
    - from: FAILED
      to: UNINITIALIZED

    - from: FAILED
      to: ADMITTED

    - from: FAILED
      to: EXECUTING

    - from: FAILED
      to: COMPLETED

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # COMPLETENESS GUARANTEE
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  completeness:

    total_states: 5

    expected_transitions: 25   # N x N (5 × 5)

    coverage:

      allowed_count: 4
      forbidden_count: 21

      rule: >
        allowed + forbidden MUST equal total possible transitions

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # TRANSITION PROPERTIES
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  properties:

    deterministic: true
    replay_safe: true

    rules:

      - exactly_one_transition_per_step
      - no_multi_state_overlap
      - no_implicit_transition
      - terminal_states_are_final
      - forward_progress_only

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # INVARIANTS (ENFORCED CONTRACT)
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  invariants:

    - I19_STATE_TRANSITION_TOTALITY
      # All transitions explicitly defined

    - I19_1_ALLOWED_ONLY
      # Only declared allowed transitions can execute

    - I19_2_FORBIDDEN_ENFORCED
      # Forbidden transitions must always fail

    - I19_3_NO_IMPLICIT_TRANSITIONS
      # Any undefined transition is illegal

    - I19_4_REPLAY_MATCH
      # Replay must produce identical sequence

    - I19_5_SINGLE_STATE_AT_TIME
      # System can only occupy one state

    - I19_6_INITIAL_STATE_FIXED
      # Must always start from UNINITIALIZED

    - I19_7_TERMINAL_STATE_FINAL
      # No transitions from terminal states

    - I19_8_TOTAL_STATE_SPACE_COVERED
      # allowed ∪ forbidden = ALL possible transitions

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # VALIDATION RULES (STRICT)
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  validation:

    enforce_totality: true
    enforce_disjoint_sets: true
    enforce_unique_ids: true
    enforce_terminal_finality: true

    failure_policy:

      type: HARD_FAILURE
      effect: EXECUTION_ABORT

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # TRACE BINDING REQUIREMENTS
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  trace_binding:

    enabled: true

    rules:

      - each transition MUST map to trace event.step
      - event index MUST reflect transition order
      - transition_hash MUST match trace event_hash

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # REPLAY CONTRACT
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  replay:

    deterministic: true

    required:

      - identical_transition_sequence
      - identical_final_state
      - identical_transition_hashes

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # METADATA
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  metadata:

    version: v1
    environment: production

    description: >
      Fully closed state transition system with total coverage.
      No undefined behavior exists. All transitions are explicitly
      classified as allowed or forbidden.

    notes: >
      This file guarantees semantic closure.
      Any transition outside defined sets MUST cause rejection.

===== ./afritech/trace/trace_schema.yaml =====
schema: afritech.trace.v1

trace:

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # TRACE IDENTITY
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  trace_id: string                # UUIDv4 (externally assigned or deterministic)
  request_hash: sha256           # Canonical hash of request payload

  authority_profile: string      # MUST match registry authority
  epoch_id: string               # MUST match active epoch

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # TRACE EVENTS (ORDERED + PARTIAL DAG)
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  events:

    - index: int                 # STRICT: 0..N-1 (no gaps)

      step: string               # canonical step name (enum-bound)

      # -------------------------
      # CAUSAL STRUCTURE
      # -------------------------

      parent_event_hash: sha256  # previous event hash OR "GENESIS" if index=0
      depends_on:                # optional DAG edges
        - int                    # indices of prior events (must be < index)

      # -------------------------
      # AUTHORITY CONTEXT
      # -------------------------

      authority_context_hash: sha256
      # derived from:
      #   authority_profile
      #   runtime_context
      #   permissions snapshot

      # -------------------------
      # INPUT / OUTPUT BINDING
      # -------------------------

      input_hash: sha256         # canonical input
      output_hash: sha256        # canonical output

      # -------------------------
      # EVENT HASH (CRITICAL)
      # -------------------------

      event_hash: sha256
      # sha256 over:
      #   index
      #   step
      #   parent_event_hash
      #   depends_on
      #   authority_context_hash
      #   input_hash
      #   output_hash

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # TRACE ROOT (GLOBAL COMMITMENT)
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  trace_root_hash: sha256
  # sha256(
  #   canonical_list(event_hash)
  # )

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # OPTIONAL EXTENSIONS (STRICTLY CONTROLLED)
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  metadata:

    version: int                 # trace versioning for compatibility

    generation_mode:             # deterministic / replay / test
      enum:
        - deterministic
        - replay
        - test

    origin:

      runtime_id: string         # runtime instance id
      certificate_id: string     # runtime certificate binding

    integrity:

      canonicalization: json_sorted_compact
      hashing_algorithm: sha256
      encoding: utf-8

  # -----------------------------------------------------------------
  # VALIDATION RULES (FULL CONTRACT)
  # -----------------------------------------------------------------

  invariants:

    - I16_CANONICAL_TRACE_BINDING

    - I16_1_INDEX_CONTIGUITY
      # index MUST be contiguous [0..N-1]

    - I16_2_PARENT_CHAIN_VALID
      # each event[i].parent_event_hash == event[i-1].event_hash

    - I16_3_DEPENDENCY_VALIDITY
      # depends_on ONLY references indices < index

    - I16_4_DEPENDENCY_ACYCLIC
      # DAG must contain no cycles

    - I16_5_EVENT_HASH_CORRECT
      # recomputed hash MUST match event_hash

    - I16_6_ROOT_HASH_CORRECT
      # recomputed root MUST match trace_root_hash

    - I16_7_DETERMINISTIC_SERIALIZATION
      # canonical JSON:
      #   sorted keys
      #   compact separators
      #   UTF-8 encoding

    - I16_8_AUTHORITY_BINDING
      # authority_context_hash MUST be derivable and consistent

    - I16_9_INPUT_OUTPUT_BINDING
      # input/output hashes MUST match execution replay

    - I16_10_REPLAY_EQUALITY
      # replay(trace) MUST produce identical trace_root_hash

    - I16_11_NO_EXTERNAL_STATE
      # trace MUST encode all state required for replay

    - I16_12_IMMUTABILITY
      # any mutation MUST invalidate trace_root_hash


===== ./afritech/truth/epistemic_confidence.yaml =====
# afritech/truth/epistemic_confidence.yaml
#
# STATUS: CANONICAL EPISTEMIC CONFIDENCE SPECIFICATION
#
# This file defines the ONLY admissible epistemic confidence
# structure permitted in a TruthPacket during the
# FIRST_EXECUTABLE_PROOF phase.
#
# Confidence is treated as a constitutional artifact.
# It must be decomposed, normalized, auditable, and replayable.
#
# Any TruthPacket containing confidence information that
# deviates from this schema is constitutionally invalid.

version: EPISTEMIC_CONFIDENCE_V1

applicability:
  phase: FIRST_EXECUTABLE_PROOF
  enforced_by:
    - TruthPacketConstructor
    - ConstitutionalAgent
    - ReplayVerifier

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# GLOBAL EPISTEMIC INVARIANTS
# -------------------------------------------------------------------

global_invariants:

  - id: NO_SCALAR_CONFIDENCE
    description: >
      Scalar or collapsed confidence values are forbidden.
      Confidence MUST be decomposed into explicit dimensions.

  - id: EVIDENCE_BOUND_ONLY
    description: >
      Confidence MUST derive exclusively from attestable,
      replayable inputs.
      Model self-assessed confidence is forbidden.

  - id: REPLAY_REPRODUCIBILITY_REQUIRED
    description: >
      Every confidence dimension MUST be recomputable
      during replay under identical conditions.

  - id: NORMALIZATION_REQUIRED
    description: >
      All confidence dimensions MUST be normalized
      onto a common numeric scale.

  - id: UNCERTAINTY_IS_LEGITIMATE
    description: >
      Low confidence values are acceptable.
      Absence of confidence inflation is not a failure.

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# NORMALIZATION RULES
# -------------------------------------------------------------------

normalization:

  scale:
    min: 0.0
    max: 1.0

  semantics:
    "0.0": >
      No admissible epistemic support.
      Dimension is effectively unsatisfied.
    "0.5": >
      Partial, weak, or incomplete epistemic support.
    "1.0": >
      Fully satisfied epistemic condition
      under declared constitutional constraints.

  rounding:
    precision: 4
    deterministic: true

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# EPISTEMIC CONFIDENCE DIMENSIONS
# -------------------------------------------------------------------

epistemic_confidence:

  # ===============================================================
  # EVIDENTIARY CONFIDENCE
  # ===============================================================

  evidentiary:
    description: >
      Measures whether claims are supported by
      identifiable, citable evidence.
    inputs:
      - provenance_chain
      - citation_count
    constraints:
      min_citations: 1
    replay_dependencies:
      - provenance_chain_hash
    normalization_rule: >
      f(citation_count, evidence_uniqueness)

  # ===============================================================
  # SOURCE CONSENSUS CONFIDENCE
  # ===============================================================

  source_consensus:
    description: >
      Measures agreement across independent sources.
      Disagreement lowers confidence but does not
      invalidate claims.
    inputs:
      - provenance_chain
      - source_overlap
    constraints:
      independence_required: true
    replay_dependencies:
      - provenance_chain_hash
    normalization_rule: >
      f(independent_source_count, contradiction_ratio)

  # ===============================================================
  # REPLAY DETERMINISM CONFIDENCE
  # ===============================================================

  replay_determinism:
    description: >
      Measures whether execution is deterministically
      reproducible under replay.
    inputs:
      - execution_trace
      - replay_hash
    constraints:
      deterministic_required: true
    replay_dependencies:
      - execution_trace_hash
    normalization_rule: >
      1.0 if replay_hash matches exactly
      else 0.0

  # ===============================================================
  # ATTESTATION STRENGTH
  # ===============================================================

  attestation_strength:
    description: >
      Measures support from required attestations.
      During FIRST_EXECUTABLE_PROOF, this dimension
      may be minimal but must be explicit.
    inputs:
      - attestations
    constraints:
      min_attestations: 0
    replay_dependencies:
      - attestation_hashes
    normalization_rule: >
      f(attestation_count, attestation_weight)

  # ===============================================================
  # TEMPORAL STABILITY
  # ===============================================================

  temporal_stability:
    description: >
      Measures whether claims remain stable over
      constitutional time.
      Cross-epoch evaluation is optional at this phase.
    inputs:
      - epoch_id
      - prior_claim_hashes
    constraints:
      requires_cross_epoch_check: false
    replay_dependencies:
      - epoch_id
    normalization_rule: >
      1.0 if no known prior contradiction
      else value < 1.0

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# OPTIONAL AGGREGATION (STRICTLY CONTROLLED)
# -------------------------------------------------------------------
#
# Aggregation is optional and MUST NOT replace or
# obscure decomposed confidence dimensions.

aggregation:

  allowed: true

  produces:
    - optional_summary_metric

  constraints:
    method_must_be_declared: true
    aggregation_must_reference_dimensions: true
    aggregation_must_be_replayable: true
    aggregation_must_not_be_decision_authoritative: true

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# PROHIBITED CONFIDENCE PRACTICES
# -------------------------------------------------------------------

forbidden_practices:

  - scalar_confidence
  - model_self_confidence
  - narrative_confidence_labels
  - undocumented_aggregation
  - non_normalized_values
  - confidence_without_provenance
  - confidence_without_causal_trace

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# FAILURE CONDITIONS
# -------------------------------------------------------------------

failure_conditions:

  - missing_required_dimension
  - non_normalized_value
  - irreproducible_computation
  - scalar_confidence_detected
  - confidence_without_evidence
  - confidence_without_causality

failure_response:
  type: HARD_FAILURE
  effect: >
    TruthPacket legitimacy is invalidated and
    execution proof fails.

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# CONSTITUTIONAL ASSERTION
# -------------------------------------------------------------------

constitutional_assertion: >
  AfriTech treats epistemic confidence as a
  constitutional computation, not an expression
  of belief.
  What cannot be decomposed, normalized, and replayed
  is epistemically illegitimate.

===== ./ecosystems/afriride/core/constitutional/determinism_spec.yaml =====

#ecosystems/afriride/core/constitutional/determinism.yaml
determinism_contract:
  domain: afriride

  version: "0.1"
  status: enforced

  # --------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ WHAT IS GUARANTEED
  # --------------------------------------------------
  scope: decision_causality

  guarantees:
    - identical_inputs_produce_identical_decisions
    - identical_event_streams_produce_identical_state
    - execution_trace_is_deterministically_hashable

  # --------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ DETERMINISTIC DECISIONS (MUST BE PURE)
  # --------------------------------------------------
  deterministic_decisions:
    - ride_request_admission
    - authority_validation
    - guard_evaluation
    - driver_assignment
    - dispatch_retry_policy
    - trip_state_transition
    - fare_policy_application

  # --------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ NON-DETERMINISTIC INPUTS (MUST BE NORMALIZED)
  # --------------------------------------------------
  nondeterministic_inputs:
    - gps_noise
    - driver_location_latency
    - network_delay
    - timestamp_variability
    - driver_availability_fluctuation

  # --------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ NORMALIZATION RULES (MANDATORY)
  # --------------------------------------------------
  normalization_rules:
    driver_selection:
      - driver_list_sorted_by_id
      - stable_priority_ordering

    time_handling:
      - timestamps_truncated_to_seconds
      - no wall_clock_dependency_in_decisions

    geo_handling:
      - geo_positions_rounded_5dp
      - distance_calculated_with_fixed_precision

    collections:
      - unordered_sets_must_be_sorted_before_iteration

    randomness:
      - randomness_forbidden
      - if_required_must_use_fixed_seed

  # --------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ EVENT & TRACE CONSISTENCY
  # --------------------------------------------------
  event_constraints:
    - events_must_be_emitted_in_deterministic_order
    - event_payloads_must_be_serialization_stable
    - event_ids_must_not_depend_on_runtime_entropy

  trace_constraints:
    - decision_trace_structure_is_static
    - serialization_must_use_sorted_keys
    - hash_function_must_be_sha256

  # --------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ REPLAY CLAIM (CRITICAL)
  # --------------------------------------------------
  replay_claim:
    guarantees_decision_trace_identity: true
    guarantees_event_sequence_identity: true
    guarantees_state_reconstruction_equivalence: true

    does_not_claim_physical_identity: true
    does_not_claim_real_time_equivalence: true

  # --------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ VIOLATION POLICY (STRICT)
  # --------------------------------------------------
  violation_policy:
    on_nondeterminism_detected: reject_execution
    on_trace_mismatch: fail_replay
    on_event_divergence: invalidate_state
    on_unstable_sort_detected: halt_dispatch

  # --------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ OBSERVABILITY (MINIMAL BUT CRITICAL)
  # --------------------------------------------------
  observability:
    required_metrics:
      - decision_hash
      - replay_hash
      - determinism_match (boolean)

    kpi:
      decision_determinism_rate:
        description: "Percentage of executions where decision hash == replay hash"
        target: 1.0

  # --------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ EXPLICIT NON-GOALS (PREVENT SCOPE CREEP)
  # --------------------------------------------------
  non_goals:
    - real_time_prediction_accuracy
    - optimal_driver_matching
    - economic_optimization
    - fairness_scoring
    - machine_learning_decisions

  # --------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ ENFORCEMENT NOTE
  # --------------------------------------------------
  enforcement:
    enforced_by:
      - runtime_adapter
      - admission_layer
      - guard_layer
      - replay_tests

    invariant:
      - any_non_deterministic_execution_is_invalid

===== ./ecosystems/afriride/v0_2/determinism_envelope.yaml =====
# ecosystems/afriride/v0_2/determinism_envelope.yaml

schema: afriride.determinism_envelope.v0_2
kind: determinism_envelope

envelope:
  domain: afriride
  version: v0.2
  status: ACTIVE
  classification: bounded_deterministic_execution

  description: >
    This determinism envelope defines the complete and exclusive
    boundary of allowed variability for AfriRide v0.2.
    All execution, failure handling, replay verification,
    and continuity proofs MUST operate entirely within
    this envelope. Any behavior outside this envelope
    is constitutionally invalid.

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ CORE DETERMINISM PRINCIPLE
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  core_principle:
    statement: >
      Given identical inputs, identical parameters, identical
      authority scope, and identical envelope constraints,
      AfriRide v0.2 MUST produce identical decision traces,
      identical event sequences, and identical replay hashes.

    applies_to:
      - assignment decisions
      - retry sequencing
      - failure handling
      - refusal outcomes
      - trace generation

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ ALLOWED VARIABILITY (EXPLICITLY BOUNDED)
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  allowed_variability:

    scenario_parameters:
      description: >
        Scenario parameters may vary ONLY if explicitly
        declared in scenario YAML files.
      examples:
        - initial_driver_count
        - dropout_count
        - rejection_sequence
        - timeout_threshold

      constraints:
        - parameters must be scalar or ordered lists
        - parameters must be replay-bound
        - no implicit defaults permitted

    ordered_collections:
      description: >
        Collections may vary in size but MUST be ordered
        deterministically before use.
      ordering_rules:
        - explicit sort key required
        - stable ordering guaranteed
        - no runtime reordering

    retry_depth:
      description: >
        Retry count may vary as a function of deterministic
        exhaustion of ordered candidates.
      constraints:
        - retry is strictly sequential
        - no backtracking
        - no parallel attempts

    logical_step_count:
      description: >
        Logical step counters may advance deterministically
        and are used for timeout evaluation.
      constraints:
        - counter increments must be explicit
        - counters must appear in trace
        - no wall-clock dependency

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ❌ FORBIDDEN VARIABILITY (ABSOLUTE)
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  forbidden_variability:

    randomness:
      - random()
      - sampling
      - shuffle
      - probabilistic_branching

    time_sources:
      - wall_clock_time
      - system_time
      - sleep
      - async_delay

    external_state:
      - environment_variables
      - network_state
      - I/O side effects
      - shared mutable globals

    inference:
      - heuristic_selection
      - optimization
      - scoring_functions
      - ML_model_outputs

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ NORMALIZATION RULES
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  normalization:

    identifiers:
      rule: >
        Identifiers must be stable, immutable, and comparable.
      constraints:
        - no mutation of ids
        - ids must be hash-stable

    collections:
      rule: >
        All collections MUST be normalized before use.
      normalization_steps:
        - explicit sorting
        - explicit truncation
        - explicit filtering

    state_transitions:
      rule: >
        State transitions must be atomic, ordered,
        and traceable.
      constraints:
        - no partial mutation
        - no implicit transitions

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ TRACE & REPLAY BINDING
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  trace_binding:

    requirements:
      - every decision emits a trace event
      - every failure emits a trace event
      - trace order is strict
      - trace content is deterministic

    invariants:
      - identical trace sequence → identical hash
      - trace omission → invalid execution
      - trace divergence → replay failure

  replay_binding:

    requirements:
      - replay uses identical envelope
      - replay forbids external inputs
      - replay recomputes all decisions

    acceptance_rule:
      description: >
        Replay is accepted ONLY if recomputed trace hash
        exactly matches original execution hash.

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ AUTHORITY & SCOPE BINDING
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  authority_binding:

    requirements:
      - authority must be explicit
      - authority scope must be identical for replay
      - no authority inference permitted

    forbidden:
      - implicit authority escalation
      - authority mutation during execution

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ FAILURE HANDLING CONSISTENCY
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  failure_handling:

    rule: >
      All failures MUST map to declared failure taxonomy
      and handling modes.
    constraints:
      - no undeclared failure paths
      - no silent failure
      - refusal must be explicit

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ VALIDATION & ENFORCEMENT
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  validation:

    must_hold:
      - execution conforms to envelope
      - replay conforms to envelope
      - trace and replay hashes identical
      - no forbidden variability observed

    violation_effect:
      classification: CONSTITUTIONAL_INVALIDATION
      consequence:
        - scenario proof rejected
        - continuity coverage reduced to zero
        - v0.2 claim invalidated

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ RELATIONSHIP TO v0.1
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  compatibility:

    v0_1_status:
      description: >
        AfriRide v0.1 remains frozen and unaffected.
      guarantees:
        - no weakening of v0.1 determinism
        - no reinterpretation of v0.1 proofs

    v0_2_extension:
      description: >
        v0.2 extends proof coverage ONLY within this
        determinism envelope.

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ FINAL ASSERTION
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  final_assertion:
    statement: >
      AfriRide v0.2 is deterministic if and only if
      all execution paths, failures, retries, and refusals
      operate strictly within this determinism envelope.


===== ./ecosystems/afriride/v0_2/failure_taxonomy.yaml =====
failure_taxonomy:
  domain: afriride
  version: v0.2
  classification: deterministic_failure_space

  governing_epoch: EPOCH_0008

  doctrine: OBSERVATIONAL_ADMISSIBILITY_GOVERNANCE

# =====================================================
# PRINCIPLE
# =====================================================

  principle:
    description: >
      All coordination failures must be explicit, deterministic,
      and replay-verifiable. No failure may occur implicitly,
      probabilistically, or without trace representation.

    guarantees:
      - every failure must be declared in this taxonomy
      - every failure must produce a deterministic outcome
      - every outcome must be replay-identical
      - no silent failure is permitted

# =====================================================
# OBSERVATIONAL DOCTRINE BINDING
# =====================================================

  observational_doctrine:
    rule: >
      Taxonomy may declare only replay-verified deterministic
      runtime behavior without introducing semantic interpretation.

    admissibility_conditions:
      - execution_preexisting: true
      - deterministic: true
      - replay_verified: true
      - semantic_free: true
      - runtime_unchanged: true

    prohibited_actions:
      - semantic_interpretation
      - equivalence_inference
      - normalization
      - runtime_behavior_mutation

# =====================================================
# EPISTEMIC MODEL
# =====================================================

  epistemic:
    base_classification:
      epistemic_status: OBSERVED_FACT
      semantic_commitment: NONE
      interpretation_required: false

    constraints:
      - all failure classifications are replay-observed facts
      - failures MUST NOT encode meaning or intent identity
      - replay evidence supersedes all interpretation
      - historical outcomes are immutable

# =====================================================
# FAILURE MODES
# =====================================================

  failure_modes:

    DRIVER_DROPOUT:
      description: >
        A driver becomes unavailable after initial eligibility
        evaluation but before final assignment.

      trigger_condition:
        - driver_list_reduced_deterministically
        - availability_flag_false

      deterministic_handling: RETRY_OR_REFUSE

      expected_outcomes:
        - deterministic_driver_reselection
        - fallback_to_next_available
        - deterministic_refusal_if_exhausted

      invariants:
        - driver ordering is stable
        - retry sequence is deterministic
        - no randomness in selection

    DRIVER_REJECTS:
      description: >
        A driver rejects an assignment request.

      trigger_condition:
        - driver_response == REJECTED

      deterministic_handling: RETRY_NEXT_DRIVER

      expected_outcomes:
        - sequential driver iteration
        - rejection recorded in execution trace

      invariants:
        - rejection ordering is preserved
        - no reordering of candidates
        - deterministic traversal only

    NO_DRIVER_AVAILABLE:
      description: >
        No eligible driver exists at evaluation time.

      trigger_condition:
        - driver_pool_empty
        - all drivers unavailable

      deterministic_handling: DETERMINISTIC_REFUSAL

      expected_outcomes:
        - explicit refusal outcome
        - complete trace emission

      invariants:
        - refusal is replay-identical
        - no partial assignment permitted

    TIMEOUT_EXCEEDED:
      description: >
        Execution exceeds declared deterministic step bound.

      trigger_condition:
        - execution_steps > declared_threshold

      deterministic_handling: DETERMINISTIC_REFUSAL

      expected_outcomes:
        - deterministic timeout refusal
        - trace record emission

      invariants:
        - threshold is constant
        - no real-time dependency
        - no external clock influence

# =====================================================
# OBSERVATIONAL FAILURE OVERLAY
# =====================================================

  observational_failures:

    DUPLICATE_INTENT_REFUSAL:
      base_mode: DETERMINISTIC_REFUSAL
      classification: OBSERVATIONAL_REFUSAL

      epistemic_status: OBSERVED_FACT
      semantic_commitment: NONE
      interpretation_required: false

      description: >
        Deterministic refusal observed for execution traces with
        identical replay hash signature.

      properties:
        deterministic: true
        replay_stable: true
        hash_stable: true
        non_semantic: true
        non_equivalence_bound: true
        runtime_existing_behavior: true

      replay_guarantees:
        - identical replay hash signature MUST produce identical refusal
        - refusal MUST produce identical replay hash signature
        - transcript MUST remain unchanged

      prohibited_interpretations:
        - equivalence inference
        - similarity inference
        - normalization
        - deduplication logic
        - intent identity assignment

      constitutional_basis:
        - ADR-0011
        - EPOCH_0008

# =====================================================
# HANDLING MODES
# =====================================================

  handling_modes:

    RETRY_OR_REFUSE:
      description: >
        Deterministic reassignment until candidates are exhausted,
        then deterministic refusal.

    RETRY_NEXT_DRIVER:
      description: >
        Sequential deterministic selection of next available driver.

    DETERMINISTIC_REFUSAL:
      description: >
        Explicit refusal outcome with full trace emission.

# =====================================================
# GLOBAL INVARIANTS
# =====================================================

  invariants:

    determinism:
      - no random selection
      - no probabilistic branching
      - no nondeterministic iteration

    replay:
      - identical replay hash signature yields identical outcome
      - all failure traces are replay-identical

    ordering:
      - all collections are explicitly ordered
      - driver traversal is stable

    traceability:
      - every failure produces a trace entry
      - every decision is auditable

    epistemic:
      - all outcomes are observed facts
      - no semantic interpretation permitted
      - runtime outcomes are immutable across epochs

# =====================================================
# FORBIDDEN BEHAVIORS
# =====================================================

  forbidden:

    execution:
      - implicit_fallback
      - silent_failure
      - untraced_execution

    determinism:
      - random_selection
      - probabilistic_branching
      - time_based_variation

    structure:
      - undeclared_failure_modes
      - runtime_extension_without_epoch

    semantics:
      - equivalence inference
      - similarity reasoning
      - normalization
      - deduplication
      - intent classification

# =====================================================
# VALIDATION CONTRACT
# =====================================================

  validation:

    required:
      - all scenarios reference declared failure_modes
      - all failures map to handling_modes
      - all outputs are replay-verifiable

    admissibility:
      - replay_verified: true
      - deterministic: true
      - semantic_free: true
      - runtime_unchanged: true

    rejection_conditions:
      - replay divergence
      - semantic dependency
      - equivalence requirement
      - runtime mutation
      - normalization dependency

    success_condition: >
      All failure scenarios resolve into deterministic,
      replay-identical outcomes without semantic interpretation.

    failure_condition: >
      Any deviation from declared modes, determinism,
      or replay consistency invalidates v0.2 compliance.

===== ./ecosystems/afriride/v0_2/scenarios/driver_dropout.yaml =====
# ecosystems/afriride/v0_2/scenarios/driver_dropout.yaml

schema: afriride.scenario.v0_2
kind: failure_scenario

scenario:
  id: DRIVER_DROPOUT
  version: v0.2
  classification: deterministic_failure_scenario
  domain: afriride
  status: ACTIVE

  description: >
    This scenario validates deterministic handling of driver dropout,
    where a subset of initially eligible drivers becomes unavailable.
    The system must re-evaluate assignment deterministically without
    introducing randomness or altering replay consistency.

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ TAXONOMY LINK (MANDATORY)
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  failure_mode: DRIVER_DROPOUT
  governed_by:
    taxonomy: ecosystems/afriride/v0_2/failure_taxonomy.yaml
    handling_mode: RETRY_OR_REFUSE

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ INPUT PARAMETERS (FULLY DETERMINISTIC)
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  parameters:
    initial_driver_count: 10
    dropout_count: 5

    driver_definition:
      format: list_of_dicts
      required_fields:
        - id
        - available
      id_constraints:
        type: integer
        uniqueness: required
        mutation: forbidden

    ordering_rule:
      description: >
        Drivers must be sorted in ascending order by id before
        any assignment or dropout logic is applied.
      key: id
      order: ascending
      requirement: strict

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ DERIVED CONDITIONS (EXPLICIT — NO RUNTIME INFERENCE)
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  derived_conditions:
    remaining_driver_count: 5

    dropout_strategy:
      description: >
        Dropout is applied deterministically by truncating
        the ordered driver list.
      algorithm:
        steps:
          - step: sort
            rule: ascending_id
          - step: truncate
            rule: remove_last_N
            parameter: dropout_count
      forbidden:
        - random_removal
        - probabilistic_selection
        - availability_sampling

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ EXPECTED SYSTEM BEHAVIOR
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  expected_behavior:

    assignment_strategy:
      description: >
        Assignment must always select the first available driver
        from the deterministically ordered list.
      rules:
        - select_first_available
        - no_random_selection
        - no_scoring
        - no_weighting
        - no_reordering

    fallback_behavior:
      description: >
        If the selected driver becomes unavailable,
        the system must select the next driver in strict order.
      rules:
        - strictly_sequential_retry
        - no_skipping
        - no_reordering
        - bounded_by_remaining_driver_count

    exhaustion_behavior:
      description: >
        If all drivers are exhausted due to dropout,
        the system must deterministically refuse.
      output:
        type: refusal
        reason: NO_DRIVER_AVAILABLE
        refusal_classification: DETERMINISTIC_REFUSAL
        retry_permitted: false

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ TRACE REQUIREMENTS
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  trace_requirements:

    required_events:
      - DriverPoolInitialized
      - DriverPoolOrdered
      - DriverDropoutApplied
      - AssignmentAttempted
      - DriverSelected
      - DeterministicRefusal

    event_ordering:
      requirement: strict
      branching_allowed: false

    trace_invariants:
      - identical input yields identical event sequence
      - identical event sequence yields identical hash
      - no event omission
      - no extra events

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ REPLAY REQUIREMENTS
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  replay_requirements:

    admissibility_conditions:
      - identical scenario_id
      - identical parameters
      - identical driver ordering
      - identical dropout_count
      - identical authority scope

    guarantees:
      - identical trace reconstruction
      - identical event ordering
      - identical replay hash

    invalidation_rule:
      description: >
        Any divergence between original execution and replay,
        including trace order or hash, invalidates this scenario proof.

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ VALIDATION RULES
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  validation:

    must_hold:
      - driver list sorted before processing
      - dropout applied exactly once
      - assignment order preserved
      - no randomness introduced
      - determinism contract honored

    must_not_occur:
      - implicit_fallback
      - silent_failure
      - dynamic_reordering
      - missing_trace_events
      - external_state_dependency

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ KPI EXPECTATIONS (LIMITED — v0.2)
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  kpi_expectations:

    determinism:
      DDR: 1.0

    continuity:
      included_in_CC: true

    refusal_behavior:
      deterministic_refusal_if_exhausted: true

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ❌ FORBIDDEN BEHAVIOR
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  forbidden:

    execution:
      - random_driver_selection
      - heuristic_assignment
      - load_balancing_logic
      - optimization_routines

    determinism:
      - unordered_iteration
      - probabilistic_branching
      - wall_clock_dependency
      - entropy_sources

    structure:
      - modifying_driver_ids
      - injecting_dynamic_drivers
      - undeclared_failure_path
