# ecosystems/afriride/v0_2/scenarios/rejection_chain.yaml

schema: afriride.scenario.v0_2
kind: failure_scenario

scenario:
  id: DRIVER_REJECTION_CHAIN
  version: v0.2
  classification: deterministic_failure_scenario
  domain: afriride
  status: ACTIVE

  description: >
    This scenario validates deterministic handling of sequential driver
    rejections during ride assignment. Drivers reject assignments in a
    fixed order, and the system must retry deterministically without
    reordering, skipping, or introducing randomness, preserving replay
    identity across all retries.

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ TAXONOMY LINK (MANDATORY)
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  failure_mode: DRIVER_REJECTS
  governed_by:
    taxonomy: ecosystems/afriride/v0_2/failure_taxonomy.yaml
    handling_mode: RETRY_NEXT_DRIVER

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ INPUT PARAMETERS (FULLY DETERMINISTIC)
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  parameters:
    initial_driver_count: 5

    driver_definition:
      format: list_of_dicts
      required_fields:
        - id
        - available
      id_constraints:
        type: integer
        uniqueness: required
        mutation: forbidden

    ordering_rule:
      description: >
        Drivers must be sorted in ascending order by id before any
        assignment attempt.
      key: id
      order: ascending
      requirement: strict

    rejection_sequence:
      description: >
        Ordered list of driver ids that will deterministically reject
        the assignment when selected.
      type: ordered_list
      example: [1, 2]

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ DERIVED CONDITIONS (EXPLICIT)
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  derived_conditions:
    rejection_count: 2
    remaining_candidates: 3

    rejection_handling:
      description: >
        Each rejection removes the driver from future consideration.
      algorithm:
        steps:
          - step: select_next_driver
            rule: ascending_order
          - step: detect_rejection
            rule: driver_id_in_rejection_sequence
          - step: mark_driver_unavailable
            effect: remove_from_candidate_pool

      forbidden:
        - reinsert_rejected_driver
        - random_reselection
        - non_sequential_iteration

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ EXPECTED SYSTEM BEHAVIOR
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  expected_behavior:

    assignment_strategy:
      description: >
        System must attempt assignment strictly in driver id order.
      rules:
        - select_first_available
        - no_random_selection
        - no_scoring
        - no_weighting

    rejection_behavior:
      description: >
        When a driver rejects, the system must deterministically move
        to the next driver.
      rules:
        - strict_sequence
        - preserve_rejection_order
        - no_retry_of_rejected_driver

    exhaustion_behavior:
      description: >
        If all drivers reject or are exhausted, the system must
        deterministically refuse.
      output:
        type: refusal
        reason: NO_DRIVER_AVAILABLE
        refusal_classification: DETERMINISTIC_REFUSAL
        retry_permitted: false

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ TRACE REQUIREMENTS
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  trace_requirements:

    required_events:
      - DriverPoolInitialized
      - DriverPoolOrdered
      - AssignmentAttempted
      - DriverRejected
      - DriverSelected
      - DeterministicRefusal

    event_ordering:
      requirement: strict
      branching_allowed: false

    trace_invariants:
      - identical input yields identical event sequence
      - rejection order must appear explicitly in trace
      - identical trace yields identical hash
      - no event omission
      - no extra events

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ REPLAY REQUIREMENTS
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  replay_requirements:

    admissibility_conditions:
      - identical scenario_id
      - identical parameters
      - identical rejection_sequence
      - identical driver ordering
      - identical authority scope

    guarantees:
      - identical trace reconstruction
      - identical event ordering
      - identical replay hash

    invalidation_rule:
      description: >
        Any divergence in rejection order, event sequence, or hash
        invalidates the scenario proof.

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ VALIDATION RULES
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  validation:

    must_hold:
      - driver list sorted before processing
      - rejection sequence honored strictly
      - rejected drivers removed from pool
      - no randomness introduced
      - determinism contract honored

    must_not_occur:
      - implicit fallback
      - silent failure
      - driver reordering
      - retry loops
      - external_state_dependency

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ KPI EXPECTATIONS (LIMITED — v0.2)
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  kpi_expectations:

    determinism:
      DDR: 1.0

    continuity:
      included_in_CC: true

    refusal_behavior:
      deterministic_refusal_if_exhausted: true

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ❌ FORBIDDEN BEHAVIOR
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  forbidden:

    execution:
      - random_driver_selection
      - heuristic_assignment
      - load_balancing_logic
      - optimization_routines

    determinism:
      - unordered_iteration
      - probabilistic_branching
      - wall_clock_dependency
      - entropy_sources

    structure:
      - modifying_driver_ids
      - reinserting_rejected_drivers
      - undeclared_failure_path

===== ./ecosystems/afriride/v0_2/scenarios/timeout.yaml =====
# ecosystems/afriride/v0_2/scenarios/timeout.yaml

schema: afriride.scenario.v0_2
kind: failure_scenario

scenario:
  id: TIMEOUT_EXCEEDED
  version: v0.2
  classification: deterministic_failure_scenario
  domain: afriride
  status: ACTIVE

  description: >
    This scenario validates deterministic handling of coordination
    timeouts. When a coordination step exceeds its declared deterministic
    threshold, the system must refuse explicitly and replay-identically,
    without consulting wall-clock time or introducing nondeterminism.

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ TAXONOMY LINK (MANDATORY)
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  failure_mode: TIMEOUT_EXCEEDED
  governed_by:
    taxonomy: ecosystems/afriride/v0_2/failure_taxonomy.yaml
    handling_mode: DETERMINISTIC_REFUSAL

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ INPUT PARAMETERS (FULLY DETERMINISTIC)
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  parameters:
    timeout_threshold:
      description: >
        Maximum number of deterministic coordination steps
        allowed before timeout is triggered.
      unit: logical_steps
      value: 10

    coordination_step_definition:
      description: >
        A coordination step represents a single, deterministic
        state transition attempt (e.g. assignment attempt).
      counted_events:
        - AssignmentAttempted
        - DriverResponseEvaluated

    clock_model:
      description: >
        Timeout is evaluated using logical step counting only.
        Wall-clock time is explicitly forbidden.
      type: logical_counter
      wall_clock_usage: forbidden

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ DERIVED CONDITIONS (EXPLICIT)
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  derived_conditions:
    timeout_trigger_condition:
      description: >
        Timeout is triggered when the number of coordination
        steps exceeds the declared threshold.
      rule: coordination_steps > timeout_threshold

    timeout_evaluation:
      description: >
        Timeout evaluation must occur at a deterministic
        checkpoint in the execution flow.
      evaluation_point: post_step_increment

    forbidden:
      - real_time_measurement
      - system_clock_access
      - sleep_based_delay

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ EXPECTED SYSTEM BEHAVIOR
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  expected_behavior:

    normal_behavior:
      description: >
        Coordination proceeds deterministically while the
        step count remains within the threshold.
      rules:
        - step_counter_incremented_per_event
        - no timeout evaluation before threshold

    timeout_behavior:
      description: >
        When the threshold is exceeded, the system must
        immediately produce a deterministic refusal.
      output:
        type: refusal
        reason: TIMEOUT_EXCEEDED
        refusal_classification: DETERMINISTIC_REFUSAL
        retry_permitted: false

    post_timeout_behavior:
      description: >
        No further coordination or retries are permitted
        after timeout refusal.
      rules:
        - execution_terminates
        - no state mutation
        - no retry_attempts

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ TRACE REQUIREMENTS
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  trace_requirements:

    required_events:
      - CoordinationStarted
      - CoordinationStepIncremented
      - TimeoutThresholdEvaluated
      - DeterministicRefusal

    event_ordering:
      requirement: strict
      branching_allowed: false

    trace_invariants:
      - coordination_step_count must be explicit in trace
      - identical inputs yield identical step counts
      - identical trace yields identical hash
      - no missing or extra events

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ REPLAY REQUIREMENTS
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  replay_requirements:

    admissibility_conditions:
      - identical scenario_id
      - identical timeout_threshold
      - identical coordination_step_definition
      - identical authority scope

    guarantees:
      - identical step counter reconstruction
      - identical event ordering
      - identical replay hash

    invalidation_rule:
      description: >
        Any divergence in step count, event order,
        or replay hash invalidates the scenario proof.

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ VALIDATION RULES
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  validation:

    must_hold:
      - timeout evaluated using logical steps only
      - threshold constant across executions
      - refusal occurs immediately after threshold breach
      - determinism contract honored

    must_not_occur:
      - wall_clock_dependency
      - time.sleep or delay logic
      - probabilistic timeout
      - implicit continuation after timeout
      - external_state_dependency

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ✅ KPI EXPECTATIONS (LIMITED — v0.2)
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  kpi_expectations:

    determinism:
      DDR: 1.0

    continuity:
      included_in_CC: true

    refusal_behavior:
      deterministic_refusal_on_timeout: true

  # -----------------------------------------------------
  # ❌ FORBIDDEN BEHAVIOR
  # -----------------------------------------------------

  forbidden:

    execution:
      - retry_after_timeout
      - partial_execution_post_refusal
      - heuristic_grace_period

    determinism:
      - wall_clock_time
      - entropy_sources
      - probabilistic_thresholds

    structure:
      - dynamic_threshold_adjustment
      - undeclared_timeout_paths
